<pb n="001"/>
<q>mīmāṁsādarśanam</q>
prathamē'dhyāyē prathamaḥ pādaḥ
<q>athātō dharmajijñāsā ।। 1 ।।</q>
śābarabhāṣyam
<q>lōkē yēṣvarthēṣu prasiddhāni padāni, tāni</q>
br̥hatī
<q>prabhākaramiśraviracitā</q>
(śābarabhāṣyaṭīkā)
<q>।। athātō dharmajijñāsā ।।</q>
<q>lōkē---ityādibhāṣyasya <quote>“athātaḥ”</quote>---ityētasmin padadvayē'lauki-</q>
﻿<pb n="002"/>
kārthāśaṅkānivr̥ttiḥ prayōjanam । kuta ētat ? svādhyāyādhyayanavidhē-
ravivakṣitārthatvanirākaraṇāt । kathaṁ punaravivakṣāśaṅkā ? svādhyāyādhyayana-
vidhēradhikārāśravaṇāt, ācāryakaraṇavidhiprayōjyatvācca । kathaṁ punaranyasya
vidhēranyēna prayuktiḥ ? prayājādivaditi cēnna; tatra svādhikārābhēdādyuktam ।
﻿<pb n="003"/>
atrāpyadhikārāṁśō na bhidyata iti cēnna, aṅgāṅgibhāvābhāvāt । kathaṁ punaraṅgatā
nāsti, prayōjyatvaṁ ca ? na prayuktiraṅgatvē hētuḥ । kastarhi ? viniyōgaḥ । nanu
viniyōgaḥ pārārthyē kārāṇam; viniyuktasyaiva hyaṅgatvaṁ darśayati <quote>“na cāvihitamaṅgaṁ
bhavati,”</quote> <quote>“phalavatsan‍nidhāvaphalaṁ tadaṅgam”</quote> iti ca । maivam; pārārthyamēva
hyaṅgatōcyatē; parasyōtpattau kāryē vā yadanugrahāya vartatē, tat parārthamityucyatē;
tadēva cāṅgam । tasmādviniyōgakr̥tamēvāṅgatvam, na prayuktikr̥tam । kathaṁ
punarēkatvādīnāmaṅgatvam ? uktaṁ hi paśōrupādānaśēṣatvam; prayuktikr̥taṁ ca
tat । tadapi naiva prayuktikr̥tam । kiṁ tarhi ? viniyōgakr̥tamēva । nanu
vibhaktibhiḥ prātipadikārthō viniyujyatē, na punarēkatvādayō vibhaktyarthāḥ ।
﻿<pb n="004"/>
satyam na viniyujyantē; na punarviniyuktōpādānē'pi nāvagamyantē
vibhaktibhiḥ । viniyuktasyaikatvādayō vibhaktibhirabhidhīyantē, asaṁbaddhasyānava-
gamāt । ata ēva caikavākyatvaṁ saṁkhyāvidhānasya vibhaktividhānasya
ca । tasmādyuktamupādānaśēṣatvamēkatvādēḥ । svādhyāyādhyayanaṁ tu na
viniyuktam, nāpi viniyuktasthamavagamyatē । ataḥ prayōjyam, na
cāṅgamiti siddham । kathaṁ punaraviniyuktamasaṁbaddhamēvākṣipyatē ? naiva viniyōga
ākṣēpē hētuḥ । kiṁ tarhi ? kāryam । viniyuktasthamapi kāryēṇaivākṣipyatē ।
tātsthyaṁ tvaṅgatvē hētuḥ । yatpunaridamuktam---<quote>“na cāvihitamaṅgaṁ bhavati,”</quote> <quote>“phala-
﻿<pb n="005"/>
vatsannidhāvaphalaṁ tadaṅgam”</quote>---iti ca, kāryē'ṅgatvapratipattyarthō'yaṁ granthaḥ; na
punaraṅgatvapratipattyarthaḥ । asti hi kāmasyādhikārē prayōjyatvam, na cāṅgatā ।
tasmādanyat prayōjyatvam, anyā cāṅgatā । tathā cōhyapadānāmasti
prayōjyatvam, na śēṣatā; mantrasya hi viniyōgēna śēṣatōcyatē, ūhyapadā-
nāmamantratvāt । tasmāt prayōjyatvādanaṅgatvācca svādhyāyādhyayanasya bhavati
saṁśayaḥ---kiṁ prayōjyatvādēkakāryatvam, utānaṅgatvādbhin‍nakāryatvam ---iti ।
atra pūrvapakṣavādī prayōjyatvādēkakāryatāṁ manvānō'vivakṣāṁ mēnē । tanni-
rākr̥taya idam <quote>“athātaḥ”</quote>---iti padadvayamaṅgīkr̥tavān sūtrakāraḥ । na
cānēna padadvayēnāyamarthō nirākr̥ta iti pāṭhādēvāvagamyatē, pūrvamanupanyastatvā-
dasyārthasya । atō bhavatyalaukikārthāśaṅkā kasyacit । atō'ntarṇīta-
pūrvapakṣanirasanasamarthaṁ padadvayaṁ manvānō bhāṣyakāra āha - <quote>“lōkē yēṣvarthēṣu
prasiddhāni padāni, tāni sati sambhavē tadarthānyēva sūtrēṣvityavagantavyam;
﻿<pb n="006"/>
nādhyāhārādibhirēṣāṁ parikalpanīyō'rthaḥ paribhāṣitavyō vā”</quote> iti ।</p>
<p>kiñca, na kavēlamasyālaukikārthāśaṅkānirāsaḥ; avagamyatē, paribhāṣā-
diyat‍nagauravākaraṇāt ।।</p>
<p><quote>“tatra lōkē'yamathaśabdō vr̥ttādanatantarasya prakriyārthō dr̥ṣṭaḥ; na
cēha kiñ‍cidva‍r̥ttamupalabhyatē”</quote> ---ityalaukikāśaṅkāṁ prakaṭayati । <quote>“bhavitavyaṁ
tu tēna”</quote>---iti nyāyānapētatāmāśaṅkāyāḥ kathayati । sidhyarthaṁ hi prakaraṇā-
dyanvēṣyam; śrutasya hyayathārthatvē na śrutatvamēva karaṇam । tacca prakaraṇādikaṁ</q>
﻿<pb n="007"/>
sarvamatrāstīti---<quote>“tattu vēdādhyayanam”</quote>---ityuktam । <quote>“tasmin hi sati sāva-
kalpatē”</quote>---itīdānīmavivakṣitārthasvādhyāyādhyayanavādyāha । iti tāvat bhavān
sakalatantrārthaparyālōcanayāṁ vēdādhyayanasya vr̥ttatvaṁ manyatē; tadayuktam,
svādhyāyādhyayanavidhērācāryakaraṇavidhiprayuktatvādavivakṣitasvārthataivāvagamyatē ।
athādr̥ṣṭārthamēvēdaṁ sūtram, <quote>“vēdamadhītya, anantaraṁ dharmajijñāsā”</quote> iti, ēvaṁ
tarhyarthadvayavidhānaṁ prāpnōti---vēdamadhītya, anantaraṁ cēti । yadi ca vēda-
madhītya---ityucyatē, anyasyāpi karmaṇō'nantaraṁ dharmajijñāsā'vakalpatē;
athānantaryaṁ vidhīyatē, prāgapi vēdādhyayanāt prāpnōti । na cādr̥ṣṭārthasya
vākyasyārthadvayavidhānaṁ dvidhā saṁbhavati । ucyatē---naivēdamadr̥ṣṭārthaṁ sūtram;
vēdārthavicārāyaivēdamārabhyatē । kutaḥ ? <quote>“tādr̥śīṁ tu dharmajijñāsāmadhi-
kr̥tyāthaśabdaṁ pratyuktavānācāryaḥ, yā vēdādhyayanamantarēṇa na saṁbhavati ।
katham ? vēdavākyānāmanēkavidhō vicāra iha vartiṣyatē”</quote> । nanvavivakṣi-
﻿<pb n="008"/>
tasvārthaṁ vēdādhyayanamityuktam । vivakṣitē vā kiṁ vēdādhyayanapūrvakēṇā-
nantaryavidhānēna ? svataḥ prāptēḥ । api caivaṁ sati <quote>“naiva vayamiha vēdādhyaya-
nāt pūrvaṁ dharmajijñāsāyāḥ pratiṣēdhaṁ śiṁṣmaḥ ; na hyētadēkaṁ vākyaṁ
purastādvēdādhyayanāddharmajijñāsāṁ pratiṣēdhiṣyati, parastāccānantaryaṁ prakariṣyati ;
bhidyēta hi tathā vākyam ; anyā hi vacanavyaktirasya purastādvēdādhyaya-
nāddharmajijñāsāṁ pratiṣēdhataḥ, anyā ca parastādānantaryamupadiśataḥ---vēdaṁ
nānadhītya---ityēkasyāṁ vidhīyatē'nūdyānantaryam, viparītamēkasyām; arthai-
katvāccaikavākyatāṁ vakṣyati”</quote> । ata ēvādr̥ṣṭārthāśaṅkā naiva sūtrē kartavyā । kimarthaṁ
tarhi sūtram ? svādhyāyādhyayanavidhērācāryakaraṇādga‍urukulānnivr̥ttirēvānantaraṁ
bhāti । anaṅgatvāttu svārthaparataivāsya nyāyyā, nāvivakṣitārthatēti sūtrasya
prayōjanam । tadidamāha---<quote>“adhītē vēdē dvayamāpatanti---gurukulācca sāmāvartti-
tavyam, vēdavākyāni ca vicārayitavyāni; tatra gurukulānmā samāvartiṣṭa,
kathaṁ nu vēdavākyāni vicārayēt---ityēvamarthō'yamupadēśaḥ”</quote> । <quote>“yadyēvam, na
tarhi vēdādhyayanaṁ pūrvamanantaraṁ dharmajijñāsāyāḥ; avivakṣitasvārthatāṁ vēdādhyanasya
﻿<pb n="009"/>
smr̥tikārō manyatē---<quote>“vēdamadhītya s‍nāyāt”</quote> ---iti vadan । na cēdamanyāyyaṁ
﻿<pb n="010"/>
smr̥tivacanam, svādhyāyādhyayanavidhērviniyuktaviṣayatvāt, tatpūrvakatvācca
svārthāvagatēḥ । tasmādavivakṣitasvārthataiva nyāyyā vēdādavagamyatē । <quote>“na
cām‍nāyō nāmātikramitavyaḥ । taducyatē---atikramiṣyāma imamāmnāyam,
anatikrāmantō vēdamarthavantaṁ santamanarthakaṁ kalpayēma”</quote> । ācāryakaraṇavidhē-
radhyayanamātrācca nārthāvabōdhapratyarthitā sambhavati । nanu ca
svādhyāyādhyayanavidhēḥ prayōjanadvayāsambhavādavivakṣaiva । kēna vōktam---
﻿<pb n="011"/>
svādhyāyādhyayanavidhēḥ prayōjanamētat---iti ? <quote>“dr̥ṣṭō hi tasyārthaḥ karmāva-
bōdhanaṁ nāma”</quote> । uktaṁ cāśēṣatvaṁ svādhyāyādhyayanasya, tasyādhikārāśra-
vaṇāt । tadidamāha---<quote>“na ca tatrādhyayanamātrāttatrabhavantō yājñikāḥ
phalaṁ samāmananti; yadapi samāmanantīva, tatrāpi <quote>“dravyasaṁskārakarmasu
parārthatvāt phalaśrutirarthavādaḥ syāt”</quote>---ityarthavādatāṁ vakṣyati”</quote> ।
﻿<pb n="012"/>
nanu naivātra virōdhō vidyatē; kiṁ virōdhinirākaraṇārthēna sūtrēṇa ?
kathamavirōdhaḥ ? <quote>“na cādhītavēdasya snānānantaryamētadvidhīyatē; na
hyatrānantaryasya vaktā kaścicchabdō'sti; pūrvakālatayāṁ hi ktvā smaryatē,
nānantaryē । dr̥ṣṭārthatā cānantaryē'dhyayanasya vyāhanyēta”</quote> । syādētadēvam,
yadyasyāḥ smr̥tērmūlāntaramasti । ācāryakaraṇavidhyarthaparisamāptirēvāsya mūlam,
vēdānuvacanāntatvādācāryakaraṇavidhēḥ । kiṁ tu <quote>“lakṣaṇayā tvēṣō'rthaḥ syāt ।”</quote>
﻿<pb n="013"/>
kimidamucyatē---lakṣaṇayā tvēṣō'rthaḥ syāt iti ? idamucyatē---<quote>“na cēdaṁ
snānamadr̥ṣṭārthaṁ vidhīyatē; kiṁ tu lakṣaṇayā asnānādiniyamasya paryavasānaṁ
vēdādhyayanasamakālamāhuḥ-<quote>“vēdamadhītya snāyāt”</quote>-iti”</quote> । atō'syā nyāya-
mūlatāṁ kathayituṁ sūtram---gurukulānmā samāvartiṣṭa---iti । mūlāntaratvē ca
smr̥tēradr̥ṣṭaṁ kalpayitavyam । atō'dr̥ṣṭārthatāparihārāyaivācāryakaraṇavidhirēvāsya
mūlam । <quote>“tasmādvēdādhyayanamēva pūrvamabhinirvartyānantaraṁ dharmō jijñāsitavyaḥ”</quote> iti
sthitam, athaśabdaprayōgasāmarthyāt । ēvaṁ cēnnēdamadr̥ṣṭārtham; nāpi dr̥ṣṭārtham,
﻿<pb n="014"/>
prāptatvāt; gurukulanivr̥ttirēva nivāryatē । <quote>“na brūmaḥ---anyasyāpi karmaṇō'na-
ntaraṁ dharmajijñāsā na kartavyā---iti, kiṁ tu vēdamadhītya na tvaritēna
snātavyam; anantaraṁ dharmō jijñāsitavyaḥ -ityathaśabdasyārthaḥ”</quote> ।।</p>
<p><quote>“ataḥśabdō vr̥ttasyāpadēśakō hētvarthēna”</quote> iti kasya vr̥ttasya
hētutāmupadiśati ? vēdādhyayanasyēti brūmaḥ । kathaṁ punarvēdādhyayanasya hētutā ?
adhyayanānantaramarthāvabōdhadarśanāt । atō'dhītavadēsyānantaraṁ dharmajijñāsā ।
tadidamathētyuktam । atō'nantarāvagamārthaṁ dharmajijñāsāhēturadhyayanam ।
﻿<pb n="015"/>
<quote>“yathā kṣēmasubhikṣō'yaṁ dēśaḥ; atō'hamasmin dēśē prativasāmi---iti”</quote>
(iti) pūrvōktasya vākyasyātaḥśabdō hētutāmupadiśatīti laukikārthatāṁ
darśayati । <quote>“ēvamadhītō vēdō dharmajijñāsāyāṁ hēturjñātaḥ, anantaraṁ dharmō jijñā-
sitavyaḥ”</quote>---ityathaśabdasya vyākhyānamēva pradarśitavān hētutvāvagamāya ।
<quote>“dharmāya hi vēdavākyāni vicārayitumanadhītavēdō na śak‍nuyāt”</quote>---</q>ityanē-
nādhikāraśūnyāṁ svārthavivakṣāṁ darśayati । <quote>“ata ētasmātkāraṇādanantaraṁ dharmaṁ
jijñāsitumicchēdityataḥśabdasyārthaḥ”</quote>। nigamanavākyamētat । <quote>“dharmaṁ jijñāsitu-
﻿<pb n="016"/>
micchēt”</quote>---iti kasya sūtrāvayavasya vyākhyānam ? dharmajijñāsāpadasyēti
brūmaḥ । nanu---dharmaṁ jijñāsēt---iti vaktavyam; prakr̥tipratyayayōrhi pratyayā-
rthasya prādhānyamityutsargaḥ; dharmajijñāsāpadē punaḥ prakr̥tyarthaprādhānyapradarśanā-
yāyaṁ yatnaḥ । <quote>“dharmāya jijñāsā dharmajijñāsā”</quote> । kathaṁ punaḥ ? prakr̥tyarthō
jñānārthaḥ, pratyayārtha icchā; īdr̥śa ēvārthē san smaryatē---<quote>“dhātōḥ
karmaṇaḥ”</quote>---iti । ēvaṁ tarhi jñānasya prādhānyam, na dharmasya । na hyananyārthā
kriyā pradhānaṁ bhavatīti dharmakarmikaiva sā pradhānam । atō dharmārthā jijñāsā ।
tadidamāha---<quote>“sā hi tasya jñātumicchā”</quote>---iti । uktā dharmārthā jijñāsā ।
﻿<pb n="017"/>
sa punaḥ kathaṁ jijñāsitavyaḥ ? kō dharmaḥ, kathaṁlakṣaṇaḥ, kānyasya sādhanāni,
kāni sādhanābhāsāni, kiṁparaśca---iti । ēvamavijñātō dharmō nānuṣṭhā-
nāyālaṁ bhavati; ananuṣṭhitō dharmō na dharmakāryaṁ karōti---ityuktam---
﻿<pb n="018"/>
<quote>“āsāṁ pratijñānāṁ piṇḍasyaitat sūtram---āthātō dharmajijñāsā---iti”</quote> ।
kēyaṁ kiṁparatā nāma ? adhikārābhiprāyamētaducyatē, <quote>“kva puruṣaparatvaṁ kva
vā puruṣō guṇabhūtaḥ”</quote>---iti ca ।।</p>
<p><quote>“dharmaḥ prasiddhō vāsyādaprasiddhō vā”</quote>-iti ca kō'bhiprāyaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="019"/>
yadi punarvēdādēvāyamarthō'vagamyatē, kimatra jijñāsyata iti । satyam;
vipratipannāstu maharṣayaḥ kēcit pramāṇāntarapūrvakamarthaṁ varṇayanti;
kēcinmantrārthavādānāmapi yathāśruta ēvārthē prāmāṇyamicchantyakāryē'pyarthē
vēdaḥ pramāṇamiti vadantaḥ । atō'syāṁ vipratipattau satyāṁ prārabhyatē
jijñāsā tattvāvagamāya । tattvēnāparijñātō'rthō'nuṣṭhīyamānō vihantyanuṣṭhātāram,
jñātvā'nuṣṭhitō niḥśrēyasēna saṁyunaktītyārabhyatē jijñāsā; sarvavicārāṇāṁ
pratijñāpūrvakatvāt । tadabhidhīyatē---</p>
﻿<pb n="020"/>
<p>cōdanālakṣaṇō'rthō dharmaḥ iti । <quote>“cōdanēti kriyāyāḥ pravartakaṁ
vacanamāhuḥ”</quote>---iti kāryē'rthē vēdasya prāmāṇyaṁ darśayati । tallakṣaṇō dharmaḥ---
iti vadan kāryarūpa ēvēti darśayati । <quote>“cēdanā hi bhūtam”</quote> iti ।
﻿<pb n="023"/>
yadi kārya ēvārthē vēdasya prāmāṇyam, kathaṁ tarhi bhūtādyarthāvagati-
rmantrārthavādēṣu ? tēṣāmapi hi kāryārthatā dvitīyē pādē vakṣyati । taduktam---
<quote>“śaknōtyavagamayitum”</quote>---iti । na ca pramāṇāntarāvagamyō'yamarthaḥ---iti
<quote>“nānyatkiñcanēndriyam”</quote>---iti darśayati । <quote>“nanvatathābhūtamapyarthaṁ brūyāccō-
﻿<pb n="024"/>
danā”</quote>---iti śabdasyārthāsaṁsparśitāṁ vadan pratijñādōṣamāha । kathaṁ punararthā-
saṁsparśitā śabdasya ? ucyatē---arthāsaṁsparśi hīyatē pramāṇam; tasya
bādhakajñānōtpattau satyāṁ na punaḥ pratipakṣavijñānaṁ tannimittamēvōtpadyatē ।
śabdē punaḥ spaṣṭē'pi bādhakajñānē punaḥ śabdanimittamēva pratipakṣa-
vijñānamudēti---aṅgulyagrē hastiyūthamasti---iti । tathā na śuktikārajatā-
diṣvasyārthasya saṁbhavaḥ । tasmādarthāsaṁsparśitvāccōdanāyāḥ tallakṣaṇō dharmaḥ
iti pratijñā nōpapadyatē । taducyatē arthaṁ cāvabōdhayati, arthāsaṁsparśī cēti
citram । yadi tāvat bādhakajñānāvagamyamarthāsaṁsparśitvam, naiva tat pramāṇa-
janyam; viśēṣāgrahaṇāt smr̥tijñānaṁ taditi pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ । vēdē punaḥ
bādhakajñānābhāvāt arthāsaṁsparśitāśaṅkāpi nāsti । nanu ca satyapi bādhakajñānē
laukikēṣu vākyēṣu śabdādēva jñānamutpadyatē, nimittabhāvāt---aṅgulyagrē hasti-
yūthaśatam---iti; tadarthā parihr̥taivārthāsaṁsparśitāśaṅkā, naivam । anabhijñō bhavān
﻿<pb n="026"/>
bādhyabādhakabhāvasya---aṅgulyagrē hastiyūthaśatam---iti pramāṇāntaradarśanamatra
bādhyatē, na punarhastiyūthaśatam । tadidamāha---<quote>“
bravīti ca, vitathaṁ cēti”</quote> । ata ēva <quote>“taccēt pratyayitāt”</quote>-ityuktam । pratyayi-
tasya hi vacanamavyabhicāri pramāṇāntarapūrvakam, yatrōpalabhyamānaviṣayam;
﻿<pb n="027"/>
yatra tu dvayaṁ nāsti, tatra pramāṇāntaraviparyayādviparyayaḥ । vākyārthē punaruktō'-
viparyayaḥ । kasmāt punaḥ pauruṣēyē vacanē pramāṇāntaraviparyayādviparyayaḥ ? jñātaṁ
﻿<pb n="028"/>
hyarthaṁ parasmai pratipādayituṁ puruṣāḥ prayuñjatē vākyāni; na cāpratītō'rthō jñātō
bhavatīti pramāṇāntarasaṁvādinā pauruṣēyēṇa vacanēna bhavitavyam । tadidamāha---
<quote>“aśakyaṁ hi tat puruṣēṇa jñātumr̥tē vacanāt”</quote> iti । nanu aśakyaṁ hi puruṣēṇa
tat jñātumr̥tē pramāṇāntarāt---iti vaktavyē <quote>“r̥tē vacanāt”</quote> iti kō'bhi-
prāyaḥ ? ucyatē---nanu ca kāryārthatvē'pi pauruṣēyataiva vacasaḥ prāpnōtītyasya
parihārārthamidamucyatē---jñātumr̥tē vacanāt---iti । nanu ca pramāṇāntara-
saṁvāditaivaṁ na pradarśitā bhavati । bāḍhaṁ pradarśitā; sāpēkṣatvanirākaraṇadarśanāt;
nāntarīyakānapēkṣatvasiddha‍yarthaṁ tu viśēṣōdāharaṇam । nanu---r̥tē vacanā-
dityuktē prāpnōtyēva pauruṣēyatvaṁ cōdanāyāḥ । ucyatē; vacanāt---
﻿<pb n="029"/>
ityuktē prāpnōtyēva kāryē'rthē vacanasya svātantryam । ataḥ puruṣaparamparāyāmapi
na pramāṇāntaragōcarō dharma iti siddham । kathaṁ punaridaṁ siddha‍yati ? puruṣa-
paramparōpadēśānyathānupapattyā kimapyupalambhakamastīti śakyatē kalpayitum, na
svātantryaṁ vacanasya । naitadēvam; upadēśō hi vyāmōhādapi bhavati; asati
vyāmōhē vēdādapi bhavati; mūladvayē sambhavatyētasmin parigaṇitapramāṇavyati-
riktaṁ na pramāṇāntaramastīti śakyatē vaktum । ataḥ pramāṇāntaraviparyayāsaṁbhavānna
svataścārthāsaṁsparśitā śakyatē vak‍tuṁ cōdanāyāḥ । tasmāt suṣṭhu prati-
jñātam---<quote>“cōdanālakṣaṇō'rthō dharmaḥ”</quote> iti । kiñca, puruṣavacanāt
---vijñātō'yamanēnārthaḥ iti niścayō bhavati, na punaḥ pramāṇāntarabuddhirupa-
jāyatē । taduktam---<quote>“api ca, pauruṣēyādvacanāt---ēvamayaṁ puruṣō
vēdēti bhavati pratyayaḥ, na---ēvamayamartha iti”</quote> । kimivārthāntarāvagatau
pramāṇāntarāvagatirbhavati ? bāḍham; arthānusāri hi tadā pramāṇamavakalpatē ।
﻿<pb n="031"/>
nanu vēdētyētadapi kalpanīyamēva। na, prasiddhakāraṇatvāt saṁvidaḥ; aprasiddha-
mūlatvāccārthasya। vēdētyētadapi tāvat puruṣavacanānnāvagatirbhavati, vikṣēpasya
sambhavāccittānām; kimutārthē? taddarśayati---<quote>“viplavatē khalvapi kaścit puruṣa-
kr̥tādvacanāt pratyayaḥ”</quote>---iti। kimidaṁ sāmānyatō dr̥ṣṭam? dvividhasyāpi
nirastatvāt kimanyadavaśiṣyatē, yēnēdamucyatē---<quote>“nanu sāmānyatō dr̥ṣṭam”</quote>
iti? satyamēvam; kiṁ tu viṣayāntarē sāmanyatō dr̥ṣṭamanapāstaṁ manyatē---
﻿<pb n="032"/>
<quote>“viplavatē  khalvapi kaścitpuruṣakr̥tādvacanāt”</quote>---ityuktam; tadānyathaivā-
rthō'nyathā śabdādvijñānam; tadidamupapannārthaṁ bhavati; asyāṁ kimupattau?
prasaktā khalvarthāsaṁsparśitā śabdasya śabdatvādviplutārthaśabdavat iti । satyam;
yadi viplutau śabdādayathārthatvam, ayathārthasya viṣayē śabdādavagamyē
sati, nāyathārthāt । tadidamuktam---<quote>“na, anyatvāt”</quote>---iti । anya
﻿<pb n="033"/>
ēvāyathārthatvē hētuḥ śabdādviṣayē syāt । athāpi śabdādēva viplavaḥ,
tathāpyētadanumānaṁ naivōpapadyatē; aduṣṭapakṣapratijñānasāpēkṣaṁ hētuvacanaṁ bhavati;
duṣṭaścāyaṁ pakṣaḥ, saṁvidaḥ pratyakṣatvāt । tadidamuktam---<quote>“pratyakṣastu vēdavacanēna
pratyayaḥ”</quote> iti । pratītiḥ pratyayaḥ । nanu naiva kāryō dharmaḥ । kastarhi ?
guṇaḥ । tathā ca kēcit dhīguṇaṁ manvatē, kēcidātmaguṇam । tasmāt
﻿<pb n="034"/>
kriyāyāḥ pravartakaṁ vacanaṁ cōdanā, tallakṣaṇō'rthō dharmaḥ---iti vacanaṁ
nōpapadyatē, akāryatvāddharmasya । atastannirākaraṇāya cōdanālakṣaṇasya tatrōpa-
saṁhāramukhēna upanyastavān bhāṣyakāraḥ tasmāt śrēyaskarō dharmaḥ ityādi ।
kathaṁ punarnirāsaḥ ? śabdārthasambandhasya lōkavyavahāragamyatvāt kāryārthē
dharmaśabdaṁ laukikāḥ prayuñjata iti <quote>“yō yāgamanutiṣṭhati”</quote>---ityēvamādinā
﻿<pb n="035"/>
pradarśitam । arthaśabdasyānvayaprayōjanapradarśanārthaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa---<quote>“ubhayamiha
cōdanayā lakṣyatē arthō'narthaścēti”</quote>; punarapi ca praś‍napūrvakamidamuktam---
<quote>“kō'rthaḥ ? yō niḥśrēyasāya jyōtiṣṭōmādiḥ; kō'narthaḥ ? yaḥ pratyavāyāya
śyēnādiḥ”</quote>---iti । niḥśrēyasapratyavāyalakṣaṇaṁ dharmādharmatvamuktam । ēvaṁ cōpa-
darśayatā ubhayaṁ cōdanālakṣaṇamityuktaṁ bhavati ।</p>
﻿<pb n="036"/>
<p>tatra yō niḥśrēyasāya, tasyaiva dharmatā kathaṁ nāma syāt; pratyavāyahētōḥ
mā bhūt---itīdaṁ tarhyayuktam । <quote>“kathaṁ punaranarthaḥ kartavyatayōpadiśyatē”</quote>---
iti । kathaṁ kartavyatayānupadiśyamānō'rthaścōdanālakṣaṇō bhavati ? kathaṁ
cōdanālakṣaṇasya satō dharmatvanivr̥ttyarthamarthaśabdānvaya upapadyatē ? punarapi
ca spaṣṭīkarōti---<quote>“naiva śyēnādayaḥ kartavyatayā vijñāyantē”</quote>---ityuttarēṇa ।
﻿<pb n="037"/>
kartavyatayā nōpadiśyantē, cōdanālakṣaṇāśca---iti saṅkaṭamivōpalakṣyatē ।
yadapi ca <quote>“kathaṁ punarasāvanarthaḥ ?”</quote>---iti praśnamullikhya <quote>“hiṁsā hi
sā, sā ca pratiṣiddhā”</quote>---ityuktam, tadapi pūrvāparaviruddham; <quote>“yaḥ pratyavā-
yāya”</quote>---iti pratyavāyalakṣaṇamanarthatvamuktvā punaḥ pratiṣēdhalakṣaṇamuktavān ।
tasmādasāmañjasyam । atha pratiṣēdhapratyavāyayōrapyavirōdhitōcyatē pratyavāyasya
﻿<pb n="038"/>
pratiṣēdhahētutvāt, tadayuktam; nañarthasyānanyārthatvāt; nañarthaparyavasāyyēva
hi pratiṣēdhavidhiḥ, na punastadarthasyānyārthatāmavagamayituṁ kṣamaḥ ।</p>
<p>atrāha---<q>anirūpitaniyōgavyāpārasyēdaṁ cōdyam</q> । kartavyatāviṣayō
niyōgaḥ, na punaḥ kartavyatāmāha । kathaṁ tarhi kāryē'rthē prāmaṇyaṁ vēdasya-ityuktam ?
yuktam, tadviṣayatvānniyōgasya । kō'yaṁ viṣayaviṣayibhāvaḥ ? yasminnayaṁ puruṣō
﻿<pb n="039"/>
niyujyatē, sa tadviṣayaḥ । tasmānnaiva vidhiḥ kartavyatāmāha, viṣayatayā tu
upādattē । tasmādyadyadupādīyatē, tattadvidhēyamiti tantrē vyavahāraḥ । yattūpādāna-
hētutāṁ pratipadyatē, tadadhikr̥tau kāraṇam । tasmādadhikāranimittatvamaṅgīkr̥tyaita-
﻿<pb n="040"/>
ktam---<quote>“hiṁsā hi sā, sā ca pratiṣiddhā”</quote>---iti । upādānagatō hi pratiṣēdhaḥ
kratvarthaḥ syāt, nādhikāragataḥ । <quote>“na hiṁsyādbha‍ūtāni”</quote>---iti cādhikāragatō'yaṁ
pratiṣēdhaḥ puruṣārthaśca । tasmādabhicārasyānarthatāṁ pratipādayituṁ kṣamaḥ;
nāg‍nīṣōmīyādēḥ, kratvarthatvāt । atha kasmānnōbhayārthaḥ pratiṣēdhō'yam---<quote>“na
hiṁsyāt bhūtāni”</quote>---iti ? na hyēkasya vidhēḥ prayōk‍tr̥tvāprayōktr̥tvē bhavataḥ ।
atha kratvartha ēvāyaṁ kasmānna bhavati ? prayōktr̥tvāprayōk‍tr̥tvayōḥ prayōk‍tr̥tvaṁ
śrautam, anapēkṣāvagatēḥ; aprayōk‍tr̥tvaṁ tu vākyāntaraparyālōcanayā-
vagamyam । na ca <quote>“na hiṁsyāt bhūtāni”</quote>---iti vākyāntarāvagatirbhavati,
anārabhya vidhānāt । tasmādadhikāragata ēvāyaṁ pratiṣēdhaḥ । bhavati ca
cōdanālakṣaṇaḥ, tadviṣayatvāt śyēnavidhēḥ । tasmāt <quote>“ubhayamiha cōdanayā
lakṣyatē”</quote>---ityēvamādyupapannārthaṁ bhāṣyam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="041"/>
<p><quote>“nanvaśaktamidaṁ sūtram”</quote>---iti laukikavaidikavākyayōḥ vivēka-
pradarśanārtham । <quote>“atha vārthasya sataḥ”</quote>---iti yathāvākyamapyēkārthatvaṁ
saṁbhatīti pradarśayitum ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="042"/>
<lg><l><quote>“tasya nimittaparīṣṭiḥ”</quote> iti hētvabhidhānāvasaraḥ kathyatē ।।</l></lg>
﻿<pb n="043"/>
<p>kathaṁ punaḥ kāryē'rthē cōdanaiva nimittam ? anyasya pratyakṣādērasaṁbhavāt ।
kathamasaṁbhavataḥ ?</p>
<p><quote>“satsaṁprayōgē puruṣasyēndriyāṇāṁ buddhijanma tatpratyakṣamanimittaṁ vidyamā-
nōpalambhanatvāt ।”</quote> atha kasmādanumānādēranimittatvam ? anumānādīnāṁ
hi nimittagrahaṇapūrvakaṁ svārthē prāmāṇyam; nimittaṁ cātra pratyakṣagrāhyamēva

﻿<pb n="044"/>
varṇādi; tasmāttadapyapramāṇam । nanu śābdaṁ pramāṇaṁ pramāṇāntarasāpēkṣamēva
lōkavyavahāra upalabhyatē । satyam; pramāṇāntaraviṣayamupalabhyatē, na
tu pramāṇāntarasāpēkṣam; svārthē hyautpattikī śabdaśaktiḥ । taduktam---

﻿<pb n="048"/>
<p><quote>“autpattikastu”</quote> iti । <quote>“vr̥ttikārastvanyathēmaṁ granthaṁ varṇayāṁcakāra”</quote>
-iti vyākhyānāntarōpanyāsaḥ kasmai prayōjanāya ? yadi tāvadda‍ūṣaṇābhi-
prāyaḥ; tadayuktam, samyagarthābhidhānāt । tadabhyupagatiśca sūtratrayasyā-
rthāntarapradarśanārthamiti cēt, tatrāpi vr̥ttikāragrahaṇamayuktam । arthāntara-
kathanēna vā vinā kiṁ na sidhyati ? ucyatē---dvayamapyasti dūṣaṇamarthāntara-
kathanaṁ ca । kimatra dūṣitam ? <quote>“nimittaparikṣaṇaṁ na kartavyam”</quote> ityētattāvada-
yuktam, nañō'śrutatvāt, astyarthasya nityaprāptēḥ । yadapi hētvabhidhānam---
﻿<pb n="049"/>
<p><quote>“prasiddhāni pramāṇāni”</quote>---iti, tadapyayuktam, vipratipattidarśanāt । svayaṁ
cōktam <quote>“nanu vyabhicarati pratyakṣam”</quote>---iti. nimittaparīkṣaṇēna
cāvyabhicāritōktā । sūtrakārēṇa ca tadēva pratijñātaṁ parīkṣyatayā; kathamatra
nañō'dhyāhāra upapadyatē ? vaktavyaṁ ca nirālambanatānirākaraṇārthaṁ ca, tacca
nōktaṁ vr̥ṁttikārēṇa; tasmādda‍ūṣaṇam । vaktavyaṁ punaḥ kimanyadarthāntaram ?
pūrvōktasya sūtratrayārthasya sādhanabhūtamanyadarthāntaramanēnōktaṁ pradarśayitum ।
tathā ca tatsatōrvyatyayaḥ, lakṣaṇābhidhānaṁ ca sarvapramāṇānām ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="050"/>
<p>yatpunaḥ pratyakṣalakṣaṇasyāntē <quote>“yasya ca duṣṭaṁ karaṇam, yatra ca
mithyēti pratyayaḥ, sa ēvāsamīcīnaḥ pratyaya; nānyaḥ”</quote>---ityavadhāraṇam,
kimanēnāvadhāryatē ? ucyatē---yasyēdaṁ dvayaṁ nāsti, nāsau mithyāpratyaya
ityavadhāryatē । kaḥ punarasau ? nāmajātyādiyōgēnōtpadyatē yaḥ ।
na cēdamasti tasya । tathā ca parairnārthāntarālambanatēṣyatē'sya,
﻿<pb n="051"/>
nirvikalpakapramitaviṣayataivēṣyatē vikalpamātramēvāyamiti vadadbhiḥ । sa
ēva ca saṁvr̥tirityuktam । na cāsminnapi rāddhāntē nirvikalpakapratyaya-
﻿<pb n="052"/>
pramitaviṣayataivēṣyatē savikalpakānāṁ jātyādipratyayānām । iyāṁstu
viśēṣaḥ---pūrvānubhūtārthānusandhānēnāsminnapi nirvikalpakapratyayapramitaviṣaya-
tā nāpaiti । anusandhānapratyayasyāpi nārthāntarānusandhānēna viṣayī-
taratvaṁ savikalpakasya śakyatē vak‍tum । tasmādarthāntaraviṣayatvāt
naivāsya mithyāśaṅkōpapadyatē, dvayasya cābhāvataḥ । tasmāttadarthamidramavadhāraṇaṁ
﻿<pb n="053"/>
mandataraphalamiva pratimāti । nanu ca tvayaivēdamuktam---iyāṁstu viśēṣaḥ---iti;
anēna viśēṣēṇa parairidamuktam---anusandhīyamānārthasaṁhitārthāntarāviṣayatvāt
naiva svaikapratyayaviṣayō'rthaḥ paricchēdyatāmasya pratyayasya pratipadyatē ।
ālambanatāṁ tu pratipadyatē । tasmānna paricchēdakatvamanusandhānapratyayasyē-
cchanti smr̥tivaditi vadantaḥ । iṣyatē cāsmin rāddhāntē savikalpakasyāpi
pramāṇatvam । na ca parēṣāmapyanusandhānapratyayē vikalpamātravādināṁ dvayamida-
mastīti siddham । tasmādasya pramāṇatvamicchatā kr̥tamidamavadhāraṇam । kathaṁ
punaranusandhānapratyayaṁ kalpanāṁ manyantē ? jātijātimatōrabhēdāt tadanusandhāna-
﻿<pb n="054"/>
pratyayē bhēdābhyupagamācca । ayaṁ gauḥ---iti laukikāḥ pratipadyantē, na---idaṁ
gōtvavaddravyam---iti । nanu ca bhēdapratyayē'pyabhēdōpacārō dr̥ṣṭaḥ---kuntān
pravēśaya---iti । satyamabhēdōpacāraḥ ; na punaḥ---ayaṁ gauḥ---ityatrōpacāra-
buddhirlaukikānām । tasmādupacaritō'yaṁ pratyaya iti na śakyatē vak‍tum ।
﻿<pb n="055"/>
na ca svalakṣaṇapayavasāyyavāya pratyayaḥ, athāntarānusandhānāt । atō
manyāmahē parikalpanaivēyamiti । yadyayamanyathāgrāhī pratyayaḥ syāt,
kathaṁ na viparyēti ? na ca gavādiṣu pratyayasya viparyayō bhavati । ucyatē---
yatra hi dravyaṁ dravyāntarātmanāvasīyatē, tatra viparyayō bhavati; na cēdaṁ gōtvā-
di dravyāntaram, nīlapītādivat viśēṣēbhyaḥ pr̥thaktvēnāgrahaṇāt । yata
ēva hi viśēṣāḥ sāmānyēnāvalambyantē, ata ēva ca pramāṇa-
viparyayābhyāmayamanyō vikalpākhyaḥ pratyaya iti vikalpavidaḥ । guṇakalpa-
﻿<pb n="056"/>
nā'pyanēnaiva vyākhyātā, pr̥thagagrahaṇāt । nanu nāmnaḥ pr̥thagēva grahaṇam ।
na, tatrāpi---ayaṁ viṣṇumitraḥ---ityabhēdapratyayāt । iyāṁstu viśēṣō
jātiguṇakalpanābhyām---yadēkatrābhinnayōrbhēdakalpanā, itaratra bhinnayōrabhēdakalpa-
nā । tasmādupādhiviśēṣō'yam, na kalpanāviśēṣaḥ । nanu ca karmakalpa-
nāyāṁ dvayamapyētanna saṁbhavati, bhinnayōrēva kriyākārakayōḥ sambandhō'va-
gamyatē; vyapadiśyatē ca । maivam; atrāpyabhēdōpacāra ēvāvagamyatē
﻿<pb n="057"/>
vyapadiśyatē ca---pacati dēvadattaḥ---iti sāmānādhikaraṇyadarśanāt । nanu ca
vaiyadhikaraṇya mapi dr̥śyatē---ōdanaṁ pacati, kāṣṭhaiḥ pacati, pacyatē dēvadattēna---
iti । kimidaṁ pralapyatē---vaiyadhikaraṇyadarśanāt---iti ? jātyādērapi
vaiyadhikaraṇyaṁ dr̥śyatē---gōrbhāvō gōtvam, paṭasya śuklatvam, asyēyaṁ saṁjñā---
iti । bhinnābhinnakalpanāṁ pratyabhinnasyāyamapyapadēśaḥ, na punarbhinnasya
cārthāntarasyōpanatirasti; tasmādiyamapi ca kalpanaiva---pacati dēvadattaḥ---
﻿<pb n="058"/>
iti । dravyē'pyēvam, daṇḍyayam---ityabhēdōpacārāt । tasmāt pañcavidhēyaṁ
kalpanā; nēyaṁ pramāṇam, nāpyapramāṇam । ucyatē---bhavati kalpanājñānam,
yadi pratyakṣasamadhigamyatā jñānasya syāt; ānumānikatvaṁ tu jñānasya vakṣyati ।
nanu apratyakṣajñānapakṣē'nyākāramālambanamanyathaiva jñānasyōtpattirnōpapadyatē ।
kō'yamanyathābhāvaḥ ? ayamanyathābhāvaḥ; śuktikā hi rajatavat prakāśatē ।
śuk‍tikālambanaṁ hi tajjñānam, na rajatālambanam । kathamavagamyatē ?
﻿<pb n="059"/>
śuktikāsaṁprayuktē cakṣuṣi darśanāt, andhasyānutpādāt; na hyandhaḥ
śuktikāṁ rajatam---iti vyapadiśati; cakṣuṣmānēva hi śuktikāṁ
rajatam-iti manyatē <quote>‘rajatasannitkr̥ṣṭaṁ mē cakṣuḥ’</quote> iti । ataḥ śuktikālamba-
namētajjñānam, na rajatālambanam । na cāpratyakṣē jñānē ētatsaṁbhavati ।
﻿<pb n="060"/>
atō'vidyamānākārālambanamapi jñānamastīti pratipattavyam । sēyaṁ
pañcavidhā kalpanā । nanu cāvidyamānākārālambanajñānapakṣē nirālambanataiva
jñānasya prāpnōti । maivam; nirālambanapakṣē na hyasyānyēna vyapadēśa
upapadyatē; bhavati ca vyapadēśaḥ---rajatamiti śuktikāyām । nirālamba-
najñānapakṣē hi kasya kēna vyapadēśō bhinnatvācchuktikārajatajñānayōḥ ?
nanvālambanajñānapakṣē'pi anyākārasya vijñānasyānyākāramālambanamiti
﻿<pb n="061"/>
nōpapadyatē । idamēva hyālambanasyālambanatvam, yadutātmākāramēva
jñānamutpādayati---iti; anyathā hi cakṣurādivat vyāpr̥tasyāpi
jñānōtpattāvālambanavyapadēśō na syāt । kēnōktam ālamba-
nākāranirapēkṣaivēyaṁ kalpanēti ? kathaṁ tarhi kalpanā ? arthāntarānu-
sandhānatayā । kimidam---arthāntarānusandhānatayēti ? idamidam---
yat svalakṣaṇāntarēṇaikatāpattiḥ svātmani ca bhēdādhyāsaḥ । kathaṁ tarhyavi-
dyamānajātyādiviṣayā ēva jātyādipratyayāḥ ? svalakṣaṇē hyavidyamānabhēdābhēdā-
dhyāsādavidyamānaviṣayā ityucyantē । kō'yamadhyāsō nāma ? vivēkā-
﻿<pb n="062"/>
grahaṇam; svarūpamātragrahaṇāt bhēdānanusandhānāt sāmānyādhyāsaḥ ।
abhinnasya cārthāntarēṇa sādr̥śyam; sadr̥śānanusandhānāt bhēdādhyāsaḥ;
sadr̥śānavadhāraṇaṁ tu bhēdānanusandhānāt । sēyaṁ pañcavidhā kalpanā ।
na cālambanavyatiriktaṁ rūpamasyāḥ । arthāntarānusandhānarūṣitaṁ tu---
na cārthāntaram arthāntarānusandhitayālambanamityataḥ, arthāntarānusandhānāt
svalakṣaṇālambanamapi kalpanētyucyatē । tasmāt svasaṁvēdyajñānapakṣa ēvaitadē-
kālambanatvē'pi jñānānyatvasaṁvēdanamupapadyatē । anyathā hyālambanamātrā-
﻿<pb n="063"/>
vagatirēva syāt, na svalakṣaṇasāmānyāvagatiḥ । svalakṣaṇavyatiriktaṁ ca na
sāmānyamastīti pradarśitam---rūpāntarāgrahaṇāt tadagrahē tadba‍udhyabhāvāt---
iti । arthāntarasyānusandhānācca । anusandhānaṁ ca jñānabhēdē upapadyata iti
upapannaḥ sāmānyaviśēṣavyavahārō laukikaḥ । ēvaṁ cānityē nityabuddhiḥ,
﻿<pb n="064"/>
asukhē sukhabuddhiḥ, anātmanyātmabuddhirityupapannāḥ saṁsārahētavō viparītagrahāḥ ।
tadidamuktam---<quote>“prāk bādhakajñānōtpattēḥ kathamidamavagamyatē”</quote>---iti,
ēkālambanābhiprāyēṇa sāmānyaviśēṣajñānayōḥ ।</p>
<p>na hyanyasaṁprayuktē cakṣuṣi anyālambanasya jñānasyōtpattiḥ saṁbhavati,
andhasyānutpādāt---ityuktam । ata ēvēdamucyatē---nānyākāramālamba-
﻿<pb n="065"/>
namanyākārasya jñānasyōtpattihētuḥ---iti । kathaṁ tarhi viparītagrahā
anātmanyātmādayaḥ ? ucyatē---viṣayāntaraṁ sadr̥śamavalambyāgr̥hītavivēkaṁ
yat jñānamutpannaṁ tat sadr̥śaviṣayāntarē smr̥tijñānahētutāṁ pratipadyatē---
smarāmi---iti jñānaśūnyasya । upapannāni tāvat śuktikādiṣu
rajatādijñānāni । anātmādiṣu svapnādiṣu ca katham ? svapnādiṣu
ca tāvat pūrvōktēbhyō viśēṣamabhidhāya nirālambanavādēṣu punaraviśēṣaṁ
﻿<pb n="066"/>
vakṣyati, ātmavādē cānātmādiṣu । tasmānnārthāntarānusandhānādhyāsa-
nimittaṁ jātyādijñānam । yattu---rūpāntarāgrahaṇāt tadagrahē tadba‍udhyabhāvāt---
ityuktam, tadasiddham; arthāntarānusandhānajñānasya hi svalakṣaṇajñānānya-
tvamiṣṭam । taccāpratyakṣajñānavādinō'rtha ēva prāpnōti । tasmādasiddhamidam---
rūpāntarāgrahaṇāt tadagrahē tadba‍udhyabhāvāt---iti । tasmāt sūktam---anyasaṁprayuktē
cakṣuṣyanyaviṣayaṁ jñānaṁ na pratyakṣamiti । kathaṁ tarhi viparyayaḥ ? agraha-
ṇādēva---iti vadāmaḥ । agrahaṇanimittatā ca darśitā bhāṣyakārēṇa---<quote>“yadi
﻿<pb n="067"/>
cakṣurādibhirupahataṁ manaḥ”</quote> iti । kathamanēnāgrahaṇanimittatā darśitā bhavati ?
<quote>“yadanyaviṣayaṁ vijñānam”</quote>---iti, asyāḥ pratijñāyā hētutvēnōpanyāsāt ।
yuktaṁ ca duṣṭatāyāḥ kāryākṣamatvam, na punaḥ kāryāntarasāmārthyam ।
tasmādagrahaṇanibandhanā ēva viparyayā iti । ataḥ siddham---<quote>“yasya ca
duṣṭaṁ karaṇam, yatra ca mithyēti pratyayaḥ, sa ēvāsamīcīnaḥ pratyayō
nānya iti ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="068"/>
<p>nanu sarva ēva nirālambanaḥ svapnavat pratyayaḥ; kutastatsaṁprayuktatvamata-
tsaṁprayuktatvaṁ vā, yēna viśēṣēṇa pratyakṣāpratyakṣayōrviśēṣa upalabhyatē ?
kathaṁ punaḥ sarva ēva nirālambanaḥ pratyayaḥ ? pratyayasya hi nirālambanatā svabhāva
upalakṣitaḥ svapnē । nanu śuktikāyāṁ rajatajñānam---smarāmi---iti pramōṣāt
smr̥tijñānamuktam । yuktaṁ rajatādiṣu; tatra hi śuktikāyāṁ yadbhāsvararūpaṁ
﻿<pb n="069"/>
cakṣuṣā paricchin‍naṁ tadrajatasmr̥tērudbōdhakamityupapadyētāpi; svapnādiṣu punaḥ
kasyacidagrahaṇādarthāntarē smr̥tyudbōdhaparihāraḥ śakya iva pratibhāti । tasmā-
dvāsanānibandhanamēvēdaṁ jñānajālamiti pratipadyāmahē । sadr̥śadarśanāt sadr̥śē'-
rthāntarē smr̥tērudbōdhaḥ; svapnē punaḥ kasyacidagrahaṇādityuktam । tasmādvāsa-
naiva nimittamiti laghvī kalpanā; nārthāntarāśrayaṇam, avyāptēḥ । ataḥ kuḍyā-
diṣvapi jñānaṁ vāsanānimittamēva, na kuḍyārthanimittamiti sthitiḥ । ucyatē---
kāryasidhyarthaṁ hi kāraṇaṁ kalpyatē, na punaḥ kāryavināśāya । svapnādiṣu ca
﻿<pb n="070"/>
bahiravabhāsā saṁvit; sā ca bāhyamarthamantarēṇa ca saṁbhavati; yēna ca vinā
yanna saṁbhavati, tattasya kāraṇam । tasmādartha ēva kāraṇamiti yuk‍taṁ kalpayi-
tum । nirālambanatā tu naiva saṁvēdyatē pratyakṣāvabōdhēna । tasmādakṣajaṁ jñānam,
na vāsanānimittamityuktam । nanu ca pratibuddhasya---svapnōpalabdhaṁ mithyā---
iti jñānamutpadyatē; na ca mithyābhāvasya kāraṇakalpanā yuktā । nanu cākā-
raṇasya mithyāpratyayasyāpyutpādō na ghaṭatē । satyam, na tvavagatyanuguṇaṁ tat;
﻿<pb n="071"/>
tadānuguṇyē hi mithyājñānataiva na syāt । tasmādva‍yāmōhahētavō mithyāpra-
tyayāḥ, vyāmōhanibandhanāśca sāṁsārikyō vāsanāḥ । atō vāsanānibandha-
namēvēdaṁ jñānajālamuditaṁ tattvavidbhiḥ । nanu parihr̥tamaitat---smarāmi---iti
﻿<pb n="072"/>
jñānaśūnyāni smr̥tijñānānyētāni । nanu smr̥tērudbōdhakāraṇāsaṁbhavānnaitat
saṁbhavati---ityuktam । tadasiddham, svapnādāvapi hi cintādr̥ṣṭādisaṁbha-
vāt; svapnē'pi hi sukhaduḥkhamanubhūyatē; sukhaduḥkhahētuścādr̥ṣṭam । atō'dr̥ṣṭahē-
tukamēva svapnādijñānaṁ kiñciccintādihētukamityupapannaṁ śuktikādijñānatulyatvaṁ
svapnādijñānasya । tadidamuktam---<quote>“stambhaḥ---iti jāgratō buddhiḥ supariniścitā
kathaṁ viparyasiṣyati”</quote> iti । kathamanēnēdamuktam ? niścitamavacchin‍namityarthaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="073"/>
kathamavacchinnō'rthō'navacchinnō bhavati ? kathaṁ tarhi pratibuddhaḥ---mithyā---iti
jānāti ? uktam---smarāmi---iti smr̥tipramōṣāt pratyakṣasaṁmitaṁ tat ।
pratibuddhasyācāpaiti pratyakṣābhimānaḥ । amumēvārthaṁ spaṣṭīkarōti---<quote>“atha pratī-
tistathābhāvasya hētuḥ, na śakyatē pratyayādayamanyaḥ---iti vaditum”</quote> । <quote>“yadi
pratyayatvāt”</quote> iti ca । nāvagatiṁ mithyēti manyatē; <quote>“anyatō hi svapnapratya-
﻿<pb n="074"/>
yasya mithyābhāvaḥ”</quote> iti pramōṣanimittatāṁ darśayati । kutaḥ ? indriyadaurbalyadarśa-
nāt---<quote>“nidrākrāntaṁ mē manaḥ”</quote>---ityādinā । daurbalyaṁ ca kāryāṁkṣamatvam,
na kāryāntarōtpattisamarthatvam---ityuktam ।।</p>
<p>nanu <quote>“śūnyastu”</quote> iti saiva nirālambanatōpanyastā pratyayasyārtha-
śūnyatāṁ vadatā; nirastā ca sā śuktikārajatajñānatulyatābhidhānēna ।
sa ēvāyaṁ nirāsaḥ punarākṣipyatē । kayā yuktyā ? saṁvēdyaviṣayatvāt saṁvidaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="075"/>
sā cātmanō buddhērvā jñāna ēva vā; sa ēvāsyā viṣayō yuktaḥ, yatsthā sā
saṁvit । ēvaṁ ca sa ēva saṁvēdya iti prāpnōti । tasmāt na viṣayāntaraṁ saṁvēdayituṁ
kṣamā । śabdasparśarūparasagandhātmakatā vijñānasyātmanō buddhērvā pratipattavyā । kiṁ
<quote>“arthajñānayōrākārabhēdaṁ nōpalabhāmahē”</quote> iti jñānaśabdaḥ pradarśanārtha ēvābhi-
prētaḥ ? na; saṁvidādhārē hi saṁvēdyē jñānamēvāvaśiṣyatē, budhyātmanōḥ śabdādi-
tulyatvāt । jñānāvinābhūtā ca saṁvit । suṣup‍tyavasthāyāṁ tasyā ātmani
buddhau cādarśanāt । jñānōpasaṁhr̥tirhi svāpaḥ । idamālōcyōktam---<quote>“artha-
﻿<pb n="076"/>
jñānayōrākārabhēdaṁ nōpalabhāmahē”</quote>---iti । kva punaridaṁ dr̥ṣṭam---viṣaya ēva
saṁvidā saṁvēdyatē---iti ? saṁvēdyatayaiva hi saṁvēdyatāmavagacchāmaḥ, na viṣayatayā ।
kēna vōktam nu saṁvēdyatayā saṁvēdyatāvagamyatē---iti ? kintu saṁvidaḥ
pratyakṣatvāt tasyāśca jñānātmakatvāt śabdādirūpatā tasyaivēti manyāmahē ।
kō hi nāma dvayōḥ pratyakṣatāṁ kalpayati saṁvidaḥ śabdādēśca ? tasmāt
saṁvidrūpamēvēdaṁ śabdādijātamiti sthitiḥ, na bāhyaṁ kiñcanāstīti ।
﻿<pb n="077"/>
nanu cāyathārthā saṁvit prāpnōti; śabdādyākāratvē hi saṁvidō grāhyagrāha
kasaṁvēdanaṁ nōpapadyatē । tasmāt kalpanā sēti kalpanīyam । na ca
sarvalōkāvagamyō'rthaḥ kalpanēti yuktam । na cārthāntarānusandhānānanuviddhaṁ
kvacit kalpanāśabdābhilapanīyaṁ lōkē dr̥ṣṭam । tasmādvaramubhayōḥ pratyakṣatā,
na punaravagatērapalāpaḥ । saṁvidēva hi tadā hīyēta, kasyēyaṁ śabdādirūpatā ? yuktaṁ
yadi grāhyagrāhakasaṁvēdanamākārāntarēṇa syāt; na cākārāntaramupalabhāmahē;
nīlādyakāramēva hyubhayaṁ pratibhāti । ēkākāraṁ cōbhayapratibhānaṁ kimanyadataḥ
pratibhānāt ? tadidamuktam---<quote>“arthajñānayōrākārabhēdaṁ nōpalabhāmahē”</quote> iti ।
<quote>“pratyakṣā ca nō buddhiḥ”</quote> ityētaduk‍taṁ bhavati---pratyakṣā ca naḥ saṁvit---
﻿<pb n="078"/>
iti । pratyakṣaścāyaṁ nīlādyākāraḥ । atastadākārēyaṁ saṁvit ubhayathā
pratibhāti । tasmādarthaśūnyēyaṁ saṁviditi siddham । ataḥ---tatsaṁprayōgāt
tatsaṁpratyayaḥ---iti pralāpō'yam । kiṁnimittaṁ punarubhayathā pratibhānam ?
<quote>“ākārabhēdaṁ nōpalabhāmahē”</quote>---iti pratyuktam । pratibhānakāraṇaṁ tu pratibhānā-
dēvāstītyavagantavyam । sā cēyaṁ vāsanānādikālīnā---ityuktaṁ śūnyavādibhiḥ ।
﻿<pb n="080"/>
ucyatē---ubhayapratibhānaṁ nīlapītādāvasiddham; grāhyatayaiva tat prati
bhāti; na grāhakatayā । kintu grāhakaṁ---grāhakamityēva manutē, na---nīlam,
pītam---iti vā । tadidamuktam---<quote>“sa hi bahirdēśasambaddhaḥ pratyakṣamupalabhyatē”</quote>
﻿<pb n="081"/>
iti । <quote>“arthaviṣayā hi pratyakṣā buddhiḥ, na buddhiviṣayā”</quote>
iti---grāhyatayaiva rūpapratibhānaṁ darśayati, grāhakapratibhānaṁ tu na
rūpaviṣayam । kiṁ tarhi ? jñānaviṣayam । nanu ca rūpāntaramēva nōpalabhyata ityu-
ktam; kathamatra viṣayāntarōpanyāsaḥ ? na hi; pratyakṣavādinō
hyayaṁ dōṣaḥ; ānumānikajñānavādinastu nāyaṁ paryanuyōgaḥ । nāpyanu-
﻿<pb n="082"/>
mānādūpagrahaṇam; sanmātragrāhyanumānaṁ bhavati । nanu ca saṁvit
pratyakṣētyuktam । anyā ca saṁvit, anyatsaṁvēdyam; dvayōrapi pratyakṣatvē rūpadvayō
palabdhyā bhavitavyam । na cāsāvasti । tasmāt sa ēva saṁvidviṣayāpalāpō
nyāyyatāṁ pratipadyatē । avivēkō'yamāyuṣmataḥ na hi phalē rūpāntaratēṣyatē;
rūpāntarasaṁvittau hi phaladvayāpattiḥ; ēkasaṁvēdyaviṣayaiva hyēkā saṁvit; na sā
vēdyadvayaviṣayā । kimasaṁvēdyaiva saṁvit ? na brūmaḥ---na saṁvēdyā saṁvit---
iti; saṁvittayaiva hi saṁvit saṁvēdyā, na saṁvēdyatayā । kēyaṁ vācōyuktiḥ
---saṁvēdyā, na saṁvēdyā---iti ? iyamiyaṁ vācōyuktiḥ---nāsyāḥ karmabhāvō
vidyatē---iti । karma ca saṁvēdyābhidhēyam, na saṁvit । tasmānna pr̥thak saṁvēdya-
﻿<pb n="083"/>
tayā grahītuṁ śakyatē । na cāsaṁvēdyaiva saṁvit, tanmūlatvāt, sarvabhāvānāṁ
saṁvēdyabhāvasya । kiṁ tarhyatrānumānikam ? phalamēva hi pramāṇamiti pramāṇa-
vidō manyantē । kimiti manyantē ? na punaḥ---phalamēva---iti sthitāḥ ।
kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? ēvaṁ hi laukikō vyavahāraḥ । kimidam---laukikō vyavahāraḥ---
iti ? idamidam---ākāradvayaṁ laukikāḥ pratipadyanta ityarthaḥ । siddhaṁ tarhyartha-
dvayam, vijñānasyāsaṁvēdyatvāt arthasya ca saṁvēdyatvāt । kimasaṁvēdyamēva vijñānam ?
﻿<pb n="084"/>
bāḍhamasaṁvēdyam, na tvapramēyam । kaḥ punaḥ pramēyasaṁvēdyayōrviśēṣaḥ ? yatra hi
viṣayasya svarūpaṁ paricchidyatē, tat saṁvēdyamityucyatē । ataḥ svasaṁvēdanaṁ pratyakṣa-
miti pramāṇavidaḥ । asaṁvēdanaṁ ca pramitijñānē, ākārāntarāgrahaṇāt । tasmāt
jñānaṁ pratyakṣamityayuktam । kṣaṇikatvāccāsya pratyakṣatā na saṁbhavati, pramāṇaphala-
yōrasāmpratatvāt । tadidamāha---<quote>“kṣaṇikā hi sā, na budhyantarakālamavasthāsyatē”</quote>
iti । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---svayaṁ pramāṇarūpatvānna pramāṇāntaramapēkṣatē jñānam---
﻿<pb n="085"/>
iti । taduktam <quote>“utpadyamānaivāsau jñāyatē, jñāpayati cārthāntaraṁ pradīpa-
vaditi yadyucyēta”</quote> iti । satyaṁ pramāṇaṁ pramāṇāntaraṁ nāpēkṣatē pramitau । na ca vayaṁ
pramāṇatayaiva vijānīmaḥ, taddhētutvādvijñānasya । na ca tadavasthaṁ jñānaṁ jñēyatayā
jñānāntarasyāpi vadāmaḥ; kintu tadavasthā tāvadastītyanumānasya viṣayaḥ; na
hyasatyāmavasthāyāmavasthāvatō'stitvaṁ śakyatē jñātum । tadidamuktam---<quote>“na
hyajñātē'rthē kaścidba‍uddhimupalabhatē; jñātē tvanumānādavagacchati; tatra yauga----
﻿<pb n="086"/>
padyamanupapannam”</quote> iti । nanu ca---jñātam---iti pramēyamanusmaranti pramāṇa-
vidaḥ । satyaṁ jñātaṁ smaranti, na tu---jñātam---iti । taduktam---
<quote>“satyaṁ pūrvaṁ buddhirutpadyatē, na tu pūrvaṁ jñāyatē”</quote>---iti । nanu
cēdaṁ lōkaviruddham;---jñātō hyaḥ---iti smaraṇaṁ vyapadiśanti, na punaḥ
---ghaṭō hyaḥ---iti । satyaṁ viruddham, yadi sarvadaivāyaṁ vyapadēśaḥ syāt;
<quote>“bhavati hi kadācidētat yajjhātō'rthaḥ san---ajñātaḥ---ityucyatē”</quote> । yatra hi
﻿<pb n="087"/>
---jñātaḥ -iti smr̥ti, sā pramāṇadvayavyāpārajā । tasmāt vivēkaśūnyamidaṁ
vacaḥ---<quote>“smr̥tēruttarakālaṁ ca”</quote>---iti । kiñca ubhayōḥ pratyakṣatvē'rthēna jñānasya
vyapadēśō nōpapadyatē rūpasparśayōriva । na cārthavyapadēśamantarēṇa buddhē-
rūpōpalambhanam । tasmānna buddhiviṣayaṁ pratyakṣam; arthaviṣayaṁ hi tat । ataḥ
siddhamānumānikatvaṁ buddhēḥ phalataḥ । yaścāsāvavivēkaḥ phalapramēyayōḥ pramā-
ṇāntarābhāvāt, sa tadviṣayō yuktaḥ । ataḥ pramāṇāpalāpa ēva nyāyyaḥ,
na pramēyāpalāpaḥ । ataḥ <quote>“kāmamēkarūpatvē buddhērēvābhāvaḥ, na tvarthasya
﻿<pb n="088"/>
pratyakṣasya sataḥ । na caikarūpyam; nirākārāmēva hi buddhimanumi-
mīmahē, sākāraṁ cārthaṁ pratyakṣamavagacchāmaḥ । tasmādarthālambanaḥ pratyayaḥ ।”</quote> kiṁ
punaḥ kāraṇaṁ tulyē phalāpalāpē pramāṇasyaivāpalāpaḥ, na tvarthasya pramēyasya,
ubhayōḥ phalāyattatvāt ? maivam; utpattau hyubhayōḥ phalāyattatā, na punaḥ
pramitau । kasyōtpattau ? jñāpakē hi phalē pramēyamēva hi jñēyam, nōtpā-
dyam; pramāṇāyattā ca pramitiriti utpattāvityasambaddham । pramitau kriyā-
kārakatvamaṅgīkr̥tyōtpattiruktā, na cāvagamyamānatām; jñānē tvavagamyamānatāpi
﻿<pb n="089"/>
phalāyattaivēti yuktam । kiñca jñānamātravādē hi jñānavāsanayōrēva janya-
janakabhāvaḥ, na jñānasya jñānāntarēṇa; atastantujñānōtpādē'pi
paṭajñānōtpādō nōpapadyatē । <quote>“dr̥ṣṭaśca niyatanimittastantuṣvēvōpādīyamānēṣu
paṭapratyayaḥ । itarathā atantūpādānē'pi kadācit paṭabuddhiravikalēndriyasya
﻿<pb n="090"/>
syāt”</quote> । tasmānna vāsanānibandhanamēvēdaṁ jñānajālam । kiṁ tarhi ? arthani-
bandhanamiti sthitam । ata upapannaṁ pramāṇalakṣaṇābhidhānam ।।</p>
<p><quote>“anumānaṁ jñātasambandhasyaikadēśadarśanādēkaśāntarē'sannikr̥ṣṭē'rthē buddhiḥ”</quote>
iti । jñātasambandhasya---ityucyatē, kasya jñātasambandhasya ? nanvēkadēśasya ।
naitadupapadyatē, darśanōpasarjanatvādēkadēśasya; na hyupasarjanaṁ padaṁ padāntarēṇa
sambaddha‍yatē rājapuruṣavat । puruṣasamudāyayōranupādānādēvāsambandhaḥ । tasmānna
﻿<pb n="091"/>
vidmaḥ---kasya jñātasambandhasya---iti । ucyatē---sambandhāparijñānanibandhanō'yaṁ
vyāmōhaḥ । kaḥ punarasau sambandhaḥ ? ayamasau sambandhaḥ---anumānamēkadē-
śadarśanādēkadēśāntarē'sannikr̥ṣṭē'rthē buddhiḥ । kasyaikadēśasya darśanāt ?
jñātasambandhasya । nanvasminnapi sambandhē ēkadēśasyōpasarjanatā tadavasthaiva ।
﻿<pb n="092"/>
upasarjanamiti nāyaṁ sambandhahētuḥ; tathā anupasarjanamityapi । ākāṅ‌kṣitaṁ pūraṇa-
samarthaṁ ca sambandhitāmāpadyatē । atra ca---ēkadēśadarśanāt-ityuktē; kasyaika-
dēśasya---ityākāṅkṣā, darśanasya dr̥śyapradhānatvāt, tajjanyatvāccārthāntarabuddhēḥ ।
ata ēva ca---atrōttarapadapradhānatā, atra pūrvapadapradhānatā---iti kvacit
kvacit sthāpitam । tasmāt prayōgasidhyarthaivēyamupasarjanasaṁjñāṁ; artha-
sambandhē hi yasmādarthākāṅkṣaiva hētuḥ, nōpasarjanatā anupasarjanatā vā; kasya
﻿<pb n="093"/>
gurukulam ?---ityēvamādiṣu darśanāt। ucyatē---vyāpyaṁ hi dr̥ṣṭaṁ vyāpakaṁ
gamayati; jñātasambandhasya---iti ca na vyāpya ēṣā ṣaṣṭhī; sambandhimātra-
vacanāddhi prātipādikāt ṣaṣṭhīṁ smaranti। ūcyatē---satyaṁ sambandhini ṣaṣṭhī;
﻿<pb n="094"/>
vyāpya ēva tu sambandhī bhavati । avyāpyē'pi hi vastuni vyāpya-
vivakṣāyāmēva yathā ṣaṣṭhī, tathā tatra tatra ṣaṣṭhyarthaṁ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ । tathā
ca laukikāḥ---mamāyam, ayaṁ punaranyasyāpi---iti vyapadiśanti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="097"/>
<p><quote>“tattu dvividham”</quote> iti । kimidaṁ dvaividhyam ? lakṣaṇadvaividhyaṁ tāva-
nnāsti,---ēkadēśadarśanāt---ityēkatvāllakṣaṇasya । atha pramēyadvaividhyamaṅgī-
kr̥tyaitaducyatē---ēkatra viśēṣādviśēṣō'vagamyatē, anyatra sāmānyātsāmā-
nyāvagatiḥ---iti; ēvaṁ ca hētumadbhēdāddhētōrapi bhēda uktō bhavati ।
kiṁ punaranayōrbhēdakathanēna prayōjanam ? lakṣaṇābhidhānēna cāvyabhicāritōktā
bhavati; tadarthaścāyaṁ prayāsaḥ; hētuhētumatōrdvaividhyaṁ bhavatu vā mā vā ।</p>
<p>atra kēcinnītijñaṁmanyāḥ anavadhr̥tasvalakṣaṇamēva kiñcidanumānēna
﻿<pb n="098"/>
sāmānyatō na gr̥hyata iti manyantē; tadbhramāpanōdanāyaitaduktam---<quote>“tattu dvivi-
dham”</quote> iti । adr̥ṣṭasvalakṣaṇaviṣayamanumānamasti kriyādiṣu । kathaṁ punaradr̥ṣṭa-
svalakṣaṇē sambandhidarśanam ? utpattimataḥ phalasya darśanāt---ityuktamupa-
﻿<pb n="100"/>
pāditamadhastādasmābhiḥ śūnyavādē । ataḥ sāmānyamātraparyavasāyyanumāna-
masti । darśitaṁ ca---<quote>“dēvadattasya gatipūrvikām”</quote>---iti । kaḥ punaranu-
﻿<pb n="101"/>
mānē vyabhicāraḥ yathā pratyakṣē śuktikādiṣu ? nanvidānīmēva dvividhaśabdēna
pradarśitam । nanvanānumānikē hyānumānikatvaṁ nirasanīyam, na punaranumānasyō-
ddhārō vaktavyaḥ । kaścātra viśēṣaḥ ? yē'pi hyānumānikamanānumānika-
micchanti, tē'pyanumānaṁ vyabhicārayantyēva । tasmādatrāpi vyabhicāra-
nivr̥ttirēva lakṣaṇābhidhānasya prayōjanam । kiñca pramēyē'pi saṅkaraḥ--- na
mahānasādiṣu dr̥ṣṭō dhūmaḥ parvatasthamagniṁ pratipādayituṁ kṣama iti kēcit;
﻿<pb n="102"/>
viśēṣā ēvāvagamyanta ityaparē; smr̥timātramēvētyanyē । tasmāt---jñāta-
sambandhasyaikadēśadarśanāt, yat ēkadēśāntarē jñānamasannikr̥ṣṭē-iti viśinaṣṭi ।
kimanēna nirākr̥tam ? smaraṇaṁ tāvannirastam, asannikr̥ṣṭē---iti vacanāt ।
apratipattirapi nirastaiva, buddha‍yutpādavacanāt । sambandhāvagamāt---
iti viśēṣāvagatirapi nirastaiva । nanu na buddha‍yutpādamātrātpramāṇaṁtā śakyatē
vak‍tum, śuktikādiṣu vyabhicārāt । asambandhasya tu darśanaṁ sambandhābhi-
dhānādēva pratyuktam । sambandhāvagamē ca pūrvānubhavō durnivāraḥ । ahō !
anubhavāvivēkinō mahān pramādaḥ । kiṁ pūrvadr̥ṣṭasyānubhavō na saṁbhavati ?
﻿<pb n="103"/>
anubhūtiśca naḥ pramāṇam । anyā ca smr̥tiranyō'nubhavaḥ । satyaṁ
sambandhasya darśanātsmr̥tiḥ ; sambandhyantarē tvanubhava ēva । tataścāsannaṁ
punaḥpunardr̥śyamānam---dr̥śyata ēva---iti tārkikāḥ vyapadiśanti,
na---smaryatē---iti । siddhaṁ cānumānādiṣu pramāṇatvamanubhūtēḥ । kiṁ
tarhi---<quote>“asannikr̥ṣṭē”</quote>---iti ? smaraṇābhimānaśūnyē ityarthaḥ । sanni-
﻿<pb n="104"/>
kr̥ṣṭāvamarśē hi smaraṇamēva manyantē । nanu smr̥tipramōṣatulyataiva prāpnōti ?
na, kāraṇāntarasya vidyamānatvālliṅgādēḥ; na hmatra pūrvānubhūtirēva
kāraṇam । tatra hi pramōṣaḥ smr̥tiviparyayē hētuḥ; iha tu liṅgādi pratyutpannaṁ
kāraṇamastīti siddhaṁ prāmāṇyam । tasmādatrāpi yatpramāṇam, na tadva‍yayabhi-
caṁrati---iti vaktavyam, uktaṁ ca । idamupamānādiṣvapi yōjyam ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="105"/>
<p><quote>“śāstraṁ śabdavijñānādasannikr̥ṣṭē'rthē vijñānām ।”</quote> kimidaṁ śabda-
vijñānāditi ? kiṁ śabdādvijñānam śabdavijñānam, śabdē ēva vā
vijñānam śabdavijñānam ? yadi tāvacchabdē vijñānam śabdālambanamityarthaḥ,
tadayuktam; na tasmācchāsanamavagamyatē; śāsanāddhi śāstram । atha śabdā-
dyadarthē vijñānamutpadyatē, tacchabdavijñānam; tatra viśēṣāvagatau kāraṇaṁ
﻿<pb n="106"/>
vaktavyam । uktaṁ ca---<quote>“śās‍tram”</quote> iti । śāstraṁ hi śāsanāt; taccā-
rthaviṣayē ēva vijñānē upapadyatē, na śabdaviṣayē । dvitīyē'pi pakṣē tanni-
mittatayōpapattēḥ siddhaṁ śāstragrahaṇāt । nanu ca śabdābhāsamapi dr̥ṣṭam---
<quote>“ēṣa vandhyāsutō yāti”</quote>---ityēvamādi; tadapi śabdādēvāvagamyatē; na
hi bāṣpāditulyaṁ kiñcitkāraṇāntaramatrōpalabhāmahē । parihr̥tamētat <quote>“taccēt
pratyayitāt”</quote> iti । lakṣaṇābhidhānēna cāyamēva vyabhicārō nirastaḥ ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="107"/>
<p><quote>“upamānamapi sādr̥śyamasan‍nikr̥ṣṭē'rthē buddhimutpādayati; yathā gavaya-
darśanaṁ gōsmaraṇasya”</quote> iti । sādr̥śyam&mdash;iti hi sādr̥śyam । gōsmaraṇasyēti,
anubhūtagōḥ puruṣasyētyarthaḥ । nanu ca jñātasambandhitā tulyā, sā cātra lakṣaṇam;
﻿<pb n="108"/>
tatra vānyatra vēti kvēdamupayujyatē ? bāḍhamupayujyatē; <quote>“ēkadēśadarśanāt”</quote> iti hi
tatra lakṣaṇam । <quote>“jñātasambandhasya”</quote> iti viśēṣaṇam । atō na gavayasthaṁ sādr̥śyaṁ
sadr̥śāvagatērēkadēśaḥ । kiñca asakr̥ddr̥ṣṭasambandhō hyanumānasya hētuḥ, asa-
jātīya vyāvr̥ttisavyapēkṣaśca; dvayamatra nāstīti pramāṇāntaram । kiṁ punaratra
vyabhicāradarśanam, yannivr̥tyarthamidaṁ lakṣaṇam ? kimanyadataḥ sadr̥śābhāsāt ?
﻿<pb n="109"/>
atra sāmānyamēva kaiścit sādr̥śyamuktam; na tatsādr̥śyam । kiṁ
tarhi ? tadēva tat, gōtvādērēkatvāt । nanu cātra pramēyamēva nāstīti
kēcinmanyantē । tadayuktam ; anubhūtamapi kāraṇāntarāvagamyaṁ pramēyamēvētyu-
ktam ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="110"/>
<p><quote>“arthāpattirapi dr̥ṣṭaḥ śrutō vā'rthaḥ anyathā nōpapadyatē ityartha-
kalpanā---yathā jīvatō dēvadattasya gr̥hābhāvadarśanēna bahirbhāvasyādr̥ṣṭasya
kalpanā”</quote> iti । kēyamanyathānupapattirnāma ? yadi tāvat - asyānēna
vinā sadbhāvō nōpapadyatē---iti । tadēvaṁ kāryataḥ kāraṇānumānamupanyastam,
na pramāṇāntaram । athēdamucyatē--- jñātasambandhasyētyanumānalakṣaṇam,
ajñātaścātra sambandhaḥ; tasmāt pramāṇāntaram- iti, tadayuktam; kathamajñā-
tasambandhaḥ śakyatē'vagantum--- ayamanēna vinā nōpapadyatē---iti;
﻿<pb n="111"/>
na hmanyathānupapattiḥ pratyakṣasamadhigamyā । kāryāvyabhicārasamadhigamyā hi
sā; avyabhicāraścāsakr̥ddarśanapūrvakaḥ । tasmāt dr̥ṣṭamadr̥ṣṭaṁ vā jñāta-
sambandhamēvāvagamyatē'nyathānupapattyā । ataḥ pramāṇāntaraṁ mr̥gatr̥ṣṇikai-
vēti । satyam; yadi yadyēna vinā nōpapadyatē tadēvāvagamakaṁ syāt;
﻿<pb n="112"/>
iha tu yannōpapadyatē, tadēvāvagamyatē । kiṁ cātra nōpapadyatē ? jīvatō gr̥hā-
bhāvadarśanāt anyatrābhāvō nōpapadyatē । tataḥ kima ? nātrābhāvasya gamyatā ।
kasya tarhi ? bhāvasya; na cāsau gr̥hābhāvadarśanēnōpapadyatē । bāḍhaṁ nōpapa-
﻿<pb n="113"/>
dyatē; na hi gr̥hābhāvadarśanēna vinā bahiḥ bhāva upapadyatē ।</p>
<p>nanu <quote>“dr̥ṣṭaḥ śrutō vā'rthaḥ anyathā nōpapadyatē”</quote> iti gamakasyānyathānu-
papadyamānatāṁ darśayati । agranthajñō dēvānāṁ priyaḥ-<quote>“dr̥ṣṭaḥ śrutō vārthō'rthakalpanā”</quote>
iti kimidamarthakalpanēti ? dr̥ṣṭaḥ śrutō vārthō'rthāntarasya pramāṇamityarthaḥ ।
<quote>“anyathā nōpapadyatē”</quote> iti kēna sambadhyatē ? pramityēti vadāmaḥ; anyathānupapadya-
mānatāmāpādayan arthāntaraṁ gamayati । kimatra jñātasambandhitā naivāpēkṣyatē ?
apēkṣyatē hi sambandhamātrajñānam, na tu sambandhitā; anumānē tu---<quote>“jñāta-
sambandhasya”</quote> iti ṣaṣṭhyā sambandhitaivāvagamikētyuktam ।
﻿<pb n="115"/>
<p><quote>“dr̥ṣṭaḥ śrutō vā”</quote> iti darśanaśravaṇōpanyāsaḥ kiṁ kāraṇāntaravyu-
dāsāya ? nēti vadāmaḥ, upalabdhō'rthaḥ-ityarthaḥ । śrutagrahaṇamidānīṁ
kimartham ? <quote>“dr̥ṣṭaḥ”</quote> ityēva vaktavyam । ucyatē-abhidhānāntaramēvēdam---
<quote>“dr̥ṣṭaḥ śrutō vā”</quote> ityupalabdhērvācakam ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="118"/>
<p><quote>“abhāvō'pi pramāṇābhāvaḥ <quote>‘nāsti’</quote> ityasyārthasyāsannikr̥ṣṭasya ।”</quote>
abhāvō'pi pramāṇābhāvaḥ---iti kiṁ pramāṇalakṣaṇamidam ? ōm---ityu-
﻿<pb n="119"/>
cyatē । kimanēna pramīyatē ? uktam---nāsti---ityayamarthaḥ ।
kiṁ ca tannāsti ? pramīyamāṇasya pramēyatā; ataścāpramitēḥ
pramāṇatētyalaukikamiva pratibhāti । lakṣaṇamapi---<quote>“pramāṇābhāvaḥ”</quote>---
﻿<pb n="120"/>
iti pramāṇaṁ na bhavatītyēva lakṣayati । asti cēyaṁ prasiddhirmīmāṁ-
sakānām---ṣaṣṭhaṁ kilēdaṁ pramāṇam---iti । na cāsya granthatō lōkataśca
﻿<pb n="121"/>
pramāṇatāvasīyatē । atō na vidmaḥ prasiddhēḥ kiṁ bījamiti । kimatra na
jñāyatē ? granthatastāvat pramāṇābhāva ēvāvasīyatē । <quote>‘nāsti’</quote> ityapyuktē
pramēyasyābhāvaṁ laukikāḥ pratipadyantē । kiṁ tarhyanēna lakṣitēna ? pramāṇā-
vagatyarthō'yamārambhaḥ, tadanusārī hyarthaniścayaḥ kathaṁ syāditi । ata
ēvēdamucyatē, yasmāt pramāṇāvagatyarthō'yamārambhaḥ । kimanēna pūrvōktānāṁ
pramāṇānāṁ svarūpamavasīyatē ? yatpūrvōktairēva svalakṣaṇairnāvasīyatē । sarvasva-
lakṣaṇābhidhānavākyaśēṣō'yaṁ granthaḥ; na hyutpādamātrājjñānasyārthē tasmin
pramāṇasya pramāṇatāvasīyatē । ataḥ svalakṣaṇamātrābhidhānāt niścaya-
﻿<pb n="122"/>
svarūpēṇa pramāṇabhāvasya samadhigamyamānatvāt sarvapramāṇānām, tasmāt
kāryapratyastamayāt <quote>‘nāsti’</quote> iti, anēna pūrvōktasyaiva lakṣaṇasya sādhutōcyatē ।
﻿<pb n="123"/>
kēyaṁ tarhi prasiddhiḥ ? prasiddhirvaṭayakṣaprasiddhivat । yadi punarvyavahārā-
nyatvāt kāraṇānyatvaṁ manyantē kiṁ kurmaḥ ? na hi vyavahārānyatvāt
pramāṇānyatvasiddhiḥ । ataḥ tallakṣaṇamēvēdam । idamēva ca tallakṣaṇam । tasmāt
prasiddhatvādaparīkṣyaṁ nimittam ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="124"/>
<p><quote>“nanu pratyakṣādīnyanyāni bhavantu nāma pramāṇāni, śabdastu na
pramāṇam । kutaḥ ? animittam, vidyamānōpalambhanatvāt । animittam
apramāṇaṁ śabdaḥ; yō hyupalambhanaviṣayō nōpalabhyatē, sa nāsti yathā
śaśasya viṣāṇam । upalambhanāni cēndriyāṇi paśvādīnām । na ca
paśukāmēṣṭyanantaraṁ paśava upalabhyantē । atō nēṣṭiḥ paśuphalā ।”</quote>
pratyakṣādīnyanyāni bhavantu pramāṇāni, śabdastu na pramāṇam---iti
kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? apamabhiprāyaḥ---yaduktam anapēkṣatvāditi pramāṇā-
﻿<pb n="125"/>
ntarānavagamyamarthamavagamayati iti, ētāvanmr̥ṣā । kutaḥ ? <quote>“bhavi-
ṣyaṁścaiṣō'rthaḥ”</quote> iti bhāvyatayā prāmāṇyamuktam, tadatra na saṁbhavati ।
kathaṁ punarasambhavaḥ ? kimaniyōgakaṁ vākyamastīti ? kimatra niyōgaḥ
kariṣyati ? pramāṇāntarāvagamyē'pi tasya darśanāt smr̥tyādau । tasmādviniyō-
gāvagamyamēvārthamālōcya niyōgasya viṣayō vaktavyaḥ । sa cāyaṁ viniyōgō
vidyamānōpalambhanaviṣaya ēvōpalabhyatē-<quote>“citrayā yajēta paśukāmaḥ”</quote> ityādau ।
﻿<pb n="126"/>
kātra vidyamānōpalambhanatā ? kriyānantaraphalabhāvitā । dr̥ṣṭārthatvācca vr̥ṣṭyādēḥ
anantaraphalabhāvitayā pramāṇāntarāvagamyataiva vastutō vak‍tuṁ śakyatē ।
saṁbhavati ca pramāṇāntaraviṣatvē kō hi nāmādr̥ṣṭaṁ lōkē svātantryaṁ śabdasya
kalpayituṁ kṣamaḥ ? tasmānniyōgaḥ praiṣādyartha ēva iti pratipattavyam ।
tadidam <quote>“kutaḥ”</quote> ityētasya praśnasya <quote>“vidyamānōpalambhanatvāt”</quote> ityuttaram ।
nanvēvaṁ granthē vyākhyāyamānē <quote>“paśavō nōpalabhyantē”</quote> ityādiranarthakō granthaḥ ।
upalabhyantāṁ mā vā paśavaḥ; sarvathā pramāṇāntarasāpēkṣaṁ śābdamityētāvadatra
﻿<pb n="127"/>
sādhyam । satyamētāvat sādhyam; kēna cōktamanyat sādhyamiti ?
anupalabdhyupanyāsō na ghaṭatē ityuktam । na na ghaṭatē, ghaṭata ēva; pramāṇāntara-
parīkṣayā prāmāṇyaṁ vaktavyam, na svataḥ---ityēvaṁparō granthaḥ । taccātra
pramāṇāntaraṁ dr̥ṣṭam । kathaṁ punaratra dr̥ṣṭāvagatiḥ ? kriyānantarabhāvitvātphalasya ।
kathaṁ tarhi kr̥ṣyādēḥ ? kiṁ kr̥ṣyādērnānantaraṁ phalamupalabhyatē ? kiṁ kriyāphalaṁ
﻿<pb n="128"/>
nāvagamyatē, uta prayōjanaphalam ? pāṭanaṁ tāvat bhūmyavayavānāṁ kriyāphala-
mavagamyatē, vrīhyutpattistu prayōjanaphalam । na ca prayōjanānavagamādadr̥ṣṭatōcyatē ।
atra ca prayōjanaṁ phalaṁ ca paśava ēvāvagamyantē, phalāntarānavagamāt । yacca
kiñcit havirvikārādyavagamyatē, na tatpāṭanādivat vrīhyādyutpattēḥ paśukāraṇa-
tayā śakyatē vak‍tum, adarśanāt । tasmāt pramāṇāntaraparīkṣaivātra dharma-
jijñāsubhiḥ kartavyā, na punaradhyayanāddharmāvagatiḥ । kathaṁ punaḥ svargakāmādiṣu
﻿<pb n="129"/>
vidyamānōpalabhbhanatā ? niyōgasya tāvanniyōgatvaṁ paśvādāvapahr̥tam; ēkaścāyaṁ
niyōgō'nubandhabhēdādbhidyata iti sthitiḥ । tasmāt sarvatra sāpēkṣa ityuk‍taṁ
﻿<pb n="130"/>
bhavati । atō yatra pramāṇāntaramasti, bhavatu tatra tathātvam; yatra nāsti, tatra mā
bhūta । tasmāt suṣṭhūktam---<quote>“śabdastu na pramāṇam”</quote>---iti । <quote>“dr̥ṣṭaviruddhaṁ ca
﻿<pb n="131"/>
kiñcidvaidikaṁ vacanaṁ pātracayanaṁ vidhāya āha---<quote>“sa ēṣa yajñāyudhī yaja-
mānō'ñjasā svargaṁ lōkaṁ yāti”</quote> iti pratyakṣaṁ śarīraṁ vyapadiśati । na ca tat
svargaṁ lōkaṁ yāti; pratyakṣaṁ hi taddahyatē । na ca ‘ēṣa yāti’ iti
vidhiśabdaḥ ēvaṁjātīyakaṁ । ca pramāṇaviruddhaṁ vacanamapramāṇam ।”</quote> kathaṁ
punaridaṁ pramāṇaviruddham ? arthavādō'yam; arthavādēṣu ca sarvē pramāṇa-
virōdhā guṇavādēna vyākhyātāḥ । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---nādyāpyarthavādā
﻿<pb n="132"/>
vyākhyāyantē---iti, bāliśabhāṣitamētat; na hyuktasyōcyamānasya vā
sthitasyākṣēpō yuktaḥ । anyatra viśēṣābhidhānāt । uktīcyamānatāviśēṣē
hi vivakṣyamāṇē sarvamanavasthitaṁ syāt । tasmāt sthitatvāt sthitatvamēva
vaktavyāvaktavyayōḥ kāraṇam । kiñca, atrōpanyastasya parihr̥tasya tatra punaru-
﻿<pb n="133"/>
panyāsō na ghaṭatē । ucyatē---sthita ēvārthavādanāṁ guṇavādēna vyākhyānē
idaṁ vacanamākṣipyatē---atra hi taduktō na bhavati; guṇavādō hi pramāṇāntara.
pratipattibalēnōpajāyatē । atra ca pramāṇāntarapratipattiḥ śarīrē ēva, na
śarīravyatiriktaṁ kiñcidupalabhāmahē; tacca <quote>‘ēṣaḥ’</quote> iti vyapadiṣṭam <quote>‘yāti’</quote>
ityanēna viruddham, dahyamānatvāccharīrasya । tasmādvidhitō'rthavādataścāya-
thārthataivāvasīyatē । kiñca, vidhau hi sati niyōgatō'pi tāvat svātantrya-
śaṅkā jāyatē; arthavādē sāpi nāsti iti prakaṭayati---<quote>“na ca
﻿<pb n="134"/>
<quote>‘ēṣa yāti’</quote> iti vidhiśabdaḥ”</quote> iti । ucyatē---na pramāṇāntarāpēkṣaḥ
śabdasyārthēna sambandhaḥ kastarhi ? autpattikaḥ । nanu ca lōkē pramāṇānta-
rāpēkṣitaiva sarvasya vacasō dr̥ṣṭā ? satyaṁ vyavahārē, na tvabhidhānē । yathā ca
lōkē'pyautpattikamabhidhānam, tathā sambandhaparihārē vakṣyāmaḥ । nanu
sarva ēvāyaṁ sūtrārthō vivr̥taḥ punarihānūditaḥ । satyam; viśēṣābhidhānāya ।।
﻿<pb n="135"/>
kaḥ punaratra viśēṣō'bhidhīyatē ? nanu ca sambandha ēva nāsti---iti pūrvō-
ktamākṣipya punaḥ samādhiḥ । nanu ca vākyārthō'yamākṣiptaḥ---<quote>“vidyamānōpala-
mbhanatvāt”</quote>---iti; padaviṣayamautpattikatvaṁ manyantē mīmāṁsakāḥ । kimana-
yānupāsitagurukathayā vikalpitayā ? yasmāddhi yaḥ pratīyatē, sa tasyārthaḥ;
na ca kēvalātpadāt vr̥ddhavyavahārē kasyacidarthasyāvagatirdr̥ṣṭā; anavagamya-
mānasya cārthasya kēnacitsambandha iti durvacaṁ vacaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi prasiddhi-
riyam ? anupāsitagurutvādityuktam । tasmādautpattikō vākyavākyārtha-
yōḥ sambandhaḥ ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="136"/>
<p>syādētadēvam; naiva śabdasyārthēnāsti sambandhaḥ; kutō'sya pauruṣē-
yatā apauruṣēyatā vā---iti ? katham ? syāccēnarthēna sambandhaḥ, kṣuramō-
dakaśabdōccāraṇē mukhasya pāṭanapūraṇē syātām । saṁślēṣasambandhamabhiprētyō-
cyatē bhavatā---kāryakāraṇanimittanaimittikāśrayāśrayiyaunādayaḥ sambandhāḥ
śabdasyārthēnānupapannā ēvēti”</quote> syādētat---iti yadi nityaḥ sambandhaḥ
syādityarthaḥ । idaṁ kimiti na syāt---<quote>“tasmāccōdanālakṣaṇō'rthō dharmaḥ”</quote>---
iti ? <quote>“syāccēdarthēna sambandhaḥ”</quote>---iti । asyābhāvē hētuṁ kṣuramō-
﻿<pb n="137"/>
mōdakaśabdōccāraṇagranthēna bruvan sambandhasyābhyupagamaṁ darśayati---<quote>“saṁślēṣa-
sambandhamabhiprētya”</quote> iti । kēnāyamabhyupagataḥ sambandhaḥ, yēna nirā-
karaṇīyatayā upanyasyatē ? nanu ca śabdasvātantryavādibhiḥ---
śabdādarthō'vagamyatē---ityayamēvābhyupagataḥ sambandhaḥ; anabhyupagatasya
nirākaraṇamandhapadam । idamēvātra nirākriyatē---yaduta śabdādarthō'vagamyatē
﻿<pb n="138"/>
iti । kathaṁ punaḥ saṁślēṣasambandhanirākaraṇēnēdaṁ nirākr̥taṁ bhavati ?
bhavati; śabdādarthajñānaṁ hi kāryaṁ kēnacitkāraṇēna; śabdādartha-
jñānaṁ ca na ca śabdādēvēti śakyatē vaktuṁ cakṣurādīnāmiva,
prathamaśravaṇādapratītēḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi dhūmādīnāmagnyādyarthāvagatāviva na
svarūpamēva kāraṇam । kiṁ tarhi ? sahāvasthānādilakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ ।
sa cāyaṁ śabdē na kaścidupalabhyatē prāgarthāvagamāt । tasmāt samba-
ndhāntaranirākaraṇēna vācyavācakatā nirākr̥tā bhavati । yadyēvaṁ sarva
ēva nirākaraṇīyāḥ; kimidamucyatē---yaunādayō na saṁbhavantīti saṁślē-
﻿<pb n="139"/>
ṣasyaiva sahētukaṁ nirākaraṇam ? athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---yaunādayō nōpa-
labhyanta---iti; saṁślēṣō vā kimupalabhyatē ? tathā ca---<quote>“kṣuramōdakaśabdō-
ccāraṇē”</quote> ityanupalabdhirēvōpanyastā । tasmānna vidmaḥ---kēna viśēṣēṇēdaṁ
nirākaraṇīyatayōpanyastamiti । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---saṁśliṣṭasyaivārthasya gamyatvaṁ
gamakatvaṁ cēti, tadayuktam; kāryakāraṇayōrasaṁśliṣṭayōrapi gamyagamaka-
tvadarśanāt । kāryakāraṇamapi tantvādi saṁśliṣṭamiti cēt, naitannimittē
saṁbhavati; tadapi hi kāraṇamēva gamyaṁ ca । tasmādidamandhapada-
miti pratibhāti । ucyatē---atra hyautpattikavādinaḥ kēcit---sva-
﻿<pb n="140"/>
rūpamēvādhyasya śabdō'rthaṁ pratyāyayati---iti pratipannāḥ; yukti-
ścōktā---svamēva rūpaṁ śabdasya, yēyamarthapariṇatiḥ---iti । ata-
stannirākaraṇam । tasmin pakṣē saṁślēṣa ēva śabdārthayōḥ sambandhaḥ । sō'yaṁ
kāryānupalabdhyā na ghaṭatē iti---<quote>“kṣuramōdakaśabdōccāraṇē mukhasya pāṭana
pūraṇē syātām”</quote> ityuktam । kathaṁ tarhi---gaurayam---iti tulyō
nirdēśaḥ śabdārthayōḥ ? astyayaṁ nirdēśaḥ, sa tu nādhyāsakr̥ta iti ākr̥tigranthē
vakṣyāmaḥ । <quote>“yaunādayastu sambandhāḥ śabdasyārthēnānupapannā ēva”</quote> ityana-
bhyupagamaṁ darśayati । <quote>“yō'tra vyapadēśyaḥ sambandhaḥ, tamēkaṁ na vyapadiśati
bhavān pratyāyyasya pratyāyakasya ca saṁjñāsaṁjñilakṣaṇaḥ ”</quote>---ityanēnau-
﻿<pb n="141"/>
tpattikatvaṁ punarupōdbalayati । <quote>“āha---yadi pratyāyakaḥ śabdaḥ, prathamaśrutaḥ
kiṁ na pratyāyayati”</quote> ? svatō hi sarvabhāvānāṁ pravr̥ttiścakṣurādīnāmiva rūpa-
grahaṇē; tasmāt sāpēkṣatvaṁ śabdasyārthapratipattāvastīti <quote>“prathamaśrutaḥ kiṁ
na pratyāyayati”</quote> ityuktam । <quote>“sarvatra nō darśanaṁ pramāṇam”</quote> iti svābhā-
vikānāṁ sāpēkṣatvaṁ nirapēkṣatvaṁ ca darśanādēvāvagamyatē; dr̥ṣṭaṁ hi
cakṣurādēḥ svābhāvikatvē'pi rūpāvagatāvapēkṣitvam, dahanē cānapēkṣitva-
magnyādēḥ । tadidamuktam---<quote>“sarvatra nō darśanaṁ pramāṇam”</quote>---iti ।
﻿<pb n="142"/>
dr̥ṣṭaṁ hi kāryaṁ puruṣaprayatnānapēkṣam, puruṣānupalabdhēḥ; sāpēkṣaṁ ca, prathama-
prayōgānavagatēḥ, prayōgāntarē cāvagamāt । <quote>“yadi prathamaśrutō na pratyāyayati,
kr̥takastarhi”</quote>---iti kō'bhiprāpaścōdakasya ? yadi tāvat---kr̥takaḥ
kāryaḥ, na sāmayikaḥ---ityabhiprāyaḥ, tataḥ siddhaṁ sādhyatē; puruṣāntara-
pratyayāntarānapēkṣitā---śābdaṁ pramāṇam---iti vadatō'bhiprētā cakṣurādī-
﻿<pb n="143"/>
nāmiva rūpagrahaṇē, na punarutpattimattāpi nēṣyatē; utpadyata ēva hi
sambandhaḥ, kriyāgarbhatvāttasya; kriyāyāścōtpattimattvāt tadanuvartī samba-
ndhō'pyutpattimānēva । atha kr̥takaḥ rajjughaṭayōriva puruṣayatnajanyaḥ
ityabhiprāyaḥ; tadayuktam; cakṣurādērālōkābhāvē kadācit kāryamakurvataḥ
tatsadbhāvē ca kāryaṁ kurvatō'pi puruṣāntarapratyayāntarānapēkṣatvāt sanbandhasya,
tathā śabdasyāpi sambandhaḥ syāditi । tasmādasamarthamiva siddhāntalaṅghanē
﻿<pb n="144"/>
bhāṣyaṁ pratibhāti---<quote>“kr̥takastarhi”</quote>---iti । nēdamasamartham; ayamasyābhi-
prāyaḥ---nēdamudyōtāditulyam; udyōtasyāpyanugrāhakatvaṁ kāryasamadhi-
gamyamēva, anavagatipūrvakatvādavagatēścakṣurādīnām । śabdē punararthāvagatipūrvi-
kaivārthāvagatiḥ; hi <quote>‘ayamasyārthaḥ’</quote> ityavagamya tataḥ śabdādarthaṁ pratipadyatē ।
tasmāt sanbandhāntarapūrvikaivārthāvagatiriti sāpēkṣatā । tadidaṁ kr̥takaśabdēna
sāmayikatvaṁ kr̥takatā vōktā ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="145"/>
<p><quote>“atha <quote>‘gauḥ’</quote> ityatra kaḥ śabdaḥ”</quote>---iti kō'yaṁ praśnaḥ ? ayamayaṁ
praśnaḥ---yadyapariṇatyā śabdō'rthamavagamayati, kastarhi śabdō'bhiprētaḥ ?
yō 'yaṁ śrōtrēṇāvacchidyatē, sa śabdō'bhimataḥ ? ōm---ityucyatē; śrōtragrahaṇē
﻿<pb n="146"/>
hyarthē lōkē śabdaśabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ; tē ca śrōtragrahaṇāḥ gakāraukāravisarjanīyāḥ ।
nanvēvaṁ satyarthapratyayō nōpapadyatē, kramavartitvādvarṇānām; kṣaṇikatvācca tadupa-
labdhīnām । upalabhyamānatayā ca padādivyavasthā, na tu sanmātratayā । tasmā-
﻿<pb n="147"/>
danupapannō'rthapratyayaḥ । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---upalabdhivināśē'pi tatsmr̥tyanu-
grahādarthāvagamaḥ---iti; sāpi na sarvaviṣayiṇī upalabdhivat; upalabdhya-
nusāriṇī hi sā; atō'pyarthāvagatirna ghaṭatē । tasmāt---śabdatattva-
mēvēdamartharūpatayā vivartatē---ityuktaṁ śabdavidbhiḥ । kiṁ vā vivartapakṣē śrōtrādi-
vyāpāranirapēkṣaiva svarūpē'rghē vāvagatiḥ śakyatē vak‍tum ? bāḍham; śabdādayaḥ
śrōtrādyavacchēdēnaikarūpā apyanēkarūpā iva bhānti marakatapadmarāgādiṣu
﻿<pb n="148"/>
mukhamēkamapyanēkarūpamiva pratibhāti । nanu ca khaḍgādiṣvēkaṁ grāhakam; upā-
dhayō hi khaḍgādayaḥ । tadēkagrāhakavaśāt <quote>‘ēkaṁ mukham’</quote> iti śakyatē vak‍tum;
bhēdāścōpādhinibandhanāḥ । atra punaḥ kimēkaṁ grāhakaṁ śabdādēḥ, yadvaśāt-
śrōtrādyupādhikr̥tō bhēdaḥ, ēkamēvēdaṁ vastu-iti varṇyatē ? kimidaṁ pralapyatē---
ēkagrāhakavaśādēkaṁ vastu-iti ? ēkatvādēva hyēkatvam । nanu cōktamēka-
tvamēva na pratīyatē-iti; śrītrādayō hi pratītēḥ kāraṇam । tē ca bhēdēnaiva
pratītimutpādayanti । pratītibhēdē sati <quote>‘ēkaṁ vastu’</quote> iti durvacaṁ vacaḥ ।
kathaṁ tarhi khaḍgādiṣu <quote>‘tadēvēdaṁ mukham’</quote> iti ? bimbākārapratyabhijñānā-
﻿<pb n="149"/>
ttadupādhinibandhanō bhēda iti śakyatē vak‍tum ? uktaṁ tarhi tvayaivaikatvam
<quote>‘pratyabhijñānādēkatvam’</quote> iti । asti cēdamēkatvaṁ śabdādāvapi---gaurayam,
śuklō'yam, surabhi candanam---iti । tasmādatrāpyēkatayā pratyabhijñānāt
śrōtrādyupādhinibandhana ēvāyaṁ bhēda ityupapannam । śrōtrādēḥ kiṁnibandhanō
bhēdaḥ ? viṣayabhēdapratipattinibandhana iti vadāmaḥ । viṣayabhēdapratipattēḥ kiṁ
nibandhanam ? śrōtrādibhēda ityuktam । ēvaṁ satītarētarāśrayatōktā bhavati;
bāḍhamuktā; avidyāmātr̥kēyam; ata ēvāvidyētyucyatē budhaiḥ ।
﻿<pb n="150"/>
tasmādvivarta ēvāśrayaṇīyastattvavidbhiravagatēḥ kāraṇam । atō na
śabdajñō dēvānāṁ priyaḥ, yō hi yutasiddhayōḥ śabdārthayōḥ sambandhamarthā-
vagatau kāraṇaṁ manyatē । <quote>“pūrvavarṇajanitasaṁskārasahitō'ntyō varṇō vācakaḥ”</quote>
iti । kō'yaṁ saṁskārō nāma ? yadi tāvadvarṇāvagatiḥ; pratyuktā, 
﻿<pb n="151"/>
smaraṇamapi tayaiva । atha smr̥tikāryānyathānupapattyā kaścitpadārthaviśēṣaḥ
kālāntarāvasthāyī vidyata iti kalpyatē; asāvapi prativarṇaviṣaya ēva
śakyatē kalpayitum, ēkaikavarṇaviṣayatvādupalabdhēḥ, tadanusāritvācca smr̥tēḥ,
tatkāryatvācca saṁskārasya । tasmādvarṇōpalabdhivadasāvapi na kāraṇam ।
﻿<pb n="152"/>
na ca smr̥tijñānaśūnyaḥ saṁskārō'stīti pramāṇamasti । darśayati ca
pratyēkavarṇaviṣayamēva saṁskāram---<quote>“pūrvavarṇajanitasaṁskārasahitō'ntyō varṇaḥ
pratyāyakaḥ”</quote> iti bruvan । tasmādupalabdhismr̥tibhyāṁ kimabhyadhika-
masyārthapratipattau sāmarthyaṁ manyatē bhāṣyakāraḥ ? sphōṭavādinō vā katham
---ityētadapyanuttaram; na hyabhyupagatirarthasiddhau hētuḥ । tasmādupavarṇanīyō'yaṁ
granthaḥ । atha kālāntarāvasthāyitaiva viśēṣaḥ, tanna; parasparāsambandhē kimava-
sthitiḥ kariṣyati ? athārthapratipattirēva sambandhē hētuḥ, ēvamitarētarāśrayatā
﻿<pb n="153"/>
prāpnōti । bhavatviti cēt, na tattvāvagamē yuktō'yamabhyupagamaḥ । kathaṁ tarhi
bījāṅkurādiṣu ? darśanāt---iti yadyucyatē, tata ihāpi darśanaṁ śakyatē
vak‍tum । na, vivartapratipakṣasambhavāt; arthāvagatirhi kāraṇamātrasya hētutāṁ
pratipadyatē, na saṁskārasambandhasyaiva । bījāṅkurādiṣu viśēṣadarśanādupapannam;
﻿<pb n="154"/>
iha tvānumānikatvāt saṁskārasya viśēṣōpalabdhirnōpapadyatē । tasmādvivarta-
mēvōpapannataraṁ manyāmahē । ata idānīmidamapyayuktam । kimayuktam ? sā ca
śabdakalpanā cēti । kathamayuktam ? vivartapakṣē hi kā nāmēyaṁ śabdakalpanā ?
yasmādadhyāsitōpādhyadhyāsitaviśēṣaṁ sarvapramāṇāvagamyamēkaṁ vastvityuktam,
tasmādaśabdajñataivēyaṁ yaduta bhinnayōrapi śabdārthayōrautpattikaḥ sambandhō/?/'-
bhidhīyatē । nanvēkatvavādinō'pi naivāyaṁ vibhāgaḥ śakyatē vak‍tum---jyō-
tiṣṭōmō'yam, darśapūrṇamāsāvimau---iti; ēkatvē hi na vākyaikatva ēvāva-
sthitiḥ, kintu sarvavākyānāmēkavākyatā prāpnōti varṇānāmiva padē, padānā-
miva vākyē । kasmāt ? ēkatvāvagamādēva; bhavati hi sarvavākyēṣu <quote>‘śabdaḥ
śabdaḥ’</quote> ityēkā buddhiḥ, sarvavākyārthēṣu ca <quote>‘śabdārthaḥ śabdārthaḥ’</quote> iti ।
﻿<pb n="155"/>
tadidamabhinnamēva jyōtiṣṭōmādi karmajātaṁ prāpnōti । dr̥śyantē cādhikārabhēda-
viruddhāścāviruddhāśca । viruddhāḥ viruddhaphalāḥ, aviruddhāśca aviruddhaphalāḥ;
na caitadēkatva upapadyatē । satyaṁ naikārthatva idamupapadyatē । bhinnārthāni
caitāni vākyāni । ēkārthapratipattyarthā caikatā; na cātraikārthatāvasīyatē ।
tasmādēkasmin vākyē padavarṇāpalāpō yuktaḥ । vākyāntarēṣu kiṁkr̥tō
vākyāntarasyāpalāpaḥ ? tasmānnēyaṁ viruddhāviruddhacōdanōpapadyatē ।
śabdaprāmāṇyavādinā hyarthasambaddhaḥ śabdaśabdēnōcyatē, na kākavāśitādyapi
śrōtragrāhyam । nanu śrōtrādibhēdamupavarṇayatā sarvamētadavidyājālamityuktam ;
﻿<pb n="156"/>
kimidamidānīmardhajaratīyamupanyasyatē ? anabhiprāyajñō dēvānāṁ priyaḥ,
yatō brahmaṇyasāvabhēda uktaḥ । tadrūpatayā kēna vā bhēdō'bhidhīyatē,
śāstrāvagatau ca kēna vā bhēdō'pahnōtuṁ śakyatē śrōtrādīnāmiva ?
satyaṁ nāpah‌nūyatē ; kintvavidyā prāpnōti ; vidyā cēṣyatē vaidikō'rthaḥ ।
kathamavidyātō'bhyudayaḥ śakyatē vak‍tum ? avidyā hi pratyavāyasya nimi-
ttam । satyaṁ yathā bhavānāha । pratyavāyastvāpēkṣikaḥ; sarvaṁ hi kṣayi pratyavā-
﻿<pb n="157"/>
yāyaiva ; kintu pratyavāya ēvaikatra sa ca upāyaścānyatra iti viśēṣaḥ ।
tasmānna kiñcidatra pūrvaṁ parēṇa virudhyatē । nanu ca vākyārthayōrbhēdē'pi
karmōtpattivākyairguṇavākyānāṁ kathamarthata ēkatā śakyatē vak‍tum ? uktam
---bhinnatvē'pyēkānuṣṭhānasiddhiriti nityakāmyaprayōgayōriva । tasmātsarva-
mupapannam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="158"/>
<p>syādētadēvam, yadyēkā buddhiḥ syāt ; na hyatraikā buddhirasti ।
nanu ca sarvaśabdēṣu <quote>‘śabdaḥ śabdaḥ’</quote> ityēkā buddhirasti ; asatyāṁ
caikabuddhau śabdaśabdavācyatāpi na syāt sarvaśabdānām । ēkanimittā hyēka-
śabdavācyatā, na punarēkatākr̥tā । atra caikaṁ nimittamasti śrōtragrāhyatā;
śrōtragrahaṇē hyarthē lōkē śabdaśabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇam---śrōtragrāhya-
taivātra gr̥hyatē, na punargōtvādivat śabdatvamēvāśrīyatē ? sāmānya-
viśēṣaviṣayamajñānamatrāparādhyatē ēvaṁ cōdayataḥ । kiṁ punaḥ sāmānyaviśēṣa-
﻿<pb n="159"/>
viṣayamajñānam ? idamidamajñānam---yasmin padārthagrahaṇē sati pūrvā-
vamarśō bhavati, tat sāmānyam; na ca gakārādiṣvēkavarṇagrahē sati varṇānta-
rāvamarśō bhavati pācakādiṣviva, tasmāt kriyānibandhanaivēyaṁ śabdaśabda-
﻿<pb n="160"/>
vācyatā; kasyāyaṁ vivartaḥ, kasya ca śrōtrādaya upādhitāmāpadyantē ? tasmā-
dviḍambanaiṣā <quote>“vivartatē'rthabhāvēna”</quote> iti । tasmāt kāryata ēva sambandhō'pi
﻿<pb n="161"/>
kalpanīyaḥ saṁskārāṇām, nōpalabdhismr̥tyōḥ, anavasthānadarśanāt ।
yadapyuktam-ayuktaṁ sā ca śabdakalpanā ca---iti, tatrāpyarthāparijñānamēvā-
parādhyatē ; idaṁ hi tatrōcyatē---paramārthasyōpādhikalpanā, avidyamānasya ca
﻿<pb n="162"/>
kalpanā-iti । tadidam <quote>“sā ca śabdakalpanā ca”</quote> iti । <quote>“surabhicandanādī-
nāmākr̥tigranthē parihāraṁ vakṣyāmaḥ”</quote> ityuktam । nanu ca---śabdādarthaṁ prati-
padyāmahē---ityētadidānīṁ laukikaṁ vacanaṁ nōpapadyatē । kiṁ gakārādayō na śabdāḥ ?
śabdāstē bahavaḥ, na śabda ēkaḥ; <quote>‘śabdāt’</quote> iti caikavacanaṁ padābhiprāyam ;
na caitat padamastītyupapannaivēyamanupapattiḥ । tathā ca śāstrakārairapi padābhi-
prāyēṇaivōpanyastam---<quote>“pūrvāparībhūtaṁ bhāvamākhyātēnācaṣṭē”</quote>---iti । kāmaṁ
mōpapadi ; anupapannārthamapi hi laukikaṁ vacanaṁ dr̥ṣṭam---daśa dāḍimāni
ṣaḍapūpāḥ---iti ; lōkē cānupapannārthamēva kiñcit dr̥ṣṭvā prayōgaṁ vyākaraṇa-
śāstraṁ niyamāya pravr̥ttam । iha punarnaivānupapattiḥ ; samudāyasya nimittatvāt
﻿<pb n="163"/>
kāryaikyāccaikatvōpacāraḥ । tasmāt śāstrakāravacanamapyanayaiva yuktyōpapannam,
padavākyānirdēśaśca---gauḥ padam, aśvaḥ padam, laukikaṁ vākyam, vaidikaṁ
vākyam---iti ca । tasmāt gakārādyēva padam, sa ēva śabdaḥ ;
nānyadva‍yatiriktamastīti siddham ।।</p>
<p><quote>“atha-gauḥ-ityasya śabdasya kō'rthaḥ”</quote> ?-iti nāyaṁ praśna
upapadyatē । <quote>“atha-gauḥ-ityatra kaḥ śabdaḥ ?”</quote>-iti yuktam ; varṇapakṣē'pi hi
vācakatā nōpapadyatē---ityāśaṅkānirākaraṇāya । abhidhēyē hi na
kvacidviśēṣaḥ । ākr̥tiḥ vyaktiḥ guṇō vā bhavatu ; na hyautpattikatvē
﻿<pb n="164"/>
kaścidvirēdhaḥ । asthāyī cāyaṁ pakṣaḥ; nāyaṁ rāddhāntē yaduta---ākr̥tivacanataiva
sarvaśabdānām---iti ; guṇavacanatāpyaruṇādiṣu dr̥ṣṭā, vyaktivacanatōdbhidā-
diṣu । tasmāt praśnastāvanniṣprayōjanaḥ । uttaramapi rāddhāntaviruddham ।
athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---udāharaṇābhiprāyam---iti ; atrāpi praśnastāvanniṣprayō-
janaḥ, ēvamuttaramapi । yadi śabdasya vyaktirarthaḥ, athāpi sāmānyam ;
sambandhē kō viśēṣaḥ ? viśēṣavivakṣāyāṁ ca prayōjanaṁ vaktavyam । athēdamucyatē---
﻿<pb n="165"/>
vyaktipakṣē sambandhasya sāpēkṣatā prāpnōti---iti, kā kathā pācakādiṣu ?
tatra kriyōpalakṣaṇamiti cēt, ihāpyākr̥tirbhaviṣyati । tatra hyabhihitā kriyā
dhātubhāgēna; iha tvanabhihitā jātiḥ nālamupalakṣaṇāya---iti cēt,
kalpyatāmabhidhānam ; na punaḥ sāpēkṣatābhidhānē upayōgamasya paśyāmō
nirapēkṣatābhidhānē vā । tasmānmandaprayōjanatā praśnōttarayōḥ ।</p>
<p>atrōcyatē---<quote>‘vācakarūpaiva sarvavācyēṣvavagatiḥ’</quote> iti manvānaḥ
<quote>‘śabdārthayōrbhēdō nōpapadyatē’</quote> iti pr̥ṣṭavān pūrvapakṣavādī । itarastu---avivē-
﻿<pb n="166"/>
kō'sya prayōgē'bhidhānē ca; prāyaugikīṁ buddhimabhidhēyē'dhyavasyatīti tadapanuttayē
<quote>“sās‍nādiviśiṣṭā ākr̥tiḥ”</quote> ityuktavān । pradarśanārthaṁ caitat abhidhānavat ।
﻿<pb n="167"/>
<quote>“nanvākr̥tiḥ sādhyāsti vā na vā”</quote>---iti abhidhēyatayā śabdarūpatāṁ
na jahātītyuktavān । nanu ca tadrūpāpattāvabhāvābhidhānē kiṁ prayōjanam ?
abhidhēyābhiprāya ēvāyamabhāva uktaḥ, na svarūpābhiprāyaḥ । <quote>“na pratyakṣā satī
sādhyā bhavitumarhati”</quote>---iti । yadi paraṁ svarūpasyaivābhāvaḥ sādhyatē, tadaivānabhi-
dhēyatā ; na cābhāvaḥ śakyatē vak‍tuṁ pratyakṣagamyatvāt । <quote>“vyāmōha iti cēt”</quote>
﻿<pb n="168"/>
iti । kēna cōktam---svarūpēṇaivāsyābhāvaḥ---iti । itarastu tamēvābhiprāyaṁ
buddhau kr̥tvā <quote>“nāsati pratyayaviparyāsē vyāmōhaḥ”</quote> ityuktavān । <quote>“asatyapya-
rthāntarē ēvaṁjātīyakō bhavati pratyayaḥ <quote>‘paṅiktaḥ, yūtham, vanam’</quote> iti yathā
iti cēt”</quote>---iti abhidhēyatayābhāvaṁ prakaṭayati । naivāyaṁ pratyakṣaviruddhō'-
rthō'bhidhīyatē ākr̥tērabhāvaḥ । kiṁ tarhi ? abhidhayērūpatayā abhidhānarūpa-
﻿<pb n="169"/>
mavagamyatē---ityuktam ; na cēdamavivartavādina upapadyatē । tasmādvivartapakṣa ēva
śrēyānityabhiprāyaḥ । <quote>“asambaddhamidaṁ vacanamupanyastam”</quote> iti paṅktyādāvapi
naiva śabdarūpāvagatirastītyabhiprāyaḥ । kathaṁ tarhyēkapratyayaḥ ? na ca śabdadva‍ya-
tiriktaṁ kiñcidanyatpaṅktyādiṣu ēkamupalabhyatē ; asti cāyamēkapratyayaḥ ;
tasmācchabdādhyāsanibandhana ēvāyam । <quote>“kimasati vanē vanapratyayaḥ”</quote>---iti
asati vr̥kṣavyatiriktē ēkasmin vanābhidhēyē'rthē ēkapratyayō nōpapadyatē iti kiṁ
pratyakṣasamadhigamyā vr̥kṣā api na santīti śakyatē vak‍tum ? kō'bhiprāyaḥ ?
vr̥kṣā ēvātra ēkatayā pratīyantē, na punarvanaśabdarūpatāvagamyatē । athāyamabhi-
﻿<pb n="170"/>
prāyaḥ---<quote>“vr̥kṣā api na santi iti,”</quote> tadapi hi śabdādhyastamēva rūpam---
iti ; pratyuktaḥ sa māhāyānikaḥ pakṣaḥ । arthaviṣayā hi pratyakṣā saṁvit, na
buddhiviṣayā-ityuktam । buddhiviṣayatvē vā saṁvidaḥ kiṁ sidhyati śabdādhyāsaḥ ?
anyā hi vr̥kṣasaṁvit, anyā ca vanasaṁvit । tasmād‌buddhiviṣayā vā bhavatu,
arthaviṣayā vā ; sarvathā vanaśabdarūpatā nāstītyētāvadvaktavyam । ataḥ <quote>“pratyakṣa-
mēvātrākṣipyatē”</quote> ityēvamādērgranthasyāsambaddhataiva pratibhāti । tasmādākr̥tisadbhāva
ēvākṣipyatē iti lakṣyatē ।</p>
<p>maivam; vanaśabdākāravādinō hi bhinnarūpāvagatirēvōttaram ; sā
ca vr̥kṣarūpādbhinnaivātra pratīyatē । yadi paraṁ tadabhāvādapratītiḥ ; sa
cābhāvaḥ pratyakṣē pratyarthini nōpapadyatē । nanu vijñaptiḥ pratyakṣētyētadupapadyatē
﻿<pb n="171"/>
ityuktam । na, bhēdāvagatēḥ parikalpanāpakṣapātitvāt। tasmāt suṣṭhu---
<quote>“pratyuktaḥ sa māhāyānikaḥ pakṣaḥ”</quote> iti । nanu ēkabuddhiranālambanaivēyaṁ
﻿<pb n="172"/>
prāptā । <quote>“atha kimākr̥tidbhāvavadī upālamyatē---siddhāntāntaraṁ tē
duṣyati vanē'pi tē'sati vanapratyayaḥ prāpnōti iti”</quote> । kaḥ punaratra siddhā-
ntaḥ, yō duṣyati ? ēkasmin vartamānāt pratipadikāt ēkavacanam-iti ।
bahavaśca vr̥kṣāḥ; tatra cēdaṁ prātipadikaṁ ityuktamāyuṣmatā । yathaivākr̥tirasti-
iti, tathaivāyamapi । tadidaṁ rāddhāntadūṣaṇaṁ bhavati । pramāṇāntaramūlatvāt
smr̥tēḥ yadi dūṣaṇaṁ bhavati, bhavatu nāma; na hyabhyupagamadūṣaṇāddhētō-
raduṣṭaduṣṭatā śakyatē vaktum; aduṣṭō'yaṁ hētuḥ pratyakṣāvagatirnāma । tasmādyadyē-
﻿<pb n="173"/>
katvamantarēṇāpyēkavacanam, kiṁ kurmaḥ; kamupālabhēmahi ? na cāyamupālambhasya
viṣayaḥ । ēkasminnēkavacanam---iti prāyikamētat, dārādiṣu vyabhi-
cārāt । prāyaugikamidamēkavacanam, nānvayikam । ataḥ siddhāntāparijñānamē-
vātra garhaṇīyam । tasmānna kvacit śabdādhyastā buddhirastītyupapannaṁ jaimi-
﻿<pb n="174"/>
nērvacaḥ---ākr̥tiḥ śabdārthaḥ---iti । ākr̥tipratipattimukhēna gōśabdādīnāṁ
nimittatēti, tatrākr̥tyadhikaraṇē nipuṇataramupapādayiṣyati ।।</p>
<p><quote>“atha sambandhaḥ ka iti ? yacchabdē vijñātē'rthō vijñāyatē”</quote> । kaḥ
punarayaṁ sambandhaḥ pr̥ṣṭaścōpanyastaśca ? pūrvōkta ēvēti vadāmaḥ । nanu cāsau
saṁjñāsaṁjñilakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ; tasmādanya ēvāyaṁ sambandha iti manyatē । tadayuktam;
﻿<pb n="175"/>
tatrāpi <quote>“pratyāyyasya pratyāyakasya ca yaḥ <q>saṁjñāsaṁjñilakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ”</quote> iti
sa ēvāyaṁ jñāpyajñāpakalakṣaṇaḥ sambandha uktaḥ । nanu <quote>“pratyāyyasya
pratyāyakasya ca yaḥ saṁjñāsaṁjñilakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ”</quote> iti vadatā---pratyāyyasya
pratyāyakasya iti ṣaṣṭhyabhidhānēna sambandhāntaramuktaṁ bhavati । maivam; tadēvēdaṁ
pratyāyyapratyāyakatvaṁ saṁjñāsaṁjñilakṣaṇamiti ṣaṣṭhyā pratipāditam । kuta ētat ?
nanu vyatirēkaṁ ṣaṣṭhī pratipādayati । astyēvātra hētuhētumattayā vyatirēkaḥ;
pratyāyyapratyāyakatvaṁ saṁjñāsaṁjñilakṣaṇasambandhasyābhidhānē nimittam; anyathā
pratyāyyapratyāyakōpanyāsō'narthakaḥ; tamēkaṁ na vyapadiśati bhavān, yaḥ
﻿<pb n="176"/>
saṁjñāsaṁjñilakṣaṇa.-iti vaktavyam । ata ēva<quote>“sa tu kr̥taka iti pūrvamupapāditam”</quote> 
ityanēna granthēna pūrvōktasyaivāyamupanyāsa iti prakaṭayati । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ
praś‍nōpanyāsayōḥ? idamatra kāraṇam---vivartākṣēpē hi yutasiddhayōranapēkṣatvaṁ
na śakyatē vak‍tumiti manvānasya praś‍naḥ । śakyatē vr̥ddhavyavahārasyānādi-
﻿<pb n="177"/>
tayānapēkṣatā vak‍tumiti tasyaivōpanyāsaḥ-<quote>“sa tu kr̥takaḥ”</quote> iti pūrvōpavarṇitēnai-
vābhiprāyēṇōktam <quote>“tasmānmanyāmahē---kēnāpi puruṣēṇa śabdānāmarthaiḥ
saha sambandhaṁ kr̥tvā saṁvyavahartuṁ vēdāḥ praṇītāḥ iti”</quote>---sāpēkṣatvamupasaṁ-
hr̥tam । <quote>“tadidānīmucyatē---apauruṣēyatvāt sambandhasya siddhamiti”</quote> ।
vr̥ddhavyavahārasyānāditābhidhanōpanyāsō'yam । kimidaṁ tarhi praśnōttaram ?
katham iti pr̥ṣṭē <quote>“puruṣasya sambandhurabhāvāt”</quote>---ityuttaramayuktam ।
﻿<pb n="178"/>
vr̥ddhavyavahārasyānāditāpratipakṣanirāsāyēdamupanyastam । kathaṁ punaridaṁ
pratipakṣatayā śaṅkyatē ? bāḍhamāśaṅkyatē; anādināpi vr̥ddhavyavahārēṇa
śabdādarthāvagamasiddhau yatra kartōpalabhyatē, tatrādimattaivōpalabdhibalātprāpnōti
<quote>“vr̥ddhiraudac”</quote> itivat । tasmāt karturupalambhō nirākaraṇīyaḥ । <quote>“kathaṁ
sambandhā nāsti ?”</quote>---ityasya praśnasya kimidamuttaramupapadyatē---<quote>“pratyakṣasya
pramāṇasyābhāvāt tatpūrvakatvāccētarēṣām”</quote>---iti ? kathaṁ nōpapadyatē ?
anumānādērapi pramāṇatvābhyupagamāt । tatpūrvakatvaṁ cāyuktam, śabdasya sāpē-
﻿<pb n="179"/>
kṣatvaprasaṅgāt, kriyādiṣu cānanumēyatāpattēḥ । sāpēkṣatvē ca śabdasyautpattika-
tvaprayāsō'narthaka ēva । tadidamāpatitam---ghōṭārūḍhasya vismr̥tō ghōṭa iti ।
abhiprāyānabhijñasyēdaṁ cōdyam; kēvalānumānāgamagamyatā tāvanna saṁbhavatya-
nādau vr̥ddhavyavahārē pratyarthini । tasmāt pratyakṣaṁ tatpūrvakaṁ cāgamānumānaṁ
﻿<pb n="180"/>
niranīyamiti । tasmādupapannamuttaram । bahuvacanamidānīṁ kimartham---<quote>“itarē-
ṣām”</quote> iti ? itarayōriti vaktavyam, dvayōrāśaṅkanīyatōpanyāsāt । dvayōrā-
śaṅkanīyatōpanyāsaḥ, asambhavastu sarvēṣāmityupapannaṁ bahuvacanam ।</p>
<p><quote>“nanu ciravr̥ttatvāt”</quote> ityasiddhatāmāha । kathamasiddhatā ? pūrvajānāṁ
pratyakṣaviṣayatōpapattēḥ । <quote>“na hi ciravr̥ttaḥ san na smaryēta”</quote> iti । na pūrva-
jānāmapi pratyakṣamatra saṁbhavatītyabhiprāyaḥ । yadi syāt pāṇinivat smaryēta
﻿<pb n="181"/>
<quote>“na ca himavadādiṣu kūpārāmādivadasmaraṇaṁ bhavitumarhati”</quote> । tatrāsmaraṇē
hēturupapadyatē puruṣaviyōgādiḥ । na ca puruṣaviyōgaḥ śabdānāmasti
﻿<pb n="182"/>
iti---kimabhiprētam ? kr̥takapakṣē hi tatprāmāṇyāt prāmāṇyaṁ syāt;
na niṣprayōjanatayā vicchēdaḥ smaraṇasyōpapadyatē---ityabhiprāyaḥ । tacca
pāṇinipiṅgalōpanyāsēna prakaṭitam । <quote>“yadyapi ca vismaraṇamupapadyatē tathāpi
na pramāṇamantarēṇa sambandhāraṁ pratipadyēmahi; yathā vidyamānasyānupalambhō
bhavatīti naitāvatā vinā pramāṇēna śaśaviṣāṇaṁ pratipadyēmahi”</quote> । <quote>“yadyapi ca
vismaraṇamupapadyēta”</quote> iti kiṁ viṣayamidaṁ vismaraṇamupanyastam ? yadi tāvat
﻿<pb n="183"/>
sādhyaviṣayam tadidamēva pramāṇam---yaduta vismaraṇōpapattiḥ । uktaṁ ca---
<quote>“vismaraṇamupapadyatē”</quote> iti---tadā na pramāṇamantarēṇa sambandhāraṁ pratipadyē-
mahītyahētuḥ । yadapyucyatē <quote>“vidyamānasyāpyanupalambhanaṁ bhavatīti naitāvatā
vinā pramāṇēna śaśaviṣāṇaṁ pratipadyāmahē”</quote> iti, idamapyayuktam; yadi
vidyamānasyaiva anupalabdhiḥ; kēna śakyatē vak‍tum---śaśaviṣāṇaṁ prati-
padyāmahē, śaśaviṣāṇaṁ nāsti---iti ? athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---yadyapyanyatra
vismaraṇōpapattirdr̥ṣṭā, naitāvatānyatrāpi vismaraṇōpapattiḥ śakyatē vak‍tum
---iti ? asadabhiprāyō'yam; bāḍhamanyatra dr̥ṣṭamanyatra bhavatītyucyatē;
ayamēva hi sāmānyatō dr̥ṣṭasya viṣayaḥ । atrābhidhīyatē---naivēyaṁ pramāṇa-
﻿<pb n="184"/>
tayōpanyasyatē vismr̥tiranupalabdhirvā, kiṁ tu upalabdhasyārthasya kāraṇadōṣa-
nirākaraṇāyēdamupanyasyatē । iha punarbhavatānupalabdhāvēvēdamupanyastamiti
asambaddhamityuktam । yathā ghaṭādērupalabdhasyānupalabdhirastīti naitāvatā śaśa-
viṣāṇasyāstitvaṁ śakyatē vak‍tum । upalabdhiviṣayasyānupalabdhiḥ kāraṇāntara-
mapēkṣatē; anupalabdhē punaranupalabdhērēvānupalabdhiḥ । tasmāt sūktamidam ।
﻿<pb n="185"/>
<p><quote>“nanvarthāpattyā”</quote> iti kimiyaṁ pramāṇasaṁjñōpanyastā ? ōmityu-
cyatē । kiṁ punaratra <quote>‘nōpapadyatē’</quote>---ityanayā buddha‍yā parigr̥hyatē ?
nanu sambandhasya kartā । kathaṁ punarasau nōpapadyatē ? prathamaśravaṇē'rthāna-
vagatēḥ । yadi prathamaśravaṇē'rthaṁ na pratipadyatē, kimāyātaṁ sambandhasya
kartuḥ ? ēvaṁ tarhi yadi gr̥hē dēvadattō nōpalabhyatē, kimāyātaṁ
bahirbhāvasya ? na brūmaḥ---bahirbhāvō nōpapadyatē---iti । kiṁ
tarhi ? vidyāmānatā nōpapadyatē---ityuktam । saivēyam---bahirasti
﻿<pb n="186"/>
---iti saṁvit । iha punaḥ prathamaśravaṇē'rthānavagatēḥ sambandhasya kartrā kaḥ
sambandhō dr̥ṣṭaḥ? athēdaṁ manasi viparivartatē---na prathamaśravaṇātpratipadyantē,
pratipadyantē ca dvitīyādiśravaṇē; tasmāt śabdādanyat kāraṇāntaraṁ mr̥gyami-
ti? kāryatastarhīdaṁ kāraṇānumānamupanyastam। kathaṁ tarhi <quote>“artāpattyā”</quote>  iti?
arthādanumānāpattirityarthaḥ। kasmāt? kāryādarthāt---ityuktam। nanu cānumā-
namapi nōpapadyatē, prathamaśravaṇādapratītēranaikāntyāt, vēdavākyādēva prathama-
﻿<pb n="187"/>
