śrutādavagatēḥ । nanu ca padagatēyaṁ cintā । kimidaṁ padaṁ nāma ? gavādayaḥ---
dēvadatta gāmabhyāja---ityēvamādiṣu vākyēṣu । kiṁ kāryānyatayā prasiddhāḥ,
uta vākyārthāvagatirēva kāryam ? bāḍhaṁ kāryānyatayā prasiddhāḥ । kasmin ?
vyavahārē । kēna vr̥ddhā vyavaharanti ? <quote>‘dēvadatta gāmabhyāja śuklām’</quote>---ityā-
﻿<pb n="188"/>
dinā । ēvaṁ tarhi vākyārthēna vyavahāraḥ । na hi vyavahārāprasiddhō'rthaḥ
kāryāntaratayā śakyatē'vagantum । kathaṁ tarhi---<quote>“atha gaurityasya
śabdasya kō'rthaḥ? sās‍nādiviśiṣṭā ākr̥tiḥ”</quote>---iti cōttaramasati
kāryānyatvē ? kathaṁ vā vr̥ddhavyavahārēṇāsyautpattikatvābhidhānam ?
tasmāt pratijñāsādhanayōryathaikavākyatā bhavati, tathāyaṁ granthō varṇanīyaḥ ।
sa tu tadbha‍ūtādhikaraṇē svayamēva bhāṣyakārēṇa varṇyatē ityuparamyatē ।
﻿<pb n="189"/>
kastarhyanaikāntikaparihāraḥ ? nimittābhiprāyaṁ taducyatē, apratipannanimittaḥ
prathamaśrutānna pratipadyatē । tasmāt śabdādanyannimittāntaramastītyabhiprāyaḥ ।
kaḥ punarvācakanimittayōrbhēdaḥ ? idamarthamēva hi tad‌bhūtādhikaraṇamārabhyatē
ityalamatiprapañcēna । <quote>“na, siddhavadupadēśāt”</quote> iti । kimidam---siddhavadupadē-
śāt---iti ? idamidam---nātra kartā śakyatē kalpayitum, vr̥ddhavyavahāra-
﻿<pb n="190"/>
syānāditvāt; ata autpattikaḥ sambandha iti siddham ।</p>
﻿<pb n="192"/>
<p>kimidamanyathaiva prakrāntamanyathaivōpasaṁhr̥tam---śabdādēvārthāvagatiḥ
iti prakrāntam; vr̥ddhavyavahārāt---ityupasaṁhr̥tam; tadidamanyatrāhita-
manyatraiva nipatitamakuśalasyēva dhanvinaḥ śaranikurumbam । vr̥ddhavyavahārādapya-
rthē'vagamyamānē naiva śabdādarthō'vagatō bhavati hastasaṁjñādibhya iva ।
hastasaṁjñādayō'pi vr̥ddhavyavahāraprasiddhā ēva, nārthēna sambaddhā iti;
vyutpattirēva hyarthāvabōdhakāraṇam, na hastasaṁjñādayaḥ; vyutpattyupādhayō hi tē ।
tasmādupādhiḥ śabdaḥ, nārthāvagatēḥ kāraṇaṁ kaśāṅkuśapratōdābhighātavat ।
﻿<pb n="193"/>
ata ēva ca śabdasvabhāvajñairuktam---vivarta ēva vēdavādibhi-
rāśrayaṇīyaḥ---iti । atrābhidhīyatē---kimanēna vivartapakṣapātēna ?
pratyuktō'yamēkatvānupalabdhēḥ । yadyēvaṁ pratyuktaṁ tarhi vēdasya prāmāṇyam ।
atrōcyatē---vr̥ddhavyavahāravyutpattyāvagamyamānē'rthē śabdādanyat kāraṇaṁ kiṁ
vā manyatē bhavān ? nanu vyutpattimēva kāraṇatayā manyāmahē ।
maivam; śabdārthasambandhaviṣayā hi vyutpattiḥ; na vyutpattēḥ śabdārthā-
vagatiḥ; vyutpattirēva hyādimatī; na punaḥ śabdārthayōḥ sambandhaḥ,
tasya viṣayatvāt । tasmāt <quote>“na; siddhavadupadēśāt”</quote>---iti
samyagabhihitam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="194"/>
<p>nanu ca kāryē'pi sambandhē vr̥ddhavyavahāravyutpattirbālānāmanuguṇaiva;
kathamiyaṁ pratipakṣatayōpanyasyatē ? satyam; pramāṇāntaraparijñēyē hi
﻿<pb n="195"/>
kāryē vyutpattiḥ vyākaraṇādivyutpattiriva, na virōdha; kalpyē
punarniruṇaddhi kalpanām; na cātra pramāṇāntaramastītyuktam । kiṁ ca,
kāryē hi sambandhē na karturdurgamēṣu dēśēṣu sambandhakaraṇēna kiñcana
﻿<pb n="196"/>
prayōjanamasti; saṁvyavahārārthaṁ hi sambandhakaraṇam; na ca durgamasthaiḥ
saṁvyavahārōpapattiḥ । kiṁ ca, kāryaśca sambandhaḥ sambandhiśabdādr̥tē nōpapadyatē;
yadi kāryārthaḥ sambandhō'bhyupagamyatē, kr̥taṁ kāryēṇa । nanu vyutpattirapi
﻿<pb n="197"/>
kāryatāmapēkṣata ēva । katham ? ayamasya vācakaḥ---ityēvamavijñātārthasya na
śabdādavagatirupapadyatē । na hi dr̥ṣṭē'nupapannaṁ nāma; vyavahāramātrādēva hi
bālānāmavagatirdr̥ṣṭā । tasmātpratyakṣadr̥ṣṭē ēvamupapadyamānē'rthē na kartuḥ
kalpanōpapadyatē ।</p>
<p>idamaparaṁ vyavahārānaupayikam, kr̥takē hi sambandhē yadutādr̥śya-
mānasyārthasya dēvatādēḥ sambandhakaraṇam; aśaktistūpavarṇataiva । tasmā-
﻿<pb n="198"/>
dautpattikatvāt sambandhasya siddhamanapēkṣatvam ।</p>
<p><quote>“atha yaduktam---animittaṁ śabdaḥ”</quote> iti kimidaṁ
cōdyatē ? parihr̥tamētat autpattikatvābhidhānēna sambandhasya । kasya
﻿<pb n="199"/>
vānyasya parihārō'vagamyatē autpattikatvābhidhānēna ? naivānya-
dupanyastam । vidyamānōpalambhanatayaiva hi viṣayāntarābhāvō niyōgasya
darśitaḥ <quote>“citrayā yajēta paśukāmaḥ”</quote> ityādau । satyam,
tasyaivāyamautpattikatvaparihāra uktaḥ; kintvautpattikē'pi sambandhē
viṣayāntaravivēkō'nukta iva pratibhāti; tadvivēkāyēdaṁ punarupanyasyatē ।
<quote>“karmakālē phalādarśanāt kālāntarē ca karmābhāvāt”</quote> । nanu cānēna
﻿<pb n="200"/>
kim ? viṣayāntarābhāvāt pramāṇāntaraviṣayatayā ca sāpēkṣatvāt
tadabhāvē cāprāmāṇyaṁ darśitam; ihāpi tadēva; kiṁ punastat
yadanuktamiva pratibhāti ? idaṁ tat; pramāṇāntaraviṣayatvē hi---anēna
idam---ityasmin sati niyōgaḥ । tatra cānupalabdhē sphuṭamēvā-
prāmāṇyam । na cāsminnarthē saṁbhavati niyōgādēva niyōgasiddhiriti
śakyatē kalpayitum । tadidānīṁ nirākriyatē---syādētadēvam, yadyautpa-
ttikatā na syāt; sādhitā cāsau । tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tataḥ---
<pb n="201"/>
na <quote>‘anēnēdam’</quote> ityamumarthamapēkṣatē niyōgaḥ; pramāṇāntarasamadhigamyē'pi hi
laukikē'rthē naiva niyōgasya sādhyasādhanasiddha‍yapēkṣāvasīyatē । kāraṇadōṣa-
﻿<pb n="202"/>
saṁbhāvanānirākaraṇāya nirākriyatē; na punarātmasaṁvittau । tasmāt <quote>‘svātantryaṁ
niyōgasya’</quote> ityanēna vivēkaḥ pradarśyatē । puruṣaṁ hi niyuñjānaḥ sādhya-
siddhimavagamayatīti ṣaṣṭhē pratipādayiṣyati । kimēvaṁ satyanantarānupalabdhi-
rnirastā bhavati ? bāḍhaṁ nirastā; na hyētasmin pakṣē kriyāśaktinirūpaṇāt
sādhyasiddhiḥ । kiṁ tarhi ? niyōgārthavaśāt । tataśca <quote>‘asmādasya siddhiḥ’</quote>
﻿<pb n="203"/>
ityētāvadavagamyatē, na <quote>‘anantaraṁ vyavahitaṁ vā’</quote> iti । taccānapēkṣatvaṁ
yatrataḥ pratipāditam । kimidam <quote>“yadi pañcaiva pramāṇānyabhaviṣyan”</quote>
iti ? idamēvēdam । nanu uktam <quote>“abhāvō'pi pramāṇābhāvaḥ”</quote> iti ।
kimatō yadyēvam ? ētadatō bhavati---pañca pramāṇānīti nōpapadyatē । śakyatē
vā caturbhirnāstīti vak‍tum ? pramāṇaṁ tarhyabhāvaḥ । pramāṇaṁ vā
pramāṇābhāvaḥ---iti śakyatē vaktum ? abhāvasya prāmāṇyē pratyakṣādi-
﻿<pb n="204"/>
viṣayāpēkṣitā viṣayē । ataḥ pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayāvacchēdakatayaivāsya
lakṣaṇābhidhānam । vyavahārānyatvaṁ tu saṁpratipannamēva । vyavahārasiddha‍yartha-
ścāyamupanyāsaḥ, na pramāṇasvarūpasiddha‍yarthaḥ । pramāṇāntarābhyupagamē kō
dōṣaḥ ? na khalu kaściddōṣaḥ; kiṁ tvapramāṇaṁ pramāṇamityuktaṁ bhavati;
﻿<pb n="205"/>
lakṣaṇagranthaścānādr̥tō bhavati; anapēkṣatvaṁ ca sarvapramāṇānāṁ nirastaṁ
bhavati । tasmāt siddhaṁ viṣayāntaraṁ śabdasya । tatsiddhau ca prāmāṇyasiddhiḥ ।
kimarthaṁ tarhi pañcagrahaṇam ? vyavahārapañcakapradarśanārtham । pañcagrahaṇē hyakriya-
māṇē vyavahārāntaraṁ pradarśitaṁ na syāt । ata ēva <quote>‘aphalavatī śākhā’</quote>
iti pratyakṣajamēva vyavahāraṁ manyantē । pramāṇaviṣayāvacchēdajaścāyaṁ vyavahāraḥ ।
﻿<pb n="206"/>
na ca pramāṇaviṣayāvacchēdō viṣayāntaratayā śakyatē vak‍tum । na
ca viṣayamātrāvagamāt pūrvapramāṇānāmavacchēdādr̥tē <quote>‘nāsti’</quote> iti
vyavahārō'vakalpatē । tasmāt siddhaṁ vyavahārānyatvam । ata ēva vyavahāra-
﻿<pb n="207"/>
kāla ēva pañcasaṁkhyōpanyāsaḥ; na pramāṇasvarūpābhidhānakālē ṣaṭsaṁkhyōpa-
nyāsaḥ । tasmādatraiva pañcasaṅkhyōpanyāsādavaitu bhavān---abhāvavyava-
hārasya bhēdikēyaṁ pañcasaṅkhyā, na svarūpasya । prasiddhistu dattōttarā ।।</p>
<p><quote>“yattu pratyakṣaviruddhaṁ vacanamupanyastam---<quote>“sa ēṣa yajñāyudhī
yajamānō'ñjasā svargaṁ lōkaṁ yati”</quote>---iti pratyakṣaṁ śarīrakaṁ vyapadiśati
iti,”</quote> atrāpi śarīrakamityasiddham । kastarhi vyapadiśyatē ? yasyaitaccha-
rīram । nanu <quote>“ēṣaḥ”</quote> iti vyapadēśaḥ, na <quote>‘yasyaiṣaḥ’</quote> iti । abhēdōpacāra-
﻿<pb n="208"/>
nibandhanō'yaṁ vyapadēśaḥ---mañcāḥ krōśanti itivat । kimityaupacārikaḥ
śabdārthō gr̥hyatē ? tathāvagatēḥ; uktā hyarthavādapadānāmanyaparatvāt gauṇyēvā-
vagatiḥ । nanu cānyatvōpalabdhau satyāṁ gōrvāhīkasya ca gauṇō nirdēśa
upapadyatē <quote>‘gaurvāhīkaḥ’</quote> iti; na cātra śarīrādanyamupalabhāmahē ।
nōpalabhāmahē---iti kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? ayamēvābhiprāyaḥ---nōpalabhāmahē
iti । nanu kāryabhūtaiḥ prāṇādibhirupalabhāmahē । nanu śarīramēva prāṇityapāniti
﻿<pb n="209"/>
ca” iti । śarīraṁ nāma kimabhiprētamāyuṣmataḥ ? yō'yaṁ cāturbhautikaḥ
saṅghātaḥ । na rhi śarīrakāryāṇyētāni, ayāvaccharīrabhāvitvāt । ayāva-
﻿<pb n="211"/>
dbha‍ūtabhāvitvādityarthaḥ । satyapi bhūtatvē'nupāttānāṁ na rūpādaya ivōpalabhyantē ।
kiñca, sukhādayaśca na bhūtadharmāḥ śakyantē vak‍tum; parēndriyagrāhyā hi
bhūtadharmā rūpādayō bhūtavadēva, na sukhādayaḥ । mā bhūvan bhūtadharmāḥ sukhādayaḥ;
tadva‍yatiriktasyānyasyēti kimatra pramāṇam ? nanu ca kāryamētat kārāṇādr̥tē
nōpapadyatē---itīdamēvātra pramāṇam । nirastā ca bhūtānāṁ samavāyi-
﻿<pb n="212"/>
kāraṇatēti siddhamanyadharmatvam । naivaṁ sidhyati, parasparakāryatayā-
pyupapattēḥ । <quote>“na hi yō ya upalabhyatē tasya tasya sambandhinā
bhavitavyamiti śakyatē vak‍tum”</quote> iti yaduktam, tadayuktamiva pratibhāti;
yadutpattimad‌dr̥ṣṭam, tat kathaṁ sambandhyantaraṁ nāvagamayati ? hētumatī hyutpatti-
riti sthitam । visabhāgahētvabhiprāyamētat; na punarutpattirahētukai-
vōktā । kathaṁ punaridamavagamyatē---visabhāgahētvabhiprāyamētaditi ? <quote>“na hi
﻿<pb n="213"/>
candramasamādityaṁ vā”</quote> ityatra <quote>“sambandhyantaram”</quote> iti antara-
śabdaśravaṇāt । nanvanyatvē'pyantaraśabda upapadyata ēva । satyamupapa-
dyatē, na tu---kāryamakāraṇam---iti śakyatē'vagantum । bhavatu
﻿<pb n="214"/>
duṣṭatā granthasya; na punardōṣa ēvārthāntarāvagamē hētuḥ । na, santānā-
bhyupagamāt; santatirhi hētuhētumadbhāvanibandhanā । tasmāt visabhāga-
﻿<pb n="215"/>
hētvabhiprāyamētadityavēhi । ataḥ sabhāgasantatihētukamēvēdaṁ kāryajālam;
nātra visadr̥śōpalabdhō pramāṇamasti---ityupasaṁhr̥tam । yadi ca
visabhāgādr̥tē nōtpattiḥ syāt, avyavasthaiva syāt । anayaiva yuktyā
kartr̥śabdārthē icchā smr̥tiśca pratyuktā, anyasyādarśanāditi; na
hyadr̥ṣṭē'nyasmin visabhāgē smr̥tyādayō nōpapadyanta iti śakyatē vak‍tum;
﻿<pb n="216"/>
na hi dr̥ṣṭē'nupapannaṁ nāma । tadidamuktam---<quote>“anupapannamiti naḥ kva
saṁpratyayaḥ ?”</quote> iti । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ sarva ēvāmī ātmapratītihētava
upanyasya nirasyantē bhāṣyakārēṇa ? ēbhiranātmanyātmabuddhiḥ prāpnōti;
sarvaprakāraṁ cājñānaṁ nirasanīyam । kathaṁ punaramī hētavō'nātmanyātmabuddhi-
﻿<pb n="217"/>
mutpādayanti ? yattāvadidamuktam---<quote>“prāṇādibhirēnamupalabhāmahē”</quote>---iti,
kimatrāyuktam ? bhūtaguṇā hyamī na bhavanti, ayāvadbha‍ūtabhāvitvāt
ghaṭādiṣvadarśanāt iti nirastē ca bhūtadharmatvē āśrayitvāccānya-
sambandhitāyāmavagatāyāṁ cittacētyānāṁ svayamāśritatvāt ātmaguṇā
hyētē iti yuktamēvōktam । kathamanēnānātmanyātmabuddhiḥ śakyatē
vak‍tum ? tat sukhādayō'pyāśritatayōpalabhyamānā ayāvadbha‍ūtabhāvitayā
﻿<pb n="218"/>
ca samyagātmaguṇatayōktāḥ । atrōcyatē---prāṇādayastāvadayāvadbha‍ūtabhāvi-
tayā naivaṁ śakyantē vak‍tum । calanātmakā hyamī; vāyōścāyaṁ dharmaḥ;
sarvatra hi śvasanādiṣu calanātmakataivōpalabhyatē । tasmādayāvadbha‍ūtabhāvitva-
masiddham । sēyamanātmanyātmabuddhiḥ । yē'pi sukhādaya upanyastāḥ, tē'pi
bhūtavikārahētutvāt bhūtaguṇā ēvēti śakyantē vak‍tum; na hyaguṇō guṇinaṁ
vikartumutsahatē । avasthā hi vikāraḥ; avasthā cāvasthāvatō'vasthāntarō-
﻿<pb n="219"/>
tpattau hētuḥ; na cāvasthāvasthāvatō'nyēti siddhaṁ bhūtaguṇatvam । nanu caiva-
mēva vaktavyam । kimityuktam---kāmaṁ sukhādaya ēvaṁ syuḥ---iti ?
abhyupagamyāyamarthō na sidhyatītyabhiprāyaḥ, kāmābhidhānāt । kiṁ punara-
bhyupagamē kāraṇam ? idamasti kāraṇam---atra kēcit prajñābhimāninō
﻿<pb n="220"/>
vipratipannāḥ---kēyamāśrayāśrayitā nāma ? saṅghātamātramēvēdamupalabhyatē, na
hyēkatrōpalabdhyāśrayāśrayitā bhavati bhūtānāmiva parasparam । tasmāt tē'pi
sukhādayaḥ svatantrā vā āśrayiṇō vā---ityabhyupagamāt pradarśitam ।</p>
<p>atrāparē brahmavidaḥ---kartrabhidhānāt smr̥tēricchātaśca mahadādibhūta-
paryantāt śarīrāt atiriktamātmānamupalabhāmahē---iti pratipannāḥ । kathaṁ
﻿<pb n="221"/>
punarabhidhānādērhētutōktā taiḥ ? jñānātmakaṁ hyantaḥkaraṇaṁ mahadādi, jñēyaṁ ca
kāryam; ataḥ kāryakaraṇavyatiriktō <quote>‘jānāti’</quote> iti śakyatē vak‍tum ; 
jñānēna kimapi bhavayēditi hi pratyayaḥ । tasmāt siddha ātmā kartr̥bhūtaḥ ।
nanvasau niṣkriya ityuktam ; pratyayasya hi kartari <quote>‘jānāti’</quote>
﻿<pb n="222"/>
ityayaṁ pratyayaḥ । yēṣāṁ tāvadātmani jñānaṁ samavaiti, tēṣāṁ tatkāraṇatvāt
pratyayakartr̥tāpi siddhaiva । yēṣāṁ punaḥ buddhidharmatayaiva prasiddhā jñānādayaḥ,
tēṣāmapi bhōk‍tr̥tayāyaṁ hētuḥ । kathamicchāta upalabdhiruktā ? ēvamuktā---
bhuktapūrvaviṣayō hyabhilāṣa icchā ; na ca kṣaṇikēṣu skandhēṣu bhuktapūrvatābhimāna
upapadyatē । nanu na hi dr̥ṣṭē'nupapannaṁ nāma । dr̥ṣṭē hyanupapattirnāsti, na punaḥ
﻿<pb n="223"/>
dr̥ṣṭasyānyathābhāvō dr̥ṣṭatvānnānupapanna iti śakyatē vak‍tum ; dr̥ṣṭasyāya-
manyathābhāvaḥ । tasmādicchayā kāryakaraṇādanyamupalabhāmahē ityuktam ।
tathā smr̥tēḥ; smr̥tirapyanubhūtaviṣayaiva । na ca kṣaṇikē'rthē'yamanubhūtānubhava
upapadyatē ; na hi dr̥ṣṭē'nupapannaṁ nāma---iti । kathaṁ tarhi bhāṣya-
kārēṇa <quote>“anupapannamiti naḥ kva saṁpratyayaḥ”</quote> ityuktam ? śrūyatāṁ
yathōktam । kimanubhavasyānupapannatvam ? anubhava ēva yasyānubhūyatē,
﻿<pb n="224"/>
kā tasyānubhūyamānāpēkṣā ? tasmāt sūṣṭhūcyatē <quote>“anupapannamiti naḥ kva
saṁpratyayaḥ”</quote> iti । tasmācchūnyāḥ skandhā ityupasaṁhr̥tam । tathā ca
brāhmaṇamapyamumēvārthamanuvadati <quote>“vijñānaghana ēvaitēbhyō bhūtēbhyaḥ samutthāya
tānyēvānuvinaśyati; na prētya saṁjñāsti”</quote> iti । tasmādanātmanyātma-
buddhihētavō'mī nirākaraṇīyatayōpanyastā bhagavatā bhāṣyakārēṇa ।
﻿<pb n="225"/>
<quote>“atrōcyatē---naitadēvam; anyēdyurdr̥ṣṭē'parēdyuḥ <quote>‘ahamidamadarśam’</quote> iti
bhavati pratyayaḥ ; pratyagātmani caitadbhavati, na paratra ; parō hyasau,
yō'nyēdyurdr̥ṣṭavān । tasmāttadva‍yatiriktō'nyō'sti, yatrāyamahaṁśabdaḥ”</quote> ।
kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇamatrānumānanirākaraṇē ? asambhavāditi brūmaḥ । <quote>‘pratyakṣa-
dr̥ṣṭē'rthē'numānaṁ na saṁbhavati’</quote> iti sāhasamidam । svayamēva ca vakṣyati
<quote>“nūnamasāvanityānnityaṁ paśyati”</quote> iti । tasmānnātrāsambhavābhiprāyō
varṇayituṁ śakyatē । athaitanmanasi viparivartatē <quote>‘parōktamanumānaṁ na saṁbhavati’</quote>
﻿<pb n="226"/>
iti । pratyakṣōpanyāsastarhi kimarthaḥ ? na hyasati pratyakṣē'numānamupapadyatē
iti cēt, kimidam <quote>‘asati pratyakṣē’</quote> iti ? asti cānumānaṁ
pratyakṣavyāpāranirapēkṣam । na brūmaḥ <quote>‘anumānaṁ sarvatra pratyakṣavyāpāranirapēkṣamēva
nāsti’</quote> iti । kiṁ tarhi ? <quote>‘svayamātmānaṁ pratyakṣēṇānupalabhya nēdamanumānaṁ
pravartatē’</quote> iti । upalabdhaścēt svayam, kimanumānēna ? svaparijñānaśuddhirhi
﻿<pb n="227"/>
śrēyasē; tadarthaścāyamārambhaḥ । athāyamupadēśaḥ parārtha ēva pravr̥ttaḥ,
ātmasaṁvida idānīṁ ka upayōgaḥ ? atha parasyāpi pratipattau
pratyakṣamēva pramāṇam---iti matam, anumānōpanyāsō'narthakaḥ ।
yadapyucyatē---<quote>“yatrāyaṁ ahaṁśabdaḥ”</quote> iti, punaścāpahnūyatē---<quote>“na vayaṁ
<quote>‘aham’</quote> itīmaṁ śabdaṁ prayujyamānamasminnarthē hētutvēna vyapadiśāmaḥ”</quote> iti,
tadapyabuddhimata ivābhidhānamiti pratibhāvati; kimapahnavanīyasyāhaṁśabdasyō-
panyāsē prayōjanam ? idamaparamayuktam---<quote>“yadi vijñānādanyadasti
﻿<pb n="228"/>
vijñātr̥ vijñānapamāsya tannidarśyatām <quote>‘idaṁ tadīdr̥śaṁ ca’</quote> iti”</quote> iti ।
pr̥ṣṭē <quote>“atrōcyatē”</quote>---ityēvamādyuttaraṁ nōpapadyatē; atra vijñānāgrahaṇē
tadgrahaṇaṁ nāsti---iti cōditam; svasaṁvēdyatayā kathamasya nirākaraṇam ?
na hi svasaṁvēdyatvanibandhanaṁ vijñānagrahaṇapūrvakaṁ grahaṇaṁ vastunaḥ ।
athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---svasaṁvinnō na pr̥thaktayā vyapadēṣṭuṁ śakyatē parasmai
---iti, atyalpamidamucyatē ; apr̥thaktayā vā kathaṁ parēṇāsaṁvi-
nnō'rthō vyapadēṣṭuṁ śakyatē parasmai? tasmādidamapyanālōcanapūrvamiva
pratibhāti । pratyuktasya cōpanyāsē kiṁ prayōjanamiti naiva jñāyatē ।
﻿<pb n="229"/>
na cāyamarthaḥ parityakta ēva, vijñānagrahaṇōpasaṁhārāt । athāyamabhi-
prāyaḥ---vijñānagrahaṇapakṣē'pyātmanaḥ pratyakṣatvaṁ na śakyatē'pahnōtum
iti, <quote>“rūpāntaraṁ nōpalabhāmahē”</quote> ityanirākr̥taivēyaṁ yuktiḥ । na ca
kaścidviśēṣō'bhihitaḥ । upamānamapi naiyāyikōktamabhidadhatā svala-
﻿<pb n="230"/>
kṣaṇābhidhānaviruddhamuktam । na ca <quote>‘ahaṁ gacchāmi’</quote> iti cōdya-
syāpi spaṣṭaṁ kiñciduttaramupalabhyatē । brahmavidviruddhaṁ tvētat yadutāhaṁ-
pratyayamēyatātmanaḥ । mūrdhābhiṣiktamidamanātmanyātmajñānam ityudā-
hr̥tam---yadutāhaṁkr̥tirmamakāraśca---iti । nirmuktāhaṁkāramamakāramātma-
jñānamityātmavidō manyantē । tasmādanātmajñānavilasitamidam---ahaṁpratyaya-
﻿<pb n="231"/>
pramēya ātmā---iti । atrōcyatē---<quote>“anyēdyurdr̥ṣṭē'parēdyuḥ <quote>‘ahamidamadarśam’</quote>
iti bhavati pratyayaḥ ; pratyagātmani caitadbhavati, na paratra”</quote> kimidam
<quote>‘ahamidamadarśam’</quote> iti ? yadi tāvat pratyabhijñā, kṣaṇikatvasyaiva taduttaram,
na nairātmyasya । na cātra kṣaṇikatvanirākaraṇamabhiprētam । kiṁ tarhi ?
buddhīndriyaśarīravyatiriktasyātmanaḥ sadbhāvapratipattiḥ । na ca kṣaṇikatayā
nairātmyamuktaṁ paraiḥ । kiṁ tarhi ? skandhātiriktānupalabdhēḥ ; nityatāyā
hi kṣaṇikatvaṁ virōdhi, nātmasadbhāvasya । tasya cātra sadbhāvaḥ parairākṣiptaḥ
pratipādyatē, na punarātmanō vidyamānasya nityatāyā ākṣēpaṁ prati
﻿<pb n="232"/>
samādhiḥ । na ca---anya upalabdhā hyaḥ, adya cānyaḥ---ityētāvatā
nairātmyam । tasmāt <quote>‘ahaṁpratyayagrāhyaḥ kāryakaraṇavyatiriktō'sti’</quote>
ityētāvadvaktavyam, <quote>‘hyō'dya’</quote> cētyatiricyatē । athēyaṁ buddhiḥ---sādhitē'-
pyastitvē kṣaṇikatvādātmataiva hīyata---iti, kayaṁ muktiḥ ?
skandhānāṁ skandhatā kimiti na hīyatē ? bhōk‍tr̥tvaṁ hyātmanaḥ svarūpam,
﻿<pb n="233"/>
bhōgyatā ca skandhānām ; yathā ca kṣaṇikatvē'pi bhōgyatā nāpanētuṁ
śakyatē skandhānām, tathā bhōk‍tr̥tvamapyātmanaḥ । tadidaṁ kṣapāprayāṇakam ।
anātmajñō bhavān, yasyaivaṁvidhāni cōdyāni । vētsi kimiti kṣaṇikatā
skandhānāmuktēti ? kimiti vōktā ? bhōk‍turabhāvāt । bhōk‍turabhāvē
kṣaṇikatā skandhānām---iti kimiyaṁ rājājñā ? nēyaṁ rājājñā ; nayājñā
hyēṣā । katham ? bhōk‍tr̥sadbhāvē kāryakaraṇaṁ kṣaṇikam---iti nāsti naḥ
﻿<pb n="234"/>
pramāṇam । kasmāt ? anumēyaṁ hi kāraṇaṁ kāryataḥ ; ataśca kriyāsiddhiḥ ।
kriyāpalāpanibandhanō'yaṁ kṣaṇikatvavādaḥ । luptakriyasya ca kartr̥tva-
bhōk‍tr̥tvākṣēpaḥ । tadākṣēpē cātmākṣēpaḥ । pariṇatisvabhāvamātramidaṁ
﻿<pb n="235"/>
kāryakāraṇamiti, kalpanēyaṁ kartā bhōktā iti ca । tasmādahaṁpratyayāla-
mbanamātrasiddhau siddhē'pi buddhīndriyaśarīravyatirēkiṇi kartr̥tvabhōk‍tr̥tvē
na staḥ ; tadātmakatā cātmana ātmatā । tasmāt avināśitāpurassaraiva
bhōk‍tr̥tā---iti manvānaḥ sapratyabhijñaṁ pratyakṣamupanyastavān bhāṣyakāraḥ ।
ata ēva ca nairātmyavādinō muhurmuhuḥ kṣaṇikatāmakiñcitkaratāṁ
cāpādayantyātmanaḥ---<quote>“carmōpamaścētsō'nityaḥ khatulyaścēdasatsamaḥ”</quote> iti ।
tasmādbhōk‍tr̥taivātmēti । yuktam---bhōk‍tr̥taivātmā iti ; kartr̥tvōpanyāsastu
virudhyatē, niṣkriyatvādātmanaḥ ; sarvagatatvācca niṣkriyatvam ; pratipannaṁ
ca sarvagatatvam, sarvatra sukhōpalambhāt । na hyasatyāgamanē kiṁcidvirudhyatē ।
﻿<pb n="236"/>
calanātmikāṁ kriyāmaṅgīkr̥tya niṣkriyatōktā, na punarbhōgō-
tpattāvapi । tasmāt suṣṭhūcyatē---kartr̥bhōk‍tr̥taivātmā iti ।
tasmādupapannō'yaṁ granthaḥ <quote>“ahamidamadarśam”</quote> iti । viṣayapratyabhijñā
caitannibandhanā---iti śabdādhikaraṇē upanyasyatē । <quote>“pratyagātmani
﻿<pb n="237"/>
caitadbhavati”</quote>---iti kasyārthasya siddhayē ? bhōk‍tr̥tvasyaiva । katham ?
pratyagātmani bhōgadarśanāt । yadi parō'pyahaṁpratyayasya viṣayatāmāpadyēta,
tadā bhōk‍tr̥tvahānaṁ prāpnōti ; bhōk‍tr̥tā cātmētyuktam । <quote>“na paratra, parō
hyasau, yō'nyēdyurdr̥ṣṭavān”</quote> iti pratyabhijñānupapattiḥ । <quote>“yatrāyamahaṁśabdaḥ”</quote>
iti ahaṁśabdōpanyāsastarhi kimarthaḥ ? parāpahnavāya ? nāpahnavāya;
parapratipattayē । kimiti tarhyapahnavaḥ ? sākṣāddhētutvaśaṅkānirākaraṇāya ।
sākṣāddhētutvaṁ manvānēna <quote>‘anātmanyapyahaṁśabdō'sti’</quote> iti pradarśitam---
﻿<pb n="238"/>
<quote>“paratrāpyahaṁśabdō bhaktyā dr̥śyatē”</quote> ityēvamādinā । <quote>“na vayam”</quote>
iti na sākṣāddhētutayēdamupanyastam iti prakaṭitam । hētvarthapradarśanārthastu
śabdaprayōgaḥ । nanu ca <quote>“ahaṁ gacchāmi”</quote> iti na hētvartha-
pradarśanamātratayā śakyatē parihartum ; atra hi ahaṁpratyayō'pi
vyabhicāryēvōpalabhyatē, acalātmakatvādātmanaḥ । tasmāt skandhā
ēvālambanatāmāpadyantē ityāśaṅkanīyamidam ; kimiti nirāśaṅkairēva
gamyatē ? kimatrāśaṅkanīyam ? idaṁpratyayagrāhyaṁ hi kāryakaraṇam ;
pratyayāntaragrāhyē ca vastuni viruddhapratyayāntarālambanatā nōpapadyatē
<quote>‘gaurvāhīkaḥ’</quote> iti yathā । gauṇa upapadyatē iti cēt
﻿<pb n="239"/>
parihr̥tamētattvayaiva । tasmādasaṁbhinnēdaṁpratyaya ēva ahaṁpratyaya ātmana
ālambanam । brāhmaṇamapyamumēvārthamanuvadati---<quote>“aśīryō na hi śīryatē”</quote>
ityaśīryatayā bhōk‍tr̥tvamātmanaḥ । <quote>“vinaśvaraṁ ca vijñānam”</quote> iti
tadva‍yatiriktālambanatāmāpādayati । tasmāt vyāmōhō'yamahaṁkāragranthiriti
na śakyatē vak‍tum, <quote>“yasya ca duṣṭaṁ karaṇam, yatra ca mithyēti
pratyayaḥ, sa ēvāsamīcīnaḥ pratyayaḥ ; nānyaḥ”</quote>---iti siddhatvādasyārthasya ।
yadi paraṁ brahmavidāmēṣa niścayaḥ---yadupalabhyatē, tadasat ; yannōpalabhyatē,
tattattvam---iti, namastēbhyaḥ ; viduṣi nōttaraṁ vācyam---ityatra parihāraḥ ।
tasmādyathārthō'yamarthavādaḥ---<quote>“sa ēṣa yajñāyudhī yajamānaḥ”</quote> iti ।</p>
﻿<pb n="240"/>
<p><quote>“āha---yadi vijñānādanyadasti vijñātr̥ vijñānamapāsya,
tannidarśyatām <quote>‘idaṁ tadīdr̥śa ca’</quote> iti”</quote> iti kimidaṁ cōdyatē ? idamēva
cōdyatē । tadēva na jñāyatē । kathaṁ na jñāyatē ? itthaṁ na jñāyatē---
kiṁ vā savijñānasyātmanō'haṁpratyayaḥ pramāṇatayōpanyastaḥ, yēnēdamucyatē---
vijñānamapāsya tannidarśayitavyam iti ? anēkavastvālambanaṁ hi
yatra jñānam, tatrēdaṁ yujyatē vak‍tum---idamapāsyēdaṁ nidarśaya iti ; iha
tvēkātmarūpaiva saṁvit । tasmāt idaṁ vyudasanīyam iti tamasi padam ।
atrōcyatē---ayamasyābhiprāyaḥ ; jñēyatvē hyātmanō jñānajñātr̥ṇī vyati-
riktē na śakyētē vak‍tum ; na cāpāsyaiva tē saṁvidastīti siddham ।
﻿<pb n="241"/>
tasmāt jñānajñātr̥ṇī vyudasya pr̥thak pramēyatayā nidarśyatām ।
<quote>“atrōcyatē---svasaṁvēdyaḥ sa bhavati; nāsāvanyēna śakyatē draṣṭum”</quote> iti ।
kimidamasyōttaramupapadyatē ? kimiti nōpapadyatē ? ēvaṁ nōpapadyatē
---saivēyaṁ pūrvōktaikālambanānēkākāratā pratyayasyābhyupagatā bhavati ।
avivēkāparādhō'yam, nātrāyuṣmatō dōṣaḥ । nanu ca ahaṁpratyayō'yam
﻿<pb n="242"/>
<quote>“ahamidamadarśam”</quote> ityupanyastaḥ, na <quote>‘ahamadarśam’</quote> iti । ēvaṁ ca sati
kēyamanēkākāratā ? <quote>“avivēkaḥ paramāpadāṁ padam”</quote> । yadi hyātma-
śabdavācyatayā jñēyatōpanyastā syāt, pramēyāntaraśūnyatā vā, tadaitaccōdya-
﻿<pb n="243"/>
mabhaviṣyat; iha tu sarvajñēyapramātr̥tayaiva saṁvidupanyastā; tasmāt prati-
pakṣōpanyāsa ēvāyaṁ kathaṁ tēnaiva bādhyatē ? na hi yadyasya bādhyam,
tattasyaiva bādhakaṁ bhavitumarhati । tasmāt samyaguttaram । <quote>“yathā kaści-
ccakṣuṣmān”</quote> ityanēnāpi nidarśanēna kartr̥karaṇāntaraniṣēdha ēva sthirīkr̥taḥ ।
nanu cātra kartrantaraṁ karaṇāntaraṁ bhinnaṁ mēyāt; tat kimidaṁ
nidarśanam ? kartrantarābhāvasāmānyāt । tasmāt kāraṇadōṣarahitā aviparītā
﻿<pb n="244"/>
ca saṁvit ātmāstitvē hētuḥ । bhavatu vā kartrantaraṁ mā vā ।
uktaṁ ca---yathā avagamyantē'rthāḥ, tathā bhavanti; yathā nāva-
gamyantē'rthāḥ, tathā na bhavanti iti । atrāpi brāhmaṇaṁ bhavati
<quote>“śāntāyāṁ vāci”</quote> । ātmani vyāpr̥tē'nyatra kartr̥tayā kathaṁ kartr̥-
karaṇāntarābhāvō gr̥hyatē---iti praśnaḥ । vāggrahaṇaṁ ca karaṇāntarā-
bhāvanidarśanārtham । <quote>“ātmajyōtiḥ samrāḍiti hōvāca”</quote> ityayamarthaḥ
pūrvōttarapakṣabhaṅgyā pradarśitaḥ । ēvaṁ ca <quote>“agr̥hyō na hi gr̥hyatē”</quote> iti
﻿<pb n="245"/>
brāhmaṇamupapannam । nanu cātrāgrāhyataivōpanyastā । nanu na śrutaṁ
bhavatā <quote>“ātmajyōtiḥ samrāṭ”</quote> iti ? idamapi kiṁ na śrutam ?
dvayōḥ śrutyōstadanurōdhēnāsyāgrahaṇaśrutirāpēkṣikī, na punarātmagrahaṇamanyathā
vyākhyāyatē---iti kā yuktiḥ ? svayaṁjyōtirgrahaṇē guṇavādasyā-
sambhavāt agrāhyatvē cāpēkṣikatayōpapattēḥ, <quote>‘ātmā jñātavyō mantavyaḥ’</quote>
iti cāvirōdhāt । ēvaṁ ca svayaṁjyōtiṣṭvamupapadyata iti ।</p>
<p>nanu caivaṁ sati kathaṁ parasmai pratipādayituṁ śakyatē ? parapratya-
﻿<pb n="246"/>
yārthaścāyamārambhaḥ śāstrakārāṇāṁ śrutīnāṁ ca । svasaṁvidēvātrābhyupā-
yatāṁ pratipadyatē---ātmanā saṁvadyētē na parēṇēti । sarvapuruṣēṣu ca
parāsaṁvēdyasaṁvidastīti siddhā parasaṁvitpratiṣēdhamukhēnōpadēśānāmupadēśatā ।
tadidam <quote>“nēti nēti”</quote> ityupanyastam । nanu sukhādayō'pi svasaṁvēdyā
ēva; tē'pi parēṇa naiva parasthāḥ saṁvēdyantē । kathaṁ tēbhyō'nyatayā parasmā
upadiṣṭa ātmā bhavati ? tatra bhāṣyakārēṇa <quote>‘liṅgāvagamyatayā parēṇā-
﻿<pb n="247"/>
vagamyanta ēva’</quote> ityuktam; tadayuktam, ātmanō'pi prasaṅgāt ।
tatra cēṣṭānumānaṁ svayamupanyasyati । ataḥ pratipannārthōpaghāti kathaṁ
vidvadbhirlikhyatē ? tadidamanupāsitagurōścōdyam; cēṣṭā hi kāraṇadōṣa-
nirākaraṇatayā upanyastā; sukhādayastu bhrūbhaṅganētravilāsādigamyāḥ । kaḥ
punaranayōrviśēṣaḥ ? anēnāpi parasyaiva saṁvidgamyatē । akāryata iti
﻿<pb n="248"/>
viśēṣaḥ । kathaṁ punarasambaddhamupalakṣayati ? kathaṁ vā anupalakṣitaḥ
puruṣāntarāviparyayaḥ svātmani viparyayāśaṅkāṁ nirasyati ? viparyayāgrahaṇā-
diti brūmaḥ । na cāgrahaṇē sambandhitōpayujyata ityuktam । tasmādupapannamidaṁ
śābaraṁ vacaḥ । mā bhūt ātmanō'numānam, cēṣṭānimittā tu parātma-
pratipattiḥ kimiti parātmānaṁ nānumāpayati ? atra brūmaḥ---uktamēva
﻿<pb n="249"/>
<quote>‘bhōk‍tr̥tayā hyātmatā’</quote> iti । upamāpyatra kathanōpāyatayaivōpanyastā । kathanaṁ
ca pramāṇāntarapūrvakamiti na lakṣaṇavyavahārayōrvirōdhaḥ । <quote>“yadapyucyatē
﻿<pb n="250"/>
---vijñānamapāsya tannidarśyatāmiti”</quote> । nanu ca dattōttaramētat <quote>“svasaṁvēdyaḥ
sa bhavati”</quote> iti; dattōttarasya ca punarupanyāsō nōpapadyatē । athāya-
mabhiprāyaḥ---naiva tat, idamasyōttaram । kasya tarhi taduttaram ? yadi na
kasyaciduttaram, kimētāvatā taduttarēṇa bhavitavyam ? nanu tadanantarā-
﻿<pb n="251"/>
bhidhānāt taduttaramiti gamyatē । punaḥ praśnābhidhānānnōttaramityavēhi ;
kramācca liṅgaṁ balīyaḥ । tadidamākāśabhrāntam; ubhayaṁ tasyaivōttaram ।
<quote>“svasaṁvēdyaḥ sa bhavati”</quote> itīdamapi liṅgādēvōttaramavasīya/?/tē; vyākhyātaṁ
cāsya tadapākaraṇasāmarthyam । punaḥ praśna idānīṁ kimarthaḥ ? asti
kiñcidavalagnam । kiṁ tadavalagnam ? satyam; <quote>‘idamahaṁ vēdmi’</quote> iti
saṁvēdyatē, nākārāntarakalpanā; vijñānaviviktasya tu grahaṇaṁ na
prāpnōti, vyāpr̥tāvagamāt; vijñānāvagamē ca rūpāntarānupalabdhēḥ
﻿<pb n="252"/>
punarapi śūnyatā । tasmāt kalpita ēvāyamahaṅkāragranthiriti
punarupanyāsaḥ । <quote>“yadyupāyamēva pratiṣēdhasi”</quote> iti kimabhiprētamuttaravādinaḥ ?
idamabhiprētam---grāhyānukāritā hi grahaṇasyōktā, na grāhakānukāritā ।
vyāpr̥tāvasthōpāyatayōpanyastā kathamanupāyamupēyaṁ śakyatē kathayitumiti ।
tadidamāha---<quote>“yadyupāyamēva pratiṣēdhasi, na śakyamupāyamantarēṇōpēyamupētum ।
ayamēvābhyupāyō jñātavyānāmarthānām”</quote> iti । <quote>“tadyathā---kaḥ
śuklō nāma ? yatra śuklatvamasti”</quote> ityanēna kiṁ samarthitam ?
﻿<pb n="253"/>
idaṁ samarthitam---yathā na śuklatāmantarēṇa jñēyamavagamyata iti ।
nanu caivaṁ śuklatāpuraḥsaraiva jñēyē buddhiḥ; ēvaṁ cānabhiprētō'rthaḥ
samarthitō bhavati । nānabhiprētaḥ; ētāvadanēnōktam---nōpāyamantarēṇō-
pēyānāmupēyatvam iti; yasya yathaivōpāyatvam, tathaiva tasya; jñānasya
tūpāyatvē'pi na tatpuraḥsarā saṁvit ityuktam । tasmāt sarvavijñāna-
jñēyatātmanaḥ sthitā bhavati <quote>‘ahamidamadarśam’</quote> iti । iyān
﻿<pb n="254"/>
viśēṣaḥ---anumānādiṣvapi pratyakṣatā । viṣayabhēdāddhi pramāṇabhēdaḥ,
na pramātr̥bhēdāt । pramātr̥rūpatā tu jñānasyānāśaṅkanīyaiva, anāśaṅki-
tatvāt । yuktaṁ cēdaṁ nāśaṅkitam, karmapravaṇatvāt karmaṇaḥ
sakarmakasya । yadapi jñātr̥taiva jñānādr̥tē na śakyatē'vagantumiti,
tadadhīnatvāttadavagatēḥ; yaduktam <quote>“na ca rūpāntarōpalabdhiḥ”</quote> iti,
﻿<pb n="255"/>
tadapi pratyuktam <quote>“kāmaṁ vijñānamapahūyēta, nārthaḥ”</quote> iti । tasmāt
siddhamātmatattvamiti ।</p>
<p>yat punarbrāhmaṇam <quote>“na prētya saṁjñāsti”</quote> iti, tat pūrvōttarabhaṅgyā
svayamēva brāhmaṇāntarēṇa vyākhyātam । ēvaṁ cārthavādārthatā upapannaivēti
<quote>‘na caiṣa vidhiśabdaḥ’</quote> ityapi pratyuktam । nanu ca <quote>“sa ēṣaḥ”</quote> ityupapannārtham;
﻿<pb n="256"/>
<quote>“svargaṁ lōkaṁ yāti”</quote> iti katham ? adhikr̥takāmasiddhēḥ siddham । yaduktam
<quote>“ahaṁkāramamakārāvanātmanyātmābhimānau”</quote> iti, mr̥ditakaṣāyāṇā-
mēvaitat kathanīyam; na karmasaṅgināmityuparamyatē । āha ca bhagavān
dvaipāyanaḥ---<quote>“na buddhibhēdaṁ janayēdajñānāṁ karmasaṅginām”</quote> iti rahasyā-
dhikārē । tasmānna vivr̥tamatra bhāṣyakārēṇa bhagavatā, vacanānurōdhāt,
nājñānāt iti ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="257"/>
<p>।। karmaikē tatra darśanāt ।।</p>
<p><quote>“uktam nityaḥ śabdārthayōḥ sambandhaḥ iti; tadanupapa-
nnam”</quote> iti kēyamanupapattiḥ ? iyamēvānupapattiḥ---anityē śabdē nityaḥ
śabdārthayōḥ sambandhō nōpapadyata iti । kathaṁ tarhi samavāyē ? yutasiddha-
﻿<pb n="258"/>
yōranupapattiḥ । śabdatvaṁ ca nirastam । nanu ca gatvādyanyadanirastamasti ।
﻿<pb n="259"/>
na tat, gasya viśēṣānupalabdhēḥ । kathaṁ tarhi śukaśārikāmanuṣyēṣu ?
ata ēva svatō viśēṣō nōpalabhyatē; śukaśārikāmanuṣyā ēva
hi tatra viśēṣatāmāpadyantē । tathā ca laukikāḥ <quote>‘śukō'yaṁ paṭhati’</quote>,
<quote>‘manuṣyō'yaṁ paṭhati’</quote> iti viśēṣānabhidadhati, na punaḥ <quote>‘amuṁ gaviśēṣam,
amuṁ gaviśēṣam’</quote> iti । tasmānna nityatā sidhyati sambandhasya ।
ataḥ śabdasya nityatvaṁ vaktavyam; tadidamākṣēpapūrvakamucyatē <quote>“karmaikē
tatra darśanāt”</quote> iti । nanu caivaṁ sati kr̥takō'pi sambandhō nōpapadyatē ।
﻿<pb n="260"/>
tataḥ kim ? laukikavyavahārōcchēdaḥ । punastataḥ kim ? anityatvapratijñā
nōpapadyatē; laukikavyavahāravirōdhāt balānnityatā prāpnōti ।
laukikavyavahāravirōdhādanityatā mā bhūt; nityatāpattēḥ kimāyātam ?
idamāyātam---laukikavyavahārānupapattirēva । satyamēvam; yadi pratyasta-
mitaṁ samayēna; na hyaviṣayaḥ samayasyāsti; sarvānupapattyārtiharō'yaṁ
﻿<pb n="261"/>
samayaḥ । tasmāt śabdapramāṇakānāṁ na vyavahāradarśanamātrēṇa prāmāṇyaṁ
sidhyati । tasmānnityatvē yatnaḥ kartavyō'bhidhānasya । sa cāya-
mārabdhaḥ, vr̥ddhavyavahārapūrvakatvāt sambandhajñānasya sambandhajñāna-
pūrvakatvāccārthāvagatēḥ । na ca kṣaṇikatvē'pi cakṣurādīnāmiva prāmāṇya-
siddhiḥ, prathamaśravaṇānavagamāt । <quote>“karmaikē tatra darśanāt”</quote> iti kr̥takatvaṁ
﻿<pb n="262"/>
śabdasyōcyatē ; kimidaṁ kr̥takatvam ? puruṣaprayatnēnōtpattiḥ । nanvaprayatna-
pūrvikāpi śabdasyōtpattirdr̥ṣṭā yathā chalacchalādēḥ । nāyaṁ dōṣaḥ, abhidhānā-
dhikārāt । na cēdamabhidhānamaprayatnapūrvakaṁ dr̥śyatē । ataḥ kriyānantarōpa-
labdhēstayaivōtpadyata iti manyāmahē । kathaṁ tarhi mūlōdakādiṣu ?
anyatō'stitvāvagatēḥ ; śabdē punaḥ prayatnānantaraivōpalabdhiḥ । tasmānna
vidyamānasya prayatnō'bhivyañjaka iti śakyatē vak‍tum ।
nanvidamasti prayatnāt pūrvamastitvē pramāṇam । kimidamasti ? sapratyabhijñaṁ
﻿<pb n="263"/>
pratyakṣam । kathamatra pratyabhijñānam, anyatvānavagamāt ? anityatvavādinō
vā kimanyatvēnāvagatirasti ? kimiti nāsti pradhvastōtpannayōḥ ? viśēṣā-
grahaṇāt । kiṁ viśēṣāgrahaṇanibandhanaiva pratyabhijñā ? kiṁ vā manyatē
bhavān ? karmaṇyapi pratyabhijñā prāpnōti । svarūpagrahaṇē sati idamucyatē ;
ānumānikaṁ ca karma---ityuktam । kā vārtā jvālādiṣu ? nityatvē
﻿<pb n="264"/>
jvālādīnāmanumānavirōdha iti cēt, tulyamabhidhānē'pi, asthānādēḥ ।
tasmāt viśēṣāgrahaṇē'pyanyatā ; anyatvē ca siddhā prayatnānantarōpalabdhēḥ
prayatnanōtpattiḥ । nanu ca prayatnōtpannānāmapi kālāntarāvasthāyitayā naiva
vyavahārānupapattiḥ ; utpannasyāpi cakṣurādēḥ svābhāvikaṁ rūpagrahaṇasāmarthyaṁ
naiva vihanyatē । satyam ; naitacchabdē, asthānāt । nanu cakṣuṣō'sthā-
natvē'pi rūpagrahaṇaśaktirnaiva vihanyatē, tadvacchabdē'pīti cēt, pratyuktaṁ
﻿<pb n="265"/>
prathamaśravaṇānavagatēḥ । tasmāt <quote>‘asthānāt’</quote> ityayaṁ hēturautpattikatva-
vighātī sambandhasya । yadi kālāntarāvasthāyitā syāt, syādapi
vyavahārācchabdādarthāvagatiḥ ; asthāyitvē punaḥ samaya ēva śaraṇaṁ
bhavitumarhatītyuktam---<quote>“asthānāt”</quote> iti ।।</p>
<p>laukikamapyabhidhānamamumēva nyāyamanuvartatē । kātra nyāyānuvr̥ttiḥ ?
﻿<pb n="266"/>
mukhyārthatā karōtēḥ---śabdaṁ kuru, śabdaṁ mā kārṣīḥ, śabdakāryayaṁ
māṇavaka iti ।।</p>
<p><quote>“nānādēśēṣu ca yugapacchabdamupalabhāmahē ; tadēkasya nityasyānupapanna-
miti”</quote> kēyamanupapattiḥ ? iyamanupapattiḥ---yugapadēkasyānēkatrōpalabdhirna
dr̥ṣṭā । tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tatō bhavati---sādhitamanyatvam । nanu ca
sādhitamanyatvam । satyaṁ sādhitam ; hētupracayastu pradarśyatē ।
﻿<pb n="267"/>
kō lābhaḥ ? na khalu kaścit । na cēt kaścit, hētupracayēna kim ?
satyaṁ yathā bhavānāha ; kintvayamēvārthō rāddhāntamākṣipati । tasmāt
tadbhramapratiṣēdhārthō'yamārambhaḥ ; na hyanupanyastasya bhrāntatā śakyatē vak‍tum ;
apradarśitē ca bhrāntatvē'punaruktō'yaṁ bhavati kasyacinmandadhiyaḥ ।
sarvārthaṁ cēdaṁ śāstraṁ <quote>“mandaviṣēṇāpi”</quote> iti darśitaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa ।
<quote>“asati viśēṣē nityasya nānēkatvam”</quote> kimidam---asati viśēṣē
nityasya nānēkatvamiti ? <quote>‘asati viśēṣē nānātvaṁ nāsti’</quote> iti
śakyatē vak‍tuṁ nityasya anityasya vā ; nityagrahaṇaṁ
na vidmaḥ । yadyanityasyāsatyapi viśēṣē nānātvaṁ syāt, yuktaṁ
﻿<pb n="268"/>
vak‍tum <quote>‘nityasya’</quote> iti । tasmādvarṇanīyō'yaṁ granthaḥ । varṇyatē tarhi
---gavādērēkasyānēkatra yugapadupalabdhirdr̥ṣṭā nityasya sataḥ ; tasmāt
<quote>“sattvāntarē ca yaugapadyāt”</quote> ityasyānēnānyathāsiddhirāśaṅkitā ;
tasyēdamuttaram <quote>“asati viśēṣē”</quote> iti । kiṁ gavādērviśēṣō vidyatē ?
tadapi hyēkamaviśiṣṭam ; na hyanyacchābalēyē anyacca bāhulēyē ।
athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---asatyāśrayaviśēṣē---iti । tatrāpyāśrayasyaivānyatvam ;
kimāyātamāśrayiṇaḥ ? tasmānnityasyāpyēkasyānēkatra yugapadupalabdhirdr̥ṣṭā ।
atō nānyatvē yugapaddarśanaṁ hētuḥ । athēdaṁ matam---
﻿<pb n="269"/>
naiva gavādēryugapaddarśanamanēkatra ; bhēdā ēva hi tatrānēkadēśatayā
gr̥hyantē, na gōtvamiti । kathaṁ tarhi sarvēṣu <quote>‘gauḥ’</quote>, <quote>‘gauḥ’</quote> iti buddhiḥ ?
ata ēvānēkadēśatvaṁ gōtvasya nāsti । anyathā hi <quote>‘iha gōtvam’</quote>,
<quote>‘iha gōtvam’</quote> iti syāt । kathaṁ tarhi <quote>“iha pratyayāt samavāyaḥ” ?</quote>
﻿<pb n="270"/>
ēkadravyapadārthābhiprāyaṁ tat, na vyaktyabhiprāyam । tasmāddhēturanyatvē
yugapaddarśanam । <quote>“asati viśēṣē”</quote> iti ca yuktaṁ viśēṣagrahaṇam । nanu
cānityasyāpyasati viśēṣē naivānyatvam । bāḍhamasti jvālādiṣu ;
kāryatvāccāvirōdhaḥ । nityasya tvakāryatvādanēkatvavirōdha iti yuktō hētuḥ ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="271"/>
<p>prakr̥tivikārabhāvañca śabdajñāḥ smaranti ; na cāyaṁ nityasyōpapadyatē ;
tasmāt smr̥tirapi pūrvōktahētvanuguṇaiva । sādr̥śyamapyanuguṇamupalabhāmaha
ityupapannaṁ kāryatvam ।।</p>
<p>kāraṇavr̥ddha‍yanugamācca kāryatvaṁ manyāmahē jvālādīnāmiva ।
﻿<pb n="272"/>
tasmādanupalakṣyamāṇāvayavasyāpi avayavavr̥ddhiranumīyatē ; jvālaivātra
nidarśanam ।।</p>
<p><quote>“samaṁ tu tatra darśanam”</quote> । kimidaṁ samaṁ darśanam ? idaṁ tat samaṁ
﻿<pb n="273"/>
darśanam---kāryē cākāryē ca tulyō hēturiti । kathaṁ tulyatā ?
sāṁnyāsikatayā । kimatra saṁnyastam ? idamatra saṁnyastam---yadi
sapratyabhijñapratyakṣagrāhyatāṁ vakṣyāma iti । nanu uktaṁ tat parihr̥taṁ
ca---jvālādiṣvivānumānē pratyarthini na śakyata ēkatāṁ vak‍tumiti ।
satyam ; yadi bhēdāgrahaṇanibandhanaiva pratyabhijñōcyēta ; tadgra/?/haṇanibandhanā
sā---iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ । tasmādupapannam <quote>“samaṁ tu tatra darśanam”</quote>
iti ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="274"/>
<p><quote>“sataḥ paramadarśanaṁ viṣayānāgamāt”</quote> iti tadvadanaikāntikama-
darśanamapītyuktam । nanvētannōpapadyatē ; nityasyādarśanē kō hētuḥ ? yadi paraṁ
viṣayānāgamaḥ, astu tarhi । sa ēvātra durbhaṇaḥ । kimiti ? nityapakṣē hyabhi-
vyaṅgyatvaṁ śabdasya ; ēkaścāyaṁ śabda ēkaviṣayaśca ākāśaviṣayatvāt ;
grāhakaṁ cāsyākāśamēva ; kēyaṁ viṣayānāgatiḥ ? tasmāt dhvastasyaivānu-
palabdhirnyāyyā । kēna vōktam---na nyāyyēti ? tadgrahaṇē tu sati sarvasyai-
vāsyānyāyyatā nyāyyā । ata ēvōktam---<quote>“yadi śakṣyāmaḥ”</quote> iti ।
﻿<pb n="275"/>
nanu tad‍grahaṇē'pi nātra āvaraṇādikalpanā ātmānaṁ labhatē । kimiti ?
pūrvaklr̥ptavirōdhāt । kiṁ klr̥ptam ? ākāśamindriyam ; taccaikam ।
tasmāt saṁyōgavibhāgayōrabhivyañ‍jakatvē satyapi sarvaśabdānāṁ sarvaiścōpa-
labdhiḥ prāpnōti । yuktaṁ tāvat sarvairgrahaṇam ; sarvaśabdānāṁ tu na
yuktam, kāraṇavadabhivyañ‍jakānyatvāt । sarvaiścōpalabdhiḥ kāryapakṣē'pi
tulyaiva । yaścōbhayadōṣaḥ, na tamēkaścōdyō bhavatīti parihr̥tamidaṁ dūṣaṇaṁ
kārakābhivyañ‍jakayōrviśēṣābhidhānēna vinā naiva cōdyēran nityatvavādinaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="276"/>
ayamasti viśēṣaḥ---abhivyaktiḥ śabdasya, indriyasya vā syāt ?
tatra śabdābhivyaktau tāvadēkaviṣayatvāt sarvaśabdānāṁ ghaṭādīnāmivaika-
viṣayāṇāṁ nābhivyaktiḥ kramēṇa śakyatē vak‍tum, adr̥ṣṭatvāt prasiddhānā-
mabhivyañjakānāṁ pradīpādīnām ; kāraṇānāṁ tu kāryadarśanāt
śakyamanumānaṁ śaktēḥ । nanvabhivyañ‍jakānāmapyabhivyaktidarśanādēvānumānaṁ
yuktaṁ śaktēḥ । na kāryapakṣē pratipakṣatayā saṁbhavati । kō vā viśēṣaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="277"/>
prasiddhēṣu kāraṇēṣu darśanāt, abhivyañ‍jakēṣu cādarśanāt । dr̥ṣṭānuguṇaṁ
cānumānam, na dr̥ṣṭavirōdhi । nanu caikaviṣayatvē virōdhaḥ ; viṣayāntarē
tu virōdhakathā viruddhaiva । satyam ; viṣayāntarataivātra durvacā । na durvacā ।
śrōtramākāśamityabhyupagamāt ; abhinnaṁ cākāśam ; sarvaśabdāśca śrōtra-
viṣayāḥ ; tasmādēkaviṣayatvam ; viṣayaikyācca dr̥ṣṭavirōdhaḥ । kimidaṁ
﻿<pb n="278"/>
pralapyatē ? tadidamapatitam---karṇē spr̥ṣṭaḥ kaṭiṁ cālayati iti ;
abhivyaktērviṣayō nirupyatē, na punaḥ śabdasya ; anyaścāyaṁ pradīpādi-
viṣayādviṣayaḥ । tasmāt pradīpādivirōdhācchabdē'bhivyañjakānumānavirōdhō
na śakyatē vak‍tumityuktam । tasmāttadgrahaṇanibandhanamanumānaṁ durnivāram ।
atō'darśanamidānīmanaikāntikamityuktam । nanu śrōtraviṣayēyabhivyaktiḥ, na
śabdaviṣayā । <quote>‘abhivyaktaṁ hi śrōtraṁ śabdaṁ gr̥hṇāti’</quote> ityētāvadabhivyañjakē
śaktyanumānam, na punaḥ <quote>‘amuṁ śabdam amuṁ na’</quote> ityasaṁsparśādabhi-
﻿<pb n="279"/>
vyañjakānām । ayamēva ca siddhāntaḥ । sa cāyamanumānavirōdhītyuktam ।
satyam ; prasiddhānumānabādhanamayuktam । prasiddhapratyakṣabādhanamapyayuktamēva ।
﻿<pb n="280"/>
sapratyabhijñaṁ ca pratyakṣamātmani sāmānyādiṣu ca sthitam । ubhayōrabādhyatvē
sati kasyacidarthasyāsiddhērēkasya bādhanam ; anumānāt pratyakṣaṁ balīya
iti naiyāyikāḥ । nanu ca pratyakṣaṁ bhramabhāk । anumānē'pi bhrāntiravi-
śiṣṭā । na brūmaḥ---anumānē'pi bhrāntirnāsti iti ; kintvatra bhēdāgrahaṇā-
ttadbuddhiratasminnapi bhavati । saṁbhāvitabhramamiti pratyakṣamēva durbalaṁ manyāmahē ।
anayaiva prakaṭitāprakaṭitabhramakāraṇatayōktaṁ nyāyavidbhiḥ <quote>“bhavati vai pratyakṣā-
dapyanumānaṁ balīyaḥ”</quote> iti । kiṁ nirjñātakāraṇaduṣṭataivātrōpanyastā ? kiṁ
jātam, yadyupanyastā ? nanu ca viparyayābhāvāt naivāstitayōpanyasituṁ
﻿<pb n="281"/>
śakyatē । kiṁ viparyaya ēva mithyātvē hētuḥ ? kāraṇadōṣō'pyasamīcīnahētu-
tayōpanyasta ēva । nanu ca kāraṇadōṣaḥ prayatnēnōpalabhyamānatayōktaḥ । kō'yaṁ
prayatnō nāma, 	jō'sāvatra nāstītyucyatē ? apamēvāsau prayatnaḥ---anyatra
viparyayāt kāraṇadōṣaṁ vijñāya tadbhāvabhāvitayaiva <quote>‘ētatkr̥tō'yaṁ viparyayaḥ’</quote>
iti tamanyatra vijānāti; jñātē ca tasmin asatyapi viparyayē <quote>‘bhrānta-
midam’</quote> ityadhyavasyati । kimatraivaṁbhūtamasti ? bāḍhamasti bhēdāgrahaṇam;
bhēdāgrahaṇānibandhana ēva śuktikādiṣu rajatabhramaḥ । ēvamatrāpi bhēdāgrahaṇa-
nibandhana ēva jvālādiṣviva tadbhramaḥ । tasmāt suṣṭhūktam---
﻿<pb n="282"/>
śabda ēva tad‍grahaṇaṁ bhrāntiḥ---iti । yasya tāvadviparītākāramarthē
jñānamutpadyatē kadācit, tasya yuktaṁ vaktum <quote>‘viparyayābhāvānnāyaṁ
bhramaḥ’</quote> iti; yasya punaragrahaṇanibandhana ēva viparyayaḥ, tasya punaḥ
kā śaktirvak‍tumanumānavirōdhē sati jvālādivaiṣamyam ? nanu
cāgrahaṇamapi punargrahaṇādavasīyatē । na cātra kasyāṁcidavasthāyāṁ bhēdasya
grahaṇamasti saugandhikasphaṭikayōriva । jvālādiṣu katham ?
anumānādavagatiriti cēt, tattulyamatrāpi । tasmāt śabdaviṣayaṁ
sapratyabhijñaṁ pratyakṣamāśāpāśamātraṁ mīmāṁsakānām । yadapyuktamanyaiḥ---
﻿<pb n="283"/>
tulyē'pi saṁskāryē saṁskārabhēdāt kāryānyatvamupalabhyata iti yathā
maṇḍūkavasayāktākṣā vaṁśānuragāniva paśyanti iti, tadidamākāśavijr̥-
mbhitam; saṁskārō hi nāma sa bhavati, yaḥ svakāryē śaktimupajanayati;
na caitadindriyasya kāryam, yadidamayathārthagrahaṇam; agrahaṇanibandhanamēva
taditi pratipāditam । tasmādabhēdē'pi saṁskāryasya saṁskārānyatvēna
kāryānyatvaṁ jñāpakē na vidyatē ityanyat kiñcidupadarśanīyam । yacca---
khaḍgadarpaṇādiṣvanyathābhivyajyatē mukhamiti, kimuktaṁ bhavati ?
grāhyē'yamuparāgō dr̥ṣṭaḥ; yuktaśca, abhivyañjakasyāpi viṣayāpattēḥ;
﻿<pb n="284"/>
iha punaḥ śrōtramagrāhyam, saṁyōgavibhāgāvapi । ata idamapyākāśa-
vijr̥mbhitamēva । tasmāt <quote>‘śabdō nityaḥ’</quote> iti śraddhayaiva pratipattavyam,
śabdātmakatvādvēdasya vēdanindā mā bhūditi । paṭhitaṁ ca dharmaśāstrakāraiḥ---
<quote>“sa sādhubhirbahiṣkāryō nāstikō vēdanindakaḥ”</quote> iti । tasmādanidaṁ-
prathamataivātra śaraṇam; na punaḥ śabdanityatāpūrvakamanapēkṣatvaṁ śakyatē
yuktitō vak‍tum । kalpyatāṁ rāgādivinirmuktamapratihatajñānaṁ karuṇā-
viṣṭacētasaṁ bhagavantaṁ kaṁcana munivaram; āśrīyatāṁ vā suragurōrdarśanam---
﻿<pb n="285"/>
vyavahāramātramavēdaṁ vēdatrayābhihitaṁ paśyāmaḥ prājñairlōkayātrāsiddha‍yarthaṁ
supratibandhamanupālyamānamiti । idamēva yuktaṁ manyāmahē; na hi dr̥ṣṭē
saṁbhavatyadr̥ṣṭakalpanā nyāyyā । dr̥ṣṭaścāyamarthaḥ---yat prājñaiḥ r̥java upa-
jīvyanta iti । yathā ca siddhamāgamavādināmapi hētudarśanādaprāmāṇyam
<quote>“yūpahastinō dānamācaranti”</quote> ityēvamādiṣu । kartavyō vā
﻿<pb n="286"/>
sapratyabhijñasya pratyakṣasya śabdō viṣaya iti yatnaḥ । kathaṁ punarjvālādēri-
vānumānācchakyatē'nyatvamavagantum ? nanu cānumānādityuktam । kiṁ
tadanumānam ? anabhivyañjakavaiṣamyam । nanvabhivyañjakānāmanēkaviṣayā
śaktirdr̥ṣṭā । nanu cēdamabhivyañjakaviṣayamanumānam; kathamanyaviṣaya-
manumānamanyaviṣayasyāvacchittau hētuḥ ? śrōtrasya hyabhivyañjakasaṁskāraṁ
niruṇaddhi, na punaḥ śabdasyānyatvamavagamayati । nanu cōktam---na
cēt saṁyōgavibhāgāḥ śrōtrasya śabdagrahaṇasamarthaṁ saṁskāramāpādayanti,
śabdasyōtpādakāḥ prāp‍nuyuḥ; utpattau cānyatvam---iti । kathama-
﻿<pb n="287"/>
nyapratiṣēdhō'nyasyōtpattimavagamayati ? anyathā vyāpārānupapattēḥ । na
cētsaṁskārakāḥ saṁskuryuḥ, kimanyadataḥ śabdōtpattēḥ ? kiṁ yasya saṁskārakatā
nōpapadyētē, tēnōtpādakēna bhavitavyam ? na cēdutpādakaḥ, nirvyāpāra
ēva syāt; anyārthatā ca saṁyōgavibhāgayōrupalabdhā । satyam;
yadarthāḥ, tatra bhavantūtpādakāḥ saṁskārakā vā । parapratipattyarthatā ca siddhā;
tattayōryadiṣṭaṁ tatparikalpyatām; viṣayāntarē punaḥ sambandhābhāvāt
kimāspadaṁ kalpanāyāḥ ? tasmādanyatvē hētutāṁ saṁyōgavibhāgayōḥ
kathamiva naiyāyikā manyantē ? ēvaṁ manyantē---na cēt śrōtrē
﻿<pb n="288"/>
kāryamasti, śabdē kāryaṁ pratipadyāmahē । kiṁ kāryatastādarthyam ?
ōm ityucyatē । siddhaṁ tarhi kāryaṁ śrōtrē; na saṁyōgavibhāgāḥ
śabdārthāḥ---iti manyantē śabdavidaḥ । nanu ca kāryadarśanāt na
yuktaṁ vak‍tuṁ śabdavidām । kāryadarśanamēva nāstīti bruvatē, śabdē
tad‍grahaṇāt । kiṁ tarhi kurvanti saṁyōgavibhagāḥ ? śrōtrasaṁskāramiti
﻿<pb n="289"/>
brūmaḥ । nanu cānyaiḥ saṁskāraiḥ vailakṣaṇyamatra nōpapadyatē---ityuktam ।
anumānāt kāryābhāvaṁ manyatē bhavān; vayaṁ tu pratyakṣādutpattiṁ nēcchāmaḥ;
pratyakṣānumānayōśca pratyakṣaṁ balīya iti siddham । nanu cāgrahaṇaṁ
bhramahēturityuktaṁ jvālādīnāmiva । iha tu agrahaṇamēvāsiddham ।
﻿<pb n="290"/>
tatra katham ? kāryānumānāt । iha punastadadyāpi na sidhyati;
na cāsiddhaṁ siddhau paryāptam । pratyakṣaṁ cānapēkṣatvāt siddham ।
anumānē vā kāpēkṣā ? iyamēvāpēkṣā---siddhē'numānē kāryam, kāryē
ca satyanumānamiti; na punarēvaṁ pratyakṣaṁ tad‍grahaṇāpēkṣam; pratyakṣādēva
hi tad‍grahaṇam । kiñca, saṁyōgavibhāgau śrōtrārthatayānyataḥ prasiddhau ।
﻿<pb n="291"/>
kutō'nyataḥ ? uktam <quote>“darśanasya parārthatvāt”</quote> iti lōkataḥ । tasmāt
tādarthyē sati yathā saṁbhavati tathā kāryaṁ kalpanīyam । na kāryata-
stātparyam, anyatō'navagamāt ityuktam । tasmānnātra jvālādīnāmiva
pramāṇamasti । tasmāt <quote>“sataḥ paramadarśanam”</quote> iti yuktamanaikānti-
katvam । kathaṁ tarhyēkaviṣayaivābhivyaktiḥ śakyatē vaktum ? kārya-
darśanāt yuktā adr̥ṣṭasya kalpanā; atō dr̥ṣṭasya tad‍grahaṇasya nāpahnavō
nyāyyaḥ । kāryāntaradarśanāttu kāraṇānyatvakalpanā nyāyyaivēti ।
﻿<pb n="292"/>
<quote>“uparatayōḥ saṁyōgavibhāgayōḥ”</quote> iti kau tau saṁyōgavibhāgāvabhiprētau ?
tālvādīnāmiti brūmaḥ । kuta ētat ? uparatayōriti śravaṇāt;
vāyavīyānāmutpattiruparatiścānumēyā । <quote>“na nūnamuparamanti”</quote> iti
kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? vāyavīyān saṁyōgavibhāgān manasi kr̥tvā
kāryasamadhigamyatvādidamuttaram <quote>“na hi tē pratyakṣāḥ”</quote>---iti spaṣṭī-
﻿<pb n="293"/>
kr̥tam । yadyēvam, idānīmuttaragranthō nōpapadyatē <quote>“ākāśaviṣayatvā-
ttasya, ēkatvāccākāśasya”</quote> iti । kathaṁ nōpapadyatē ? vāyavīyānā-
mabhivyañjakatvē kāryapakṣa iva <quote>‘yatra tē, tatraivōpalabdhyā bhavitavyam’</quote>
ityēvaṁ nōpapadyatē । athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---abhivyaktipakṣē naiva vāyvāśritāḥ
śabdā bhavanti । kiṁ tarhi ? ākāśasthā ēva । yēṣāṁ punaḥ kriyantē,
﻿<pb n="294"/>
tēṣāṁ vāyavīyāḥ saṁyōgavibhāgā asamavāyikāraṇatāṁ pratipadyantē ।
tadēva samavāyikāraṇaṁ bhavati । yatraiva kāraṇam, tatraiva kāryōpalabdhi-
riti yuktam । ēvamapi nirjñātē vāyavīyasaṁyōgavibhāgayōrabhivyakti-
kāraṇatvē yatraivābhivyañjakam, tatraivābhivyaktiḥ; yathā yatraiva kāraṇam,
tatraiva kāryam । athaitanmanyasē---kāryē ētadyuktam, nābhivyaktā-
viti, tadayuktam; abhivyaktirapi kāryamēva; abhivyaṅgyaṁ tu
﻿<pb n="295"/>
pūrvōtpannam; atō yaddēśābhivyaktiḥ, tatraivōpalabdhiriti tulyamubhayōrapi
pakṣayōḥ । tasmādva‍yākhyēyō'yaṁ granthaḥ । aviśēṣajñō dēvānāṁ priyaḥ ।
kāryaṁ hi kāraṇadēśaṁ bhavati; akāryaṁ punarna parāpēkṣadēśam ।
tasmādabhivyaktirbhavatvabhivyañjakadēśā abhivyaṅgyaṁ tu kimiti
taddēśam, atajjanyatvādabhivyaṅgyasya ? taddēśasya abhivyaṅgyatvābhimata-
śabdadēśasya caikatvādākāśasya sarvairgrahaṇaṁ prāpnōti jñātēṣvapi vāyavīya-
﻿<pb n="296"/>
saṁyōgavibhāgēṣuḥ sarvaśrōtrēṣvēkamākāśaṁ yataḥ । satyam; yathā
bhavānāha---yadi śabdasyābhivyañjakāḥ saṁyōgavibhāgāḥ syuḥ; śrōtrasya
tvabhivyañjakāḥ; śrōtrasya ca śrōtr̥dēśataiva । nanu cākāśamēva
śrōtram; taccānyatrāpi tulyaṁ śabdābhivyaktyā । ucyatē---satyaṁ
sarvatrākāśamēkam; kintu tasya śrōtrabhāvaḥ śrōtr̥dēśa ēva, kartrabhisambandhēna
karaṇatvāt; karturbhōgāyatanavaśēna śarīradēśa ēva kartr̥tvānna tulyatā ।
tasmādutpattāvivābhivyaktāvapi na sarvairupalabdhiḥ । <quote>‘naitadēvam;
aprāptāścēdupakurvanti, sannikr̥ṣṭaviprakr̥ṣṭadēśasthitau yugapacchabdamupalabhēyātām’</quote>
﻿<pb n="297"/>
iti । nanu śrōtrasaṁskārapakṣē <quote>‘dūrasthitaṁ śrōtraṁ na saṁskriyatē’</quote>
iti vadatāṁ prāptairēva saṁskāra ityuktam; asatyāṁ ca prāptau dūra-
sannikr̥ṣṭavyapadēśa ēva na ghaṭatē । kimidam <quote>‘aprāptāścēdupakurvanti’</quote>
iti ? aprāptāśaṅkaiva nāsti, <quote>“dūrē satyāḥ”</quote>---ityabhidhanāt ।
tasmānna vidmaḥ kathamidaṁ bhāṣyamāyātam ? ēvamidamāyātam---śrōtra-
saṁskārapakṣē sarvagatatvācchabdasya yāvati kāryagamyaḥ saṁskāraḥ, tāvati
﻿<pb n="298"/>
yugapad‍grahaṇaṁ prāpnōti । kō'bhiprāyaḥ ? nanu ca vāyavīyāḥ saṁyōga-
vibhāgāḥ naivāprāpya śrōtraṁ saṁskartuṁ kṣamāḥ । na hi saṁyōgavibhāgaiḥ saṁyōga-
vibhāgāntaramārabhyata iti śakyatē vak‍tum, ubhayaprasaṅgāt; na
hyēkasmin kāryē kāraṇadvayakalpanā ghaṭatē; kāryaṁ hi kāraṇamavagamayati,
na punaḥ kāryāntaramapi । tasmādutpattipakṣa ēvaitadupapadyatē---yāvadvēgaṁ
﻿<pb n="299"/>
saṁyōgavibhāgāḥ kāryamārabhanta iti, na punarabhivyaktipakṣē'pi । nanu
kāryapakṣē'pi kāryāntarakalpanā naiva ghaṭatē । satyaṁ na ghaṭatē;
kāryāntarōpalabdhistu pratyakṣaiva, dūrasthasamīpasthaiḥ kramēṇōpalabdhēḥ । nanu
cābhivyaktāvapi tulyam । na tulyam; na hyabhivyaktirabhivyaktyantaramārabhatē;
kāryasya tu kāryāntarārambhē na kaścidvirōdhaḥ; bhavati hyāpēkṣikaṁ kāryaṁ
kāraṇaṁ ca; na punarabhivyaktirabhivyañjikā cēti । tasmāt dūrasthasamīpasthai-
ryugapadēva śabdagrahaṇam, yāvati grahaṇam । tasmāt yuktō'yamākṣēpaḥ ।
﻿<pb n="300"/>
uddyōtasyōddyōtāntarāpēkṣā---iti bāliśabhāṣitamētat । tasmādvāyavīyāḥ
saṁyōgavibhāgāḥ śabdamārabhantām । aulūkyō vā bhavatu rāddhāntaḥ
<quote>“saṁyōgādvibhāgācchabdācca śabdaniṣpattiḥ”</quote> iti । kimatrānuktasya
﻿<pb n="301"/>
pradarśanam ? atrāpi mē śravaṇaṁ vidyata iti kō'yamabhimānaḥ ? nāya-
mabhimānaḥ; kasyacidajñasya---nāyaṁ rāddhāntō bhagavatā bhāṣyakārēṇōpanyastō
nirastaścēti bhavati matiḥ; tadapanōdanāyēdamupanyastam । vāyuśabdō-
panyāsēnaivāyamupanyastō nirastaśca, tulyakāraṇatvādupanyāsasya nirāsasya ca ।
﻿<pb n="302"/>
tasmādabhivyaktikāryapakṣayōranyathātvapradarśanārthō'yaṁ granthaḥ ।</p>
<p><quote>“naitadēvam abhighātēna hi prēritā vāyavaḥ stimitāni vāyvantarāṇi
pratibādhamānāḥ sarvatōdikkān saṁyōgavibhāgānutpādayantō yāvadvēgamabhi-
pratiṣṭhantē”</quote> iti । nanu tadēvēdamutpādakatvamuktam; pratijñātaṁ cābhivyañjakatvaṁ
saṁyōgavibhāgānām । tasmādasambaddhamēvēdaṁ pratibhāti । kimiti bhōḥ ?
﻿<pb n="303"/>
uktamitīti । anabhivyaktijñō bhavān । kātrānabhivyaktijñatā ?
iyamanabhivyaktijñatā; abhivyaktirhi tiraskārāpanayaḥ । kēna vōktam <quote>‘na’</quote>
iti ? sa ēvāpanayō'panayāntaraṁ nārabhatē---ityuktam; sakr̥dva‍yāparā hyapanayē
﻿<pb n="304"/>
bhavantyapanētāraḥ, na yāvadapanēyamādityaprabhādaya iva । satyam; yadyēka
ēvāpanētānēkavyāpāraḥ parikalpyēta, syādayaṁ dōṣaḥ; atra punarbahavō'bhi-
vyañjakāḥ । kathamidaṁ jñāyatē ? bhavatō vā kāryapakṣē kāraṇabahutvaṁ
katham ? kāryabahutvāditi cēt, mamāpyabhivyaktibahutvādabhivyañjaka-
bahutvam । kathaṁ punarabhivyaktibahutvam ? yathaiva kāryabahutvam । ēkatvē
﻿<pb n="305"/>
punarvakṣyāmaḥ pratyakṣasya balīyastvamityuktam । ēkatvē ca nityatā;
nityatvē'bhivyaktibahutvamēva, na kāryabahutvamiti sthitiḥ ।।</p>
<p>prayōgasyēti । sthitē ētasmin nyāyē gōmayādivat prayōgasiddhiḥ,
pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayatvāllaukikasya vākyasya ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="306"/>
<p><quote>“yathaitadēkasya sataḥ”</quote> ityanēkatābhrāntimāpādayati । kathaṁ punaḥ
viparyayādr̥tē bhrāntiriti śakyatē vak‍tum ? kāraṇadōṣadarśanāt । kasya
kāraṇasyātra duṣṭatā avagamyatē ? viṣayasya tāvacchrōtrapathāsattērnaiva duṣṭatā ।
śrōtrasyāpyabhivyaktatvāt naiva । atha dr̥ṣṭaṁ śrōtramiti kalpyatē; ēvaṁ tarhi
﻿<pb n="307"/>
śabdasyaiva grahaṇaṁ na prāpnōti । na ca śabdādr̥tē'nyacchrōtrasya grāhyamasti ।
yadyēvaṁ kāryapakṣē'pi kathamanēkatvagrahaṇaṁ śrautram ? naiva tacchrautram; mānasaṁ
hi tat । manasā vā kiṁ śrōtrēṇāgr̥hītamēva bāhyaṁ vastu gr̥hyatē ? kiṁ vātra
śabdavyatiriktaṁ bāhyaṁ vastvabhiprētaṁ bhavataḥ ? yadidaṁ śabdanānātvam ।
kiṁ vā śabdavyatiriktamidaṁ śabdanānātvam ? kiṁ śabda ēva, uta
﻿<pb n="308"/>
śabdādanyaḥ śabdadharmaḥ ? na tāvadayaṁ śabdasyaiva dharmō bhavati, rūpādiṣvapi
darśanāt; rūpādyapi hi <quote>‘nānā’</quote> iti gamyatē । nāpyayaṁ śabda ēva,
<quote>‘nānātvaṁ śabdasya’</quote> iti vyatirēkadarśanāt । tasmānna vidyaḥ kasyēndriyasya
vyāpāraḥ, yasya duṣṭatā kalpyēta । kiṁ tarhīdaṁ nānātvamagrāhyamēva ? dr̥śyatē
tu sarvārthēṣu । buddhirūpatā cāgrāhyatvādba‍uddhēḥ pratyuktā । ucyatē---yadyasya
grāhyaṁ gr̥hītē ca tasmin grāhyāntarāvamarśō nānātvam । ēvaṁ tarhi śrōtrasyaiva
﻿<pb n="309"/>
dr̥ṣṭatā । duṣṭē ca śabdagrahaṇaṁ na prāpnōti । asati ca śabdagrahaṇē śabdānta-
rāvamarśaḥ kutaḥ ? tasmādavamarśē duṣṭatā kalpanīyā, na punaḥ śabdagrahaṇē ।
manasastarhi duṣṭatvam । nanu ca manasō'pi naiva duṣṭatvaṁ śakyatē vak‍tum,
śrōtragrahaṇē yathārthagrahaṇāt; na hyagr̥hītasamyagarthasya tadarthāvamarśō ghaṭatē ।
﻿<pb n="310"/>
tasmāddēvā ēnāṁ bhrāntiṁ kalpayiṣyanti, aviparyayāt duṣṭakāraṇatānavadhr̥tēśca ।
abhrāntē ca bhrāntyabhidhānaṁ bhramādapi pāpīyaḥ । tasmādbhramakāraṇamatra
vaktavyaṁ bhrāntijñaiḥ । idamabhidhīyatē---uktaṁ bhavataiva <quote>‘nāgr̥hītabāhyēndriyēṇa
manasā gr̥hyatē’</quote> iti । indriyēṇa ca tad‍grahaṇāt anēkatvaṁ
nāstīti pratyakṣēṇāvasitam । manasāpyanēkatvagrahaṇaṁ naivōpapadyatē ।
kimālambanamasyāḥ, kiñcēndriyamanēkatvāvagatēḥ ? idamindriyamidaṁ
cālambanam---nānādēśasthā hi dhvanayō yugapadāgacchanta itarētaranirapēkṣā
﻿<pb n="311"/> 
ēva yugapat saṁskārānārabhantē śrōtrasya; tatsaṁskārānurōdhāccaikamapi
śabdamanēkamiva gr̥hṇāti । ēkaikasaṁskārōpajananācchaktēḥ nāyanaśaktirivāṅu-
libhinnā ēkamapi bhinnamiva gr̥hṇāti । tasmācchaktibhēdāgrahanibandhanō'yaṁ
﻿<pb n="312"/>
bhramaḥ । anēna sāntarālagrahaṇaṁ pratyuktam । kathaṁ punaranēna sāntarāla-
grahaṇaṁ pratyucyatē ? yuktaṁ tāvat saṁskārabhēdāt śak‍tyudbōdhaḥ ।
tadanurōdhinī bhinnā ca śaktirēkamapi viṣayaṁ bhēdēna samarpayantī
svabhēdāgrahaṇādanēkagrahaṇabhramamutpādayatīti । antarālagrahaṇē kō hētuḥ ?
tasmāt kāraṇāntaraṁ brūhi । nōcyatē; idamēva kāraṇam । kathamidaṁ
kāraṇam ? nānādēśōtthā dhvanayō bhēdēna saṁskāramārabhamāṇā ā mūlaṁ śaktē-
rudbōdhaṁ janayanti । ataḥ śrōtrākāśasthitō'pi śabdō'nugrāhakānurōdhā-
ttaddēśastha iva gr̥hyatē । nanu cāntya ēva saṁyōgavibhāgaḥ saṁskarōti ।
﻿<pb n="313"/>
kēyaṁ mandatā bhavataḥ ? ananugr̥hītapūrvasaṁyōgavibhāgō'ntyaḥ saṁskarōtīti
nōpapadyatē; tadanugrāhakavaśādutpattiriva kāryam । ata ēva ca
﻿<pb n="314"/>
pūrvavēgānuvartyuparamaḥ saṁskārāṇām । tasmādātmōdayānurūpamupajanayantastathā
tathā tamavagamayanti ।</p>
<p><quote>“kāmaṁ dēśā ēva bhinnāḥ syuḥ”</quote> iti kimarthō'yamupanyāsaḥ ?
﻿<pb n="315"/>
prāpnōti, yadi śravaṇēndriyaṁ saṁyōgavibhāgadēśamāgacchēt; na caitadasti,
bhāṣya ēva pratyuktatvāt । ata ēva <quote>“kāmam”</quote> ityuktam । sattvāntara-
pakṣē'pi tāvat bhēdō na prāpnōtītyabhiprāyaḥ । nanu ēkasyānēkatrōpa-
labdhiḥ । mūrkhapralapitamētat; ēkasyānēkatrōpalabdhiḥ paricōditā
parihr̥tā ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="316"/>
<p><quote>“śabdāntaramavikāraḥ”</quote> naivēha <quote>“ikō yaṇaci”</quote> iti prakr̥tivikārabhāva
upadiśyatē; na hi lōkē yakāraṁ prayuyukṣamāṇā ikāramupādadatē । lōka-
siddhasya cādēśā bhavanti । tasmādayamartha ādēśikaḥ---aci parata
ikārasya sthānē yakāraḥ । sādr̥śyaṁ tu prakr̥tivikārabhāvē'naikāntikam ।
﻿<pb n="317"/>
dadhipiṭakakundapiṭakayōradarśanāt ityuktam, ataḥ siddhaṁ śabdāntaratvam ।।</p>
<p><quote>“nādavr̥ddhiḥ parā”</quote> tulyaṁ bhēdaparihārēṇa; yathaiva hi tatra bhinnā
bhinnamivāvagamayanti, ēvamatrāpi pracitāḥ pracitamiva, vibhāgasthitā
vibhaktamiva । atō mahāniva avayavavāniva ca bhrāntirupapadyatē ।
﻿<pb n="318"/>
saṁskārānurōdhācchaktērudbōdhaḥ---ityuktam । tasmādayamapi saṁskārabhēdāgrahaṇa-
nibandhana ēva bhramaḥ । ataḥ sthitē sapratyabhijñapratyakṣē pūrvōktamanaikāntikī-
kr̥tamanityatvē hētujātam ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="319"/>
<p>idānīṁ sapratyabhijñapratyakṣasya śabdaviṣayatōcyatē---<quote>“nityastu
syāddarśanasya parārthatvāt”</quote> iti । <quote>“darśanasya parārthatvāt”</quote> iti kasyāyaṁ
hētuḥ ? nityatāyāḥ śabdasya । nanu cāyamapakṣadharmaḥ; apakṣadharmasya cāsya
hētutvaṁ nāstīti naiyāyikāḥ । aśrutaśāstrā hi tē । darśanamēvātra parārthatayōpa-
nyasyatē; tacca nirviṣayaṁ nāstīti śabdō'tra viṣayatayōpanyasyatē । tataḥ
﻿<pb n="320"/>
kim ? idaṁ tataḥ---<q>parārthadarśanasambandhitā hētuḥ । ētaduktaṁ bhavati
---parārthaṁ darśanaṁ yasya । tasya kim ? nityatā । kasya yathā ?
sarvasyēti brūmō dhūmādēḥ । nanu ca svapratipattyarthamapi darśanaṁ dhūmādēḥ ।
bhavatu; parapratipattyarthatāpi, anirākaraṇīyaṁ caitadavirōdhāt । śabdē'pi
﻿<pb n="321"/>
vidyamānatvāt । kālāntarāvasthāyitvaṁ ca nityaśabdēnōcyatē, na
sadakāraṇatvam । nanu caṁ sannakāraṇaśca śabda iṣyatē । bāḍhamiṣyatē;
sa tu parārthamātratayaiva darśanasya siddhati । kimiti tarhi viśēṣa
ucyatē ? kathaṁ nāmanityasyāpi dhūmādērdr̥ṣṭāntatā syāt । nanu
﻿<pb n="322"/>
cāsyāpyanityatā prāpnōti, prasiddhē darśanāt । ata ēva kālāntarā-
vasthāyitvamātraṁ sādhyatayōcyatē । kālāntarāvasthāyitayā ca siddhaṁ
śabdasya sadakāraṇatvam । darśanamēva hi tasya kāraṇatayā śaṅkitaṁ paraiḥ;
tacca parārthatayā akāraṇatāṁ gatam । tasmāt parārthadarśanasambandhitā-
mātrasya hētutvaṁ śabdasya sadakāraṇatvaṁ siddham । nanu ca
tattulyōpādānamabhēdamupādāya sidhyati pārārthyaṁ darśanasya । satyaṁ
﻿<pb n="323"/>
sidhyati; kintu nētthaṁbhūtatvē pramāṇamasti । na kasyaci-
dapyāsaṁsāraṁ jantōḥ <quote>‘pūrvōktasadr̥śamuccārayāmi, tatsadr̥śa ēvāyam’</quote>
iti jñānōtpādō dr̥ṣṭaḥ । ata ēva cāviparītaṁ pratipadyantē । anyathā
mālāśabdapratyayasyēva śālāśabdasaṁvēdanādviparyayaḥ syāt । nanu ca na
﻿<pb n="324"/>
sādr̥śyē'pi viparyayō dr̥śyatē yathā gōgāvīśabdayōḥ । tadēkagrāhiṇāṁ
tu na dr̥śyatē viparyayaḥ, na sādr̥śyagrāhiṇām; tattvavidāṁ tvanutpattirēva ।
kimidaṁ tattvavidāmiti ? gōśabdasya gāvyādayō'pabhraṁśāḥ---ityēvaṁvidaḥ
tattvavidaḥ । tēṣāṁ naiva gāvyādibhyō'pyarthajñānamutpadyatē gōśabdādēvārthaṁ
pratipadyantē---ityuktaṁ vyākhyātr̥bhiḥ । na cānāditayā saṁsārasyādi-
﻿<pb n="325"/>
śabdatā kasyacitkalpayituṁ śakyatē, yatsadr̥śōpādānāt saṁvyavahāra-
siddhiḥ । tasmāt sapratyabhijñapratyakṣamūlō'yaṁ vyavahāra iti sthitam ।</p>
﻿<pb n="326"/>
<p>anyadēva ca sādhitam, anyaccōpasaṁhr̥tam; kālāntarāvasthitiḥ
sādhitā, sapratyabhijñaṁ pratyakṣamupasaṁhr̥tam; anyadēvōpanyastam,
anyaccōpanipatitam । tadēvēdam; pratyabhijñānādēva hi kālāntarāvasthāyitā
sidhyati । kālāntarāvasthitiśca sapratyabhijñapratyakṣagamyētyuktam । yadi
pratyabhijñayaiva kālāntarāvasthāyitvaṁ sādhyatē, kimiti tarhi parārthadarśana-
sambandhitā hēturityuktam ? yata ēva pratyabhijñayaiva kālāntarāvasthāyitā,
ata ēva parārthadarśanasambandhitā hēturityuktam; pratyabhijñaiva hyabhinnārtha-
﻿<pb n="327"/>
darśanamityucyatē, na punaranyat । svarūpasya darśanāntarasiddhatvāt
tatpūrvakatvācca pratyabhijñāyāḥ । na ca svārthaparārthatāmēkō yatnaḥ pratipattuṁ kṣamaḥ ।।</p>
<p><quote>“sarvatra yaugapadyāt”</quote>---iti । anēnānvayavyatirēkasamadhigamya-
marthāvagatihētutvaṁ darśayati śabdasya । kimatō yadyēvam ? kālāntarāva-
﻿<pb n="328"/>
sthāyitā sidhyati; na hi kālāntarānavasthāyinō'nvayavyatirēkaniścayaḥ;
ataḥ kālāntarāvasthāyitā sidhyati । kālāntarāvasthitiśca sapratyabhijña-
pratyakṣasamadhigamyētyuktam । kathaṁ punaranvayavyatirēkasamadhigamyamasyārthāvagati-
hētutvam ? ākr̥tēḥ padārthatvāt । na caikaprayōgāvagamyā ākr̥tēḥ padārthatā,
svātantryēṇāgrahaṇāt dravyāśritānām; agr̥hītānāṁ ca pr̥thaṅ‌nirdēśā
﻿<pb n="329"/>
yōgyatvāt । tasmāt vyavahārasamadhigamyaivākr̥tipadārthatā, na nirdēśa-
samadhigamyā । vyavahāraścānvayavyatirēkasamadhigamya iti siddhā pratyabhijñā ।।</p>
<p><quote>“saṁkhyābhāvāt”</quote> tadēvēdaṁ sapratyabhijñaṁ pratyakṣaṁ punarupanyasyatē
hētupracayadarśanārtham । hētupracayē punaḥ kō'rthō'bhyadhikaḥ sidhyati
hētvantaranirapēkṣatvāddhētūnāṁ svārthasiddhau ? na khalu kaścit । anarthakastarhi
﻿<pb n="330"/>
pracayōpanyāsaḥ । na cānarthakaḥ; pracayē sati dārḍhyamāhāryadhiyāṁ bhavati;
tadarthaścāyaṁ prayāsaḥ, na kr̥tadhiyām । tasmādasti prayōjanam । kathamasau
kr̥tvasuc pratyabhijñāyāṁ hētuḥ ? ēkasyāvr̥ttau darśanāt । satyamēkasya;
sa tu kriyāyāḥ <quote>“kriyābhyāvr̥ttigaṇanē”</quote> ityādēśāt; na hi śabdaḥ
kriyā । kiṁ tarhi ? dravyaṁ guṇō vā syāt । tadidamanyadīyamanyasyōcyamānaṁ
﻿<pb n="331"/>
mātuladhanakathananyāyamāvahati । atrōcyatē---vastusvabhāvānabhijñō bhavān ।
vastusvabhāvāpēkṣiṇō hyādēśā bhavanti । anumānagamyā ca kriyā । tataḥ
kim ? na cānumānagamyasya svarūpamupalabhyata ityuktam । anupalabdhasva-
lakṣaṇasyāvr̥ttiḥ kēnāvagantuṁ śakyatē ? nanu ca yēnaivāsti ; kāryataḥ ;
﻿<pb n="332"/>
āvr̥ttirapi tatō bhavatu । maivam ; kāryāvr̥ttāvāvr̥ttiḥ śakyatē'vagantum,
na kāryataḥ । kāryasya tu kāryatayā āvr̥ttirdurlabhā ; kāryāntarataiva
tatra syāt । jñāpyē punaridaṁ saṁbhavati । jñāpyaśca śabda uccāraṇasyētyuktam ।
tasmāt punaḥ punaḥ jñāpyamānatā śabdasya gamyatē, nōtpadyamānatā । atō
bhaṅgitvē karmaṇō jñāpyaikyādāvr̥ttirityucyatē ; na svataḥ, kāryasvā-
bhāvyāt । kr̥tasya karaṇaṁ nāstīti kr̥tinaḥ । tasmādēvaṁviṣaya ēvāyaṁ
﻿<pb n="333"/>
kr̥tvasuc । kāryaikyaṁ ca pratyabhijñānādityuktam । tasmāt yuktaḥ
kr̥tvasujarthasya hētutōpanyāsastadgrahaṇē । <quote>“anyatvē'pi sati sādr̥śyēna
vyāmūḍhāḥ <quote>‘saḥ’</quote> iti vakṣyanti”</quote>---iti kimidamupanyastam ?
idamēvōpanyastam । na brūmō nōpanyastamiti ; kimanēna nirākr̥taṁ
pratyabhijñāyā iti na vidmaḥ । idamanēna nirākriyatē---bhēdāgraṇa-
nibandhanēyaṁ <quote>‘saḥ’</quote> iti buddhiḥ ; bhēdasya cāgrahaṇamatisādr̥śyādajāvikānāṁ
jvālādīnāṁ dr̥ṣṭam ; agrahaṇē ca bhēdasya nānyatvaṁ vyapadēṣṭuṁ śakyatē ;
﻿<pb n="334"/>
anyatvāvyapadēśē ca kimanyadavaśiṣyatē <quote>‘sa ēva’</quote> iti vyapadēśāt ?
vivēkāgrahaṇamēvātrāparādhyatē maṇimuktādiṣviva vivēkaśūnyānām ; tasmā-
dvivēkē yatra āsthīyatām ; <quote>“avivēkaḥ paramāpadāṁ padam”</quote> ;
āpatsu jātōdvēgānāṁ vivēka ēvaikaḥ śaraṇaṁ param । satyaṁ yathā bhavānāha ;
kintu atra vivēkāgrahaṇē jvālādīnāmiva hēturnāsti---iti <quote>“asthānāt”</quote>
ityasmin sūtrē likhitaṁ vistarēṇa ।</p>
<p><quote>“syādētat buddhikarmaṇī api hi tē pratyabhijñāyētē ; tē api nityē
prāp‍nutaḥ”</quote>---iti kimidaṁ kūśmāṇḍapatanam ? uttarēṇāpi kūśmāṇḍataiva
﻿<pb n="335"/>
pradarśitā---<quote>“atha pratyakṣē, nityē ēva”</quote> iti ; pratyabhijñā hi
kālāntarāvasthāyitvē hēturuktaḥ । yadi karmaṇyapi sāsti, kō'ya-
mupālambhaḥ ? athāyamabhiprāyaḥ---abhyupagamahānaṁ prāpnōti iti ; satyama-
nityatvamabhyupagatamasmābhiḥ ; ānumānikatvamapi । na cānumānikē'rthē
pratyabhijñā bhavati । svarūpagrahaṇē hētvabhāvādasambaddhō'yamupālambhaḥ । yadi
asmadabhyupagamajñānamasti, sarvākāramastu ; kimidamardhajaratīyam ? ucyatē
﻿<pb n="336"/>
---yadyēkakāryatvāt karmābhyāsaṁ kr̥tvasujācaṣṭē, kāraṇānyatāpi na sidhyati ;
na hyanyatvāvagatāvabhyāsāvagatiḥ । gamyamānaikatvācca taddha‍u/?/ddhērapi nānā-
tvamavagamyamēva । tadidamuktam <quote>“buddhikarmaṇī api hi tē pratyabhijñāyētē,
tē api nityē prāp‍nutaḥ”</quote>---iti । syātāṁ nityē, yadi tē pratyakṣē ;
﻿<pb n="337"/>
na hyapratyakṣē'rthē pratyabhijñā prāpnōti । nanu ca bhēdāgrahaṇaṁ pratyabhijñā ;
sā ca buddhikarmaṇōrapyastītyuktam, kāryagamyatvādanumēyānām । satyam,
yadi bhēdāgraṇaṁ pratyabhijñā ; tad‍grahaṇaṁ tu pratyābhijñā ; kāryaṁ hi kāraṇa-
mastītyētāvati jñānamutpādayati, na punastadvā anyadvēti । pratyabhijñā tu
<quote>‘tadēvēdam’</quote> iti prasiddhā lōkē ।</p>
<p><quote>“hyastanasya śabdasya vināśādanyō'dyatana iti cēt”</quote> iti ।
﻿<pb n="338"/>
kimatrānuktamu1ktaṁ bhāṣyakārēṇa ? nanu satyāṁ pratyabhijñāyāmanupalambhē kāraṇāntaraṁ
kalpanīyamityuktam; kalpitāḥ stimitā vāyavaḥ ; tadapagamē cōpalabdhiriti;
saṁyōgaviyōgā apagamahētavaḥ ; kimanyadavaśiṣyatē ? idamavaśiṣyatē---
upalabdhaṁ hyanupalabhyamānaṁ <quote>‘nāsti’</quote> ityasya jñānasya gōcaratāmāpadyatē ;
na hyatyantānupalabhyamānaṁ <quote>‘nāsti’</quote> iti grahamāskandati । yadyupalabdhamapi na
﻿<pb n="339"/>
gōcarībhavati, anāspadamēvēdamabhyupagataṁ bhavati । abhyupagataṁ caitat <quote>“nāstī-
tyasyārthasyāsannikr̥ṣṭasya”</quote> iti । tasmādabhāvō nirviṣayō'nēna vā viṣayēṇa
viṣayī vaktavyaḥ । tasmājjvālādiṣviva śabdē'pyāpatitā pratyabhijñā ।
ahō batānupalabdhāvavivēkō'yam ; yathaivātyantānupalabdhaviṣayānupalabdhiḥ
<quote>‘nāsti’</quote> ityasya jñānasyōtpattau nēṣṭē, tathā tad‍grahaṇaviṣayē'pyarthē ।
tasmādanupalabdhimātramēvēdam, yadantarā śabdē । tathā ca laukikā
﻿<pb n="340"/>
jāyādiṣu nānupalabdhimātrēṇa <quote>‘nāsti’</quote> ityavagacchanti, punardarśanē
viśvāsadarśanāt । tasmāt sapratyabhijñapratyakṣasavyapēkṣō'yaṁ pramāṇā-
bhāvastatra vaktavyaḥ । kutaḥ ? sāpēkṣatvādabhāvasya nirapēkṣatvācca pratyakṣasya ।
tadētat <quote>“ānupūrvyasiddham”</quote>---ityanēnōktam । yadapyatrānumānaṁ sarvabhāva-
﻿<pb n="341"/>
viṣayamuktaṁ nāstitāvagatau, tadapyatra na saṁbhavati ; antē kṣayadarśanāt---
﻿<pb n="342"/>
iti hi tatra hētuḥ । na ca śabdē'ntē kṣayō'sti । atō na tēnāpi
﻿<pb n="343"/>
bādhyata iyaṁ pratyabhijñā ghaṭādiṣu kadācidākampayatyapi ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="344"/>
<p><quote>“anapēkṣatvāt”</quote> iti । satyāmapi pratyabhijñāyāṁ kadācidasamavāyi-
kāraṇōpabdhēḥ anityatāśaṅkyēta ghaṭādīnāmiva; tadapyatra darśanābhāvānnāstīti
sthitā pratyabhijñā ; tatpramēyatayā ca nityatvaṁ śabdasya ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="345"/>
<p><quote>“prakhyābhāvāt”</quote> iti । anapēkṣatāyāmasiddha‍yāśaṅkāṁ nirākarōti ।
sēyamāśaṅkōpanyasyatē---<quote>“vāyurudgataḥ saṁyōgavibhāgaiḥ śabdībhavati”</quote> iti ।
tathā ca śikṣākṣarāṇyanuguṇāni dr̥śyantē---<quote>“vāyurāpadyatē śabdatām”</quote>
iti । tadidaṁ nirākriyatē---yadi vāyavīyaḥ śabdaḥ syāt, vāyōravayava-
sannivēśaviśēṣaḥ syāt ; na ca vāyavīyān sannivēśaviśēṣān śabda
﻿<pb n="346"/>
upalabhāmahē । nanu na cākṣuṣō vāyuḥ । sparśanamapyupalambhanamēva, tēnōpalabdhāḥ
syuḥ ; na cōpalabhāmahē । tasmādapratipakṣā pratyabhijñā । kathaṁ tarhi
﻿<pb n="347"/>
śikṣākṣarāṇi ? tadāyattatvāt tacchabdōpalabdhēstadupacāraḥ ।।</p>
<p>tathā ca vēdākṣarāṇyasmin pakṣē'nuguṇatarāṇi dr̥śyantē <quote>“vācā
virūpanityayā”</quote> iti । kō'trātiśayaḥ ? nityatābhidhānaṁ śrutyā ।
tasmāt pratyabhijñāpramēyatvānnityatāvasthitā śabdē ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="348"/>
<p><quote>“utpattau vāvacanāḥ syurarthasyātannimittatvāt”</quote> । <quote>“yadyautpattikō
nityaḥ śabdaḥ sambandhaśca, tathāpi na cōdanālakṣaṇō dharmaḥ”</quote>
iti । kimidamārabdham ? idamārabdham---vr̥ddhavyavahārādautpattika-
tvamuktaṁ śabdārthajñānasya । vr̥ddhavyavahāraśca pramāṇāntarāvagamyaṁ vākyēnārthaṁ
pratipādayataḥ kasyacit kaścidanyaḥ pratipadyatē । tatpratipattyā
﻿<pb n="349"/>
bālō'pi jānāti <quote>‘anēnaiva tatpratipādyatē’</quote> iti । pratipattiśca hānō-
pādānādikāryāvagamyā । hānōpādānādi ca pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayamēva
śakyatē'vagantum, nāpramitaviṣayam । ataśca pramāṇāntarapramita-
viṣayamēvautpattikatvaṁ śakyatē'vagantum; na punaryatra śabdāvagamapūrvakō
vyavahāraḥ, tatrautpattikatvaṁ śakyāvagamam । tasmādvaidikānāmagnihōtrā-
﻿<pb n="350"/>
dīnāmautpattikatvaṁ duravagamam । tasmādautpattikatvaklēśō'narthakaḥ ; vēda-
prāmāṇyasiddha‍yarthamautpattikatvamiṣyatē svatantrāgamavādibhiḥ । na ca vr̥ddha-
vyavahārāt siddhamautpattikatvaṁ vēdārthapratipattāvabhyupāyatāṁ pratipattuṁ kṣamam ।
kimiti na kṣamam ? samudāyāddhi vr̥ddhavyavahārē'rthō'vagamyatē ;
na cāsau samudāyō vēdē prayuktaḥ । tasmānna nimittatāṁ pratipadyatē । nanu
cānvayavyatirēkābhyāṁ vr̥ddhavyavahārādēva padārthapūrvakō vākyārthō'va-
gamyatē । āvāpōddhārābhyāṁ hi <quote>‘dēvadatta gāmabhyāja śuklām, dēvadatta
gāmabhyāja kr̥ṣṇām, viṣṇumitra gāṁ badhāna raktām’</quote> ityēkatrānvita-
﻿<pb n="351"/>
śuklārthaḥ, anyatrāpōddha‍r̥tataśuklārthō'nvitakr̥ṣṇārthaśca, anyatrāpōddha‍r̥tābhyā-
jāṁrthō'nvitabadhānārthaśca vākyārthō'vagamyatē । atō'vagamyatē---
padēbhyaḥ padārthā ēvāvagamyantē, na vākyārthaḥ ; padārthasamudāyēna
vākyārthō'vagamyatē । anyathā hyēkapadōddhārē sakalavākyārthānavagatirēva
syāt, na padārthamātrasya । tasmāt padēbhyaḥ padārthāḥ; padārthēbhyaḥ
parasparānvitāvagatiḥ । yadi padēbhyaḥ padārthā avasīyantē, padārthēbhyaḥ
parasparānvayaḥ, kiṁ padārthanimittaka ēva vākyārthaḥ ? ōm ityucyatē ।
kasya padārthasya kasminnanvayē hētutvam ? sarvasya sarvasminniti
brūmaḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi sarvavākyārthāvagatiḥ sarvasmāt । niyamē vā
﻿<pb n="352"/>
hēturvaktavyaḥ <quote>‘itthaṁbhūtēnētthaṁbhūtō'nvayaḥ pratipādyatē’</quote> iti । na cātra
vr̥ddhavyavahāraṁ muk‍tvānyatkāraṇamupalabhāmahē । tasmādyatra samudāyaḥ prayuktaḥ,
tatraiva padaṁ padārthamavagamayati; padārthaśca padārthāntarēṇānvitamā-
tmānamiti prayōgapratipattimūlēyaṁ kalpanā । atō'nvayavyatirēkāvapi
pratipattiviṣayāvēva ; satyāṁ hi pratipattāvāvāpōddhārāvagatirvyavahārē vyutpā-
dyasya । avagatiśca pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayaiva, hānōpādānāvagamyatvāt
﻿<pb n="353"/>
vr̥ddhapratipattērityuktam । yatra punaḥ pramāṇēna <quote>‘asminnarthē prayuktaḥ’</quote>
iti na jñāyatē, prayōgādēvārthō'vagantavyaḥ, tatra kathaṁ nimittatā
śakyatē kalpayituṁ padapadārthayōḥ, pratipattipūrvakatvānnimittabhāvasya ?
﻿<pb n="354"/>
na punanirmittāvagamādēva naimittikāvagatiḥ । yasmin hi sati
yadbhavati taddarśanāt <quote>‘asyēdaṁ nimittam’</quote> iti bhavati matiḥ ; na
punastatsambhavādēva । kēna vōktamanyathā ? naimittikāvagamādēva
nimittāvagatiḥ । avagamyatē ca <quote>“agnihōtraṁ juhuyātsvargakāmaḥ”</quote> iti
padārthānvitō vākyārthaḥ । atō'trāpi padapadārthayōrnimittatā kēna
vāryatē ? kathaṁ punargamyatē <quote>‘anvitapadārthakō vākyārthaḥ’</quote> iti ? nanvē-
tasmādēva vākyāt । tarhi nimittatāvagamādēva naimittikāvagatirityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="355"/>
vr̥ddhavyavahārē hi hānōpādānādigamyaṁ naimittikatvam ; iha punarvacanādēva
hānōpādānē pravartētē ; tasmādviparītam । nanu ca vr̥ddhavyavahārē'pi
pratipattā vākyādēvārthaṁ pratipadyatē ; bālastu pārśvasthaḥ śabdārthayōḥ sambandhaṁ
hānōpādānābhyāṁ vētti । satyam ; asāvapi tu sambandhajñānōttarakālaṁ
tatō vijānāti nimittānnaimittikam; vēdē punaravijñātanimittanaimittika-
sambandhaḥ kasya nimittattāṁ vijānātu, kasya vā naimittikatvam ? atha
﻿<pb n="356"/>
sāmānyatōdr̥ṣṭānumānaṁ kriyatē---vr̥ddhavyavahārē padapadārthayōrnimittabhāvō
dr̥ṣṭaḥ, vēdē'pi ta ēva padārthāḥ, tasmādvēdē'pi svārthānvitau nimittatvam---
iti ; ēvaṁ tarhi kiyantaḥ kasyāmityatra pramāṇaṁ nāsti । yāvantō
yasmāmavagatau pratīyantē---iti cēt, avagatipūrvakamēva tarhi
nimittatvam ; na sāmānyatōdr̥ṣṭanimittakam; na cāvagatēḥ pramāṇa-
mastītyuktam । tat sāmānyatōdr̥ṣṭanibandhanaivēyaṁ bhrāntiḥ । sāmayikī
vā dr̥ṣṭavyavahārapūrvikādr̥ṣṭāvagatiḥ ; lōkasiddhairvā saṁjñāsaṁjñisambandhaṁ
﻿<pb n="357"/>
kr̥tvā vaidikō vyavahāraḥ pravartitaḥ kēścit । nanu kāryaikyanibandhana-
mēkavākyatvaṁ bhaviṣyati । kāryaikyaṁ ca niyōgaikyāt । niyōgaikyaṁ
﻿<pb n="358"/>
cānubandhavinirmōkādityuktam । niyōgārthaśca lōkē vēdē'pi sa ēva---
ityuktam ; prāptāprāptavivēkēna hi prēṣaṇādayō'bhihitāḥ । tasmā-
nnimittapūrvakē'pi na dōṣaḥ । siddhaṁ sāmānyatōdr̥ṣṭamanumānaṁ nimittā-
vagatau । tadidamayuktam ; kiṁ niyōgārthaḥ pramāṇāntarānirjñātārthatayā-
lōkē'rthāvagatau nimittatayā dr̥ṣṭaḥ ? nēti brūmaḥ ; <quote>“prathamaśrutaḥ kiṁ na
﻿<pb n="359"/>
pratyāyayati ?”</quote>---ityanatikramaṇīyō'yaṁ hētuḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi tadarthabhēdasyāpi
pramāṇāntaraṁ mr̥gyam । anubandhāśca tadbhēdānuvartinō lōkē dr̥ṣṭāḥ, na
punastadanuvartī bhēdaḥ । tasmāt parasparānvayitā na prayōgāvacchēdamanyatō'-
vijñāya śakyatē'vagantum । na cāsāvavacchēdaḥ pramāṇāntarābhāvādvēdē
﻿<pb n="360"/>
vidyatē । tasmāt darśanāntaraṁ mr̥gyam । na nēṣṭaṁ svatantrāgamavādināmidam ।
na ca svabhāvādarthāvagatirityuktam । ataḥ pratīyamānapadārthānvayī
vākyārthaḥ, na pramāṇāntarāpēkṣā---iti gahanēyaṁ nyāyapadavī । kathamiya-
mavagāhanīyēti yuktā saṁpradhāraṇā । ata ēka ēvāyaṁ bahudhā vikalpyā-
vagamyatē lōkē vēdē cēti brahmavidō manyantē । tasmādvivarta ēvāyamiti
﻿<pb n="361"/>
brahmavidbhiravagantavyam । vēdavidbhirityarthaḥ । kathaṁ punaḥ vivartapakṣē nāyaṁ
dōṣaḥ ? ēkatāvagatistāvannaivāsti, <quote>“śrōtragrahaṇē hyarthē lōkē”</quote>---ityanēna
pratipāditatvāt । tadēvēdaṁ duruktam, kāryavirōdhādityucyatē । kiṁ
kāryataḥ pratyakṣamātmānaṁ labhatē ? mā bhūtpratyakṣam; anumānamapi pramāṇamēva ।
anumānādapi pramāṇāvagatiryuktaiva । bhavadbhirapyānumānikamēva prāmāṇyaṁ
sarvatrōktam । anumānādavagatasyārthasya kathamēkatvam ? anyatvaṁ vā katham ?
﻿<pb n="362"/>
ēkatayā ca vinā kiṁ na sidhyati idaṁ na sidhyati---na hyupāyāḥ
kalpitāḥ prāp‍nuvanti; ēkatvāvagatau śrutyāmavacchēdāḥ kalpitāḥ syuḥ । na
caikatāvagatiryuktānumānāt---iti cōditam । naiṣa dōṣaḥ; anumānāt
pramāṇatvamavacchidya, tataḥ punarēkatāmavayavairvētti <quote>‘śuklaḥ paṭaḥ’</quote> ityēvamādiṣu ।
tadidamāgamāt pratipannamēkatvam <quote>‘pratyastamitāśēṣāgamavikalpaṁ svayaṁ brahma
prakāśatē’</quote> iti । yaducyatē---<quote>“śrōtragrahaṇē hyarthē lōkē śabdaśabdaḥ prasiddhaḥ”</quote>
iti, tadapyāgamaviruddham; <quote>‘gauḥ’</quote> iti śabdaḥ, <quote>‘gauḥ’</quote> ityarthaḥ, <quote>‘gauḥ’</quote> iti
﻿<pb n="363"/>
vijñānam, ēkābhidhānanirdēśāta; na hi bhinnasya ‌yugapadēkābhidhānaṁ
saṁbhavati । kathaṁ punaḥ yaugapadyāvagamaḥ ? vācakajñānavācyānāṁ parasparāpēkṣiṇī
svarūpāvagatiryataḥ । ataśca yadapyuktam---sajātīyāvamarśaśūnyā na sāmā-
nyāvagatirasti iti, tadayuktam; bhēdanibandhanā hyēṣā yuktiḥ । vidyamānasya
hyavamarśō bhavati, na kalpitasya । uktaṁ caikatvamēkābhidhānanirdēśāt ।
﻿<pb n="364"/>
tataḥ kim ? idaṁ tataḥ---kalpanayaiva vr̥ddhavyavahārasya nimittatōcyatē । taccēdaṁ
kalpanābījaṁ bahudhōcyatē---<quote>“padamādyam”</quote> ityēvamādi । tasmāt padārtha-
vēdanēna saṁskr̥tānyabhēdaṁ pratipadyantē ityarthaḥ । na caitāvatā aprāmāṇyaṁ
śrutēḥ, pramēyē śaktisadbhāvādityuktam । tatō'nāgamikī kalpanā pratyavāyāya,
na vaidikī, paramārthaparatvādvaidikasya । ataḥ siddhamautpattikatvamasmatpakṣē ।
bhēdābhidhānapakṣē yathā na sidhyati, tathā pradarśitam । ata ēva ca
yathāviniyōgaṁ mantrārthān mantravidō varṇayanti; bhēdē hi niyatamabhidhānaṁ
﻿<pb n="365"/>
syāt । ataḥ <quote>“uṇādayō bahulam”</quote> ityēvamādyanāgamapūrvakamēva syāt ।
na caitattavāpīṣṭam । upadēśaścārthavānaṅgavidyānāma; bhēdapakṣē hi lōkata
ēva niyatatvādbhēdānāṁ kimanyadākhyāyatē ? asmatpakṣē punarāgamānusārī
vikalpaḥ; ānantyāccāgamasya upadēśō'rthavān । ataścāyaṁ bhēdavyapadēśaḥ
---laukikānāṁ vaidikānāṁ chandasi bhāṣāyāṁ nigama iti ca । āgama-
bhēdāścōpapannā bhavanti । kēnacit kvacidavacchidya tadēva pradarśitaṁ bhavati ।
ata ēva caikādaśadvādaśakapālamēkaṁ karma । anyathā hi bhēdāvagamē
﻿<pb n="366"/>
ēkatvābhidhānaṁ pralāpaḥ । na kēvalamatra, abhidhānasandarbhē'pi । api
ca kāryāvagamyatvācca pramāṇatāyā ēkatvācca kāryasya nānābhidhānaṁ na
pramāṇēnōpapadyatē । vākyasamāsayōścāvagatyanyatvē'pi tulyakalpanāpratiṣēdhārthaṁ
vāvacanamāgamavikalpajñāpanāyōpapannārthaṁ bhavati । anyathā hi vastvēva
nirōdhakam । ata ēvābhidhēyavaśavartiśaktinirūpaṇaṁ nāmākhyātōpa-
sarganipātānām; bhēdē hi svarūpabhēdaḥ pāramārthikaḥ । tatra pratyabhijñānē
sati <quote>‘vilambatē’</quote> <quote>‘pralambatē’</quote> <quote>‘vipra’</quote> ityanyatvaṁ na syāt; tathā bhavatyādiṣu
﻿<pb n="367"/>
varṇamātravādinaḥ । rājñaḥ puruṣasya hastinaḥ---iti padadvayasambandhō'pi
bhavati, na---rājapuruṣasya hastinaḥ iti । ēvamupagōridam, apatyasyēdam;
na punaḥ aupagavasyēdam---iti । tathāca karaṇam, karaṇēna---
iti vibhaktērutpattiranutpattiśca । tathā ca subdhātavaḥ---aśvaḥ gardabhaḥ
iti, aśvati gardabhati iti ca । tathā cāṣṭādaśaprabhēdamavarṇakulamartha-
pratipattayē । anyathā hyēkatvādvastunaḥ sarvārthapratipattirapratipattirvā syāta;
﻿<pb n="368"/>
vyavasthā nōpapadyatē । pramāṇāntarapratītē'rtha ēkāvagamō mr̥ṣā---surabhi
candanam, śītō vāyuriti ca । candanasya surabhiḥ, vāyōḥ śītam
ityēva syāt । upasarganipātānāṁ kvacidviśēṣaṇārthatvaṁ kvacidānarthakyaṁ
kvacidviparītārthatā tadbhāvē nōpapadyatē । padārthapūrvakatvācca vākyārthasya
tadvaśādapi nirṇayō durvacaḥ । padabhēdē ca padārthavināśaḥ syāt ।
ānarthakyē caikavākyatā katham ? vibhāgajñānaṁ ca ? varṇōpajana ēva syāt ।
﻿<pb n="369"/>
āgamavikalpapakṣē tu sarvamupapannam । āgamavikalpāvagamaḥ kutaḥ iti
cēt, āgamāntarādēva । taduktam---<quote>“r̥ṣīṇāmapi yajjñānaṁ tadapyā-
gamapūrvakam”</quote> । anidamprathamatā cāsyānāditvāt saṁsārasya śakyatē'va-
gantum । sēyamanapēkṣatā prāmāṇyahētuḥ । bhēdapakṣē sarvamidamasamañjasam ।
darśayati ca jñānapradhānavartī vēdaḥ acchidyāvabōdhakatvaṁ vēdasya ।
vēdāntāḥ katham ? <quote>“atha yadalpam, tanmartyam”</quote>; <quote>‘atha yadbha‍ūma,
tadamr̥tam’</quote>---iti । kiṁ tadalpam ? avacchēdaḥ । kalpanīyasyāvacchēdō
﻿<pb n="370"/>
dr̥ṣṭaḥ, na punastattvasya । <quote>“yāvadvācō gatam”</quote>---ityādi sarvamupapannārthaṁ
bhavati । anyathā hi virōdhaḥ syāt । virōdhē cāprāmāṇyam ।
tasmādēkānuguṇamidaṁ brahmarāśimāgamavidō vyācakṣatē । sō'yamāgamaḥ ।
tadidaṁ tattvam । ta imē brahmavidaḥ, ya ēvaṁ vijānatē । tasmānnivarta-
svaitasmādbhēdagrahāt saṁsārānupātinaḥ । nanu cātrāpi vr̥ddhavyavahāra-
vyutpattirnaivōpakārikā । āgamataścēdvikalpāḥ pravartantē, kiṁ vr̥ddhavyavahārēṇa ?
atha vr̥ddhavyavahāravyutpattyā avikalpitā nāgamavikalpān pratipadyantē;
﻿<pb n="371"/>
tadidaṁ bhēdavyavahārē'pi tulyam । athāgamata ēva vikalpāḥ pratipadyantē,
vr̥ddhavyavahāravyutpannā nimittāvagatiḥ kvōpayujyatē ? tasmādayamapi
bhēdapakṣaparyavasita ēva pakṣaḥ । athēdānīmayamaparaḥ prakāraḥ---jātiguṇa-
yōrivaikadravyanivēśādēkadravyasambandhaḥ pratīyatē; tadvajjātiguṇaśabdayōrapi
sannihitatayōccaritayōḥ tad‍dvārēṇaikārthatāvagamyata iti cēt, tanna; vyutpattau
nimittamātratayāvagatēḥ nimittamātratayaivāvagatiḥ prāpnōti । ēvamānarthakya-
﻿<pb n="372"/>
miti cēt; na hyānarthakyamarthāntarāvagatau hētuḥ । tasmādanarthaka ēvāyaṁ
vr̥ddhavyavahāranibandhanaḥ śabdārthayōrautpattikasambandhābhidhānaklēśaḥ । tasmāt
pūrvōktamēva kr̥takatvaṁ sāmayikatvaṁ vā sambandhasyēti sthitam । <quote>“yadyautpattikō
nityaḥ śabdaḥ sambandhaśca, tathāpi na cōdanālakṣaṇō dharmaḥ”</quote>---
iti vr̥ddhavyavahārasyānimittatāpratijñēyaṁ vaidikē vyavahārē; yathōktam ।
<quote>‘cōdanā hi vākyam । na hyagnihōtrāt svargō bhavatīti gamyatē’</quote>---iti
﻿<pb n="373"/>
vākyāt pratipattiryōktā, hētvabhidhānapātanikēyam । na cāyaṁ sāmudāyō
vr̥ddhavyavahārasiddhaḥ, yaḥ śrutau prayuktaḥ । tasmādanimittatā pūrvōktā asya
bhāṣyasyārthatayā varṇitā । <quote>“padāni hyamūni prayuktāni, ēṣāṁ
nityō'rthaḥ”</quote> iti vr̥ddhavyavahārē hi padānāmautpattikatvaṁ nimittatayā siddhaṁ
﻿<pb n="374"/>
tasminnēva naimittikē । iha punarnaimittikāntarāvagatāvasiddha ēva
nimittabhāvaḥ । kutaḥ ? aprayuktaḥ samudāyō yasmāt । ēvaṁ sati kr̥trimatva-
mupavarṇitam । <quote>“na ca padārthā ēva vākyārthaḥ”</quote>---iti parasparānanvayitāṁ
darśayati । parasparānvitatā hi viśēṣa ucyatē । <quote>“sāmānyē hi padaṁ
vartatē, viśēṣē vākyam”</quote>---ityanēna vyāvahārikī padavyutpattiranarthikē-
tyuktam । vistaraścātrōkta ēva pūrvam । <quote>“na ca padārthādvākyārthāvagatiḥ,
﻿<pb n="375"/>
asambandhāt”</quote> iti । nanvastyēva padārthānāṁ vākyārthēna sambandhaḥ,
tadanvayasyaiva vākyārthatvāt । na hi prayōgaśūnyā parasparānvitatā
śakyatē'vagantumiti pūrvōktānavagatiḥ ētadbhāṣyanibandhanā । <quote>“asati
cēt sambandhē kasmiścidarthē'vagatē'rthāntaramavagamyēta, ēkasminnavagatē
sarvamavagataṁ syāt”</quote>---ityapadārthanimittatvē vākyārthasya hētuḥ;
varṇitaścāyam । <quote>“aprayuktādapi vākyādasati sambandhē svabhāvā-
﻿<pb n="376"/>
darthāvagamaḥ”</quote>---ityanēnānubandhavinirmuktaṁ niyōgaikyaṁ vēdē darśayatīti
varṇitam । <quote>“śabdō dharmamātmīyaṁ vyutkrāmēt ; na caiṣa
śabdadharmaḥ, yadaprayuktācchabdādarthaḥ pratīyatē”</quote>---iti kāryānuvarti-
tāmanubandhānāmanubandhavinirmuktau darśayati ; yathōditam । <quote>“na hi
prathamaśrutāt kutaścana śabdāt kēcidarthaṁ pratiyanti”</quote>---iti
sāmānyatōdr̥ṣṭavirōdhaḥ pūrvōktaḥ । <quote>“tadabhidhīyatē---padadharmō'yam, na
﻿<pb n="377"/>
vākyadharmaḥ ; vākyāddhi prathamaśrutādapi pratiyantō dr̥śyantē”</quote>---iti ।
kathaṁ tarhyarthānavagatiḥ ? avagatērvidmaḥ---padārthamātravyutpattita ēva
vr̥ddhavyavahārō vēdārthāvagatau hētuḥ---ityupanyastamanēna bhāṣyēṇa prāguktamēva ।
<quote>“naitadēvam ; yadi prathamaśrutādavagacchēyuḥ, api tarhi sarvē'vagacchēyuḥ
padārthavidō'nyē ca ; na tvapadārthavidō'vagacchanti”</quote> iti । na hyaprayuktā-
﻿<pb n="378"/>
llōkē samudāyādarthō'vagantuṁ śakyatē । yattu padārthavidō'vagacchantīti,
tat sāmānyatōdr̥ṣṭabhrāntyā pūrvōktayā---iti mantavyam । <quote>“nanu ca
padārthavidbhirapyavagacchadbhirakr̥taka ēva vākyārthasambandhō'vagatō bhavati ;
padārthavēdanēna saṁskr̥tā avagamiṣyanti yathā tamēvārthaṁ dvitīyādi-
śravaṇēna”</quote>---iti । kimatra bhrāntyā ? āgamavikalpānuguṇyādvaraṁ nimittataiva
yathā vr̥ddhavyavahāra ēva dvitīyādiśravaṇam । ayaṁ pūrvōpavarṇitō'rthaḥ ।
<quote>“nēti brūmaḥ ; yadi vākyāntyō varṇaḥ pūrvavarṇajanitasaṁskārasahitaḥ
﻿<pb n="379"/>
padārthēbhyō'rthāntaraṁ pratyāyayati, ka upakārastadānīṁ padārthajñānādavakalpatē”</quote>-
iti pūrvōktamanimittatvaṁ vēdasya kalpanāyāmapi tulyamityasyārthaḥ । <quote>“nanvēvaṁ
saṁbhaviṣyati---sāmānyavācinaḥ padasya <quote>‘gauḥ’</quote> iti vā <quote>‘aśvaḥ’</quote> iti vā,
viśēṣakam <quote>‘śuklaḥ’</quote> iti vā <quote>‘kr̥ṣṇaḥ’</quote> iti vā padamantikādupanipatati yadā,
tadā vākyārthō'vagamyatē”</quote> iti । tadētat kāryaikyanibandhanaṁ yaduktam
arthayōriva buddha‍yēkatvōtpattihētutvam, tadupanyastam । <quote>“na hi ; kathamiva
<quote>‘gauḥ’</quote> iti vā <quote>‘aśvaḥ’</quote> iti vā sāmānyavācinaḥ padāt sarvagavīṣu sarvāśvēṣu
﻿<pb n="380"/>
ca buddhirupasarpantī śrutijanitā vākyānurōdhēna kutaścidviśēṣādapavartēta ?”</quote>
iti । nimittamātravyutpattērvyavahāravyutpattau padārthamātrāvagatiḥ prāpnōti,
na parasparānvayaḥ---iti prāguktamanēnōktam । arthanimittaṁ tvārtham,
na śābdam ; śābdaṁ tvidaṁ vicāryatē । tatra ca yāvatprayōgiṇyēva
﻿<pb n="381"/>
nimittatā uktā । na ca prayōgavyutpattau padārthāntaravyāvr̥ttyā padasya
svārthanimittatā dr̥ṣṭā, yēna padāntaraprayōgāt sarvagavīṣu pratyayō vyāvr̥ttaḥ
