śabdāt---iti śakyatē vak‍tum । nanvēvaṁ satyānarthakyaṁ bhaviṣyati ।
bhavatu; na hīdamānarthakyamarthāntaraparatayā kalpayituṁ kṣamam; ānarthakyamēva
hi tanna syāt । tasmāt kr̥trimaḥ sambandhaḥ । pratyastamitamanapēkṣatvam ।
samarthitaścāyaṁ hētuḥ---vākyātmakatvāt kr̥takō vēda iti ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="382"/>
<p><quote>“tadbhratānāṁ kriyārthēna samāmnāyō'rthasya tannimittatvāt ।”</quote> atrōcyatē
---syādanupāyatvaṁ vr̥ddhavyavahārasya, yadi padārthānyatvaṁ syāt;
āvāpōddhārataiva kēvalamanyā । katham ? vaidikalaukikayōḥ padārthayō-
ranyatvānavagatēḥ । kimidaṁ pratyuktaṁ punarucyatē ? parasparānvayō hi padārthānāṁ
vākyārtha ityuktam । na padārthāḥ; tasmānna padārthapratyabhijñānamanvayahētuḥ ।
﻿<pb n="383"/>
pramāṇāntaraṁ ca nāstyasmin prayuktamityuktam । tataḥ prayōgaśūnyō'nvayō
nirbījaḥ । padapadārthānabhijñō mātr̥priyō bhavān । kathamanabhijñaḥ ?
pādārthāstāvannāvyatiṣaktāḥ kvacidupalabhyantē, antatō'styarthēna । tataḥ
kim ? idaṁ tataḥ । tatpratipattayē hi śabdārthavyavahāraḥ ।
﻿<pb n="384"/>
vyavahārē caṁ yathāvyatiṣaṅgamēvāvāpōddhārau । tasmāt vyatiṣaktārthābhidhānam,
﻿<pb n="386"/>
vyatiṣaktēnāvagatērvyatiṣaṅgasya । kimēvaṁ bhaviṣyati ? nānanvitābhidhāyī
śabda uktō bhaviṣyati । tataśca kāryābhidhāyitā lōkē niyōgasyāvagatā ।
﻿<pb n="387"/>
<quote>“ācāryacōditaḥ karōmi”</quote>---iti hi darśitam । nanu ca prēṣaṇādayō'-
pyavagamyantē lōkē । upādhayō hi tē, na śabdārthāḥ । kēna punaramī upādhayō
nāma ? upādhayō hi taṭasthāḥ prayōgadarśanamātrācchabdārthaṁ viśēṣē'vasthāpa-
﻿<pb n="388"/>
yanti yathā dr̥tiharyabhidhēyasya paśutvam । ēvamasau niyōgaḥ samahīnajyā-
yōbhiḥ prayujyamānaḥ prēṣaṇādivyapadēśaṁ labhatē । pravartakatvaṁ tu śabdārthaḥ,
sarvatrāparityāgāt । atō niyōgābhidhānamidam । niyōgābhidhānē ca sati
tatsādhanavyatiṣaṅgō'vagamyatē । sādhanābhidhānē ca sādhyavyatiṣaṅgaḥ । ata
idamuktam-tadbha‍ūtānāṁ ātmīyēṣvarthēṣu vyasthitānāṁ vyatiṣaṅgāvagatērnimittatva-
mupapadyata iti । nanu ca prayōgē satyētadyuktaṁ vak‍tum । kēna vōktamaprayōgē
satīti ? ēvaṁbhūtēṣu hi dr̥ṣṭō laukikaḥ prayōgaḥ; vaidikā api ta ēva ।
atastathābhūtēṣvēvāyaṁ prayōgaḥ । ēvaṁ tarhi nimittatō naimittikāvagatiḥ ।
﻿<pb n="389"/>
manda ! maivam, kathanōpāyō'yam; na hyanvitō'nvayaśūnyaḥ śakyatē prati-
pattum । ta ētē'nvitāḥ padārthāḥ; ēṣāmabhidhānāni padāni; tadidaṁ vākya-
padīyam । anyathā hyavagamyamānaḥ padapadārthavivēkō'pahnutō bhavati, avidya-
mānaḥ pratipannaḥ । tasmānna kāryatastāvadvākyavākyārthayōḥ padapadārthābhyā-
manyatvaṁ kalpayituṁ kṣaṇā prajñā । pratyakṣatastu bhēdāvagamān‍nāstyēkatvamityuktam ।
﻿<pb n="390"/>
ataḥ kriyārthēna samāmnāyaḥ । nanu ca nāvaśyaṁ kriyārthēnaivāmnānaṁ lōkē । asti
tāvat kriyārthatā vēdē; tadviṣayamidamadhikaraṇaṁ bhaviṣyati । kiṁ na laukika-
viṣayamidamadhikaraṇam ? kiṁ vā manyatē bhavān ? nyāyābhidhānasāmyāt
sarvatrēti manyāmahē । bhavatu sarvatra । nanu ca kriyārthēna---ityavyāpakam ।
﻿<pb n="391"/>
vyavahārakriyaivēyaṁ kriyēti matvā śāmyatu bhavān । ataḥ siddham <quote>“arthasya
tannimittatvāt”</quote> iti vaidikānāṁ sanimittatvam । <quote>“tēṣvēva padārthēṣu”</quote> iti
anvitēṣvityarthaḥ । kutaḥ ? nānapēkṣya padārthān pārthagarthyēna vākyārthaḥ pratīyatē ।
na cēt pratīyatē, kasya vākyaṁ pramāṇatayā kalpayiṣyatē ? nanu cānvayō
na padārthaḥ; sa ca vākyārthō bhaviṣyati । ataścārthādvākyamapi
﻿<pb n="392"/>
padēbhyō'nyaditi gamyatē । <quote>“nanvarthāpattiḥ”</quote> ityanēnēdamuktam । <quote>“tanna,
arthasya tannimittatvāt”</quote> ityanvitābhidhānēna kathitō'syārthaḥ---arthā-
pattirnāstīti । <quote>“api cānvayavyatirēkābhyāmētadavagamyatē; bhavati hi
﻿<pb n="393"/>
kadācidiyamavasthā mānasādapacārāduccāritēbhyō'pi padēbhyō na padārthā
avadhāryantē; na tadānīṁ niyōgatō vākyārthamavagacchanti । na ca
niyōgatō vākyārthaṁ nāvagacchēyuḥ, yadyasya pārthagarthyamabhaviṣyat; niyōga-
tastu nāvagacchanti”</quote> iti । kimanēnānuktamuktam ? na khalu kiñcit;
pratijñātārthasyānanyatvamēva; tatsiddhayē hēturupanyastaḥ । katham ?
yadyasaṁsr̥ṣṭapadārtha ēva vākyārthō'vagamyatē, vyutpattimātraṁ padārthāvagatiḥ;
kasmāt vyutpattyavamarśaśūnyamapi kadācijjñānaṁ na bhavati nirūḍha-
vyavahārasya, yathā dhūmānmahānasādipradēśāvamarśaśūnyamagnijñānam ? na ca
vākyārthē nirūḍhavyavahārasyāpyēvaṁrūpāvagatirdr̥ṣṭā । atō na nimittatayā
﻿<pb n="394"/>
padārthā avadhāryantē । kiṁ tarhi ? naimittikatayaiva । kiṁ punaḥ kāraṇaṁ
nirūḍhavyavahārasya nimittānapēkṣā naimittikāvagatiḥ ? pracitasaṁskārō hi
nāvaśyaṁ nimittavyāpāramapēkṣatē; andha ivābhyastapadavīkō na tadīkṣaṇamapē-
kṣatē । atra punaḥ sarvadā tadapēkṣaṇāt tadēva pramēyamityucyatē । ēvaṁ tarhi
<quote>“padārthēbhyō vākyārthapratyayaḥ”</quote> iti kathamayaṁ vyatirēkaḥ? ēvamayaṁ vyatirēkaḥ
---anvitēbhyō'nvayapratyaya iti । <quote>“api ca antarēṇāpi padōccāraṇaṁ yaḥ
śōklyamavagacchati, avagacchatyēvāsau śuklaguṇakaṁ dravyam”</quote> iti ।
﻿<pb n="395"/>
kimanvayavyatirēkabhāṣyaśēṣamēvaitat ? ōmityucyatē । tatra ca padārthasya
vyatirēkadarśanam, iha cānvayasya । satyamēvam; na tvētāvanmātramēva ।
kimatiricyatē ? idamatiricyatē---yadi hi vyutpattau padānāṁ padārthamātra
ēva vyutpattiḥ, tadā ananvitapadārthadarśanē tatsmaraṇānupapattiḥ, smaryatē ca ।
ataḥ siddhamanvitābhidhānam । <quote>“nāsya padasamudāyēna saha sambandhaḥ”</quote>
﻿<pb n="396"/>
iti । na samudāyabhūtānāṁ prāmāṇyam । kiṁ tarhi ? anvayavyatirēkasamadhi-
gamyasvārthavyāpr̥tānāmēva । <quote>“yattu śrautaḥ padārthō na vākyānurōdhēna kutaści-
dviśēṣādapavartitumarhati”</quote> iti । kathaṁ punarvyutpattiśūnyaivāvagatiḥ śakyatē'-
bhidhātumityabhiprāyaḥ । parihārastu---satyamēvamētaditi । vyavahārārthatvāt
﻿<pb n="397"/>
prayōgasya viśēṣātmakatvācca vyavahārasya anvitāvagatirēva tadarthā-
nām; nānvitārthāntarasmaraṇam, vyavahārānaṅgatvāt । tadidamuktam---
<quote>“yaścārthādarthaḥ, na sa cōdanārthaḥ”</quote> iti । na cēdānīṁ tadavivakṣita-
miti pratīyamānasyāpi śabdāt avivakṣitatvaṁ śakyatē vak‍tum ।
﻿<pb n="398"/>
gamyatē ca śabdānnimittāt aśabdārthaścēti kimidam ? śabdāntarābhidhēyatayā
smaraṇāt, smr̥tēścāprāmāṇyāt । ataḥ śabdanimittatāpi bhrāntairēvōditā
pratyakṣādīnāmiva smaraṇīyē । ēvaṁ ca guṇāntarapratiṣēdhō na śabdārtha
iti kalpitanimittaparihārāt parihr̥tam । <quote>“api ca prātipadikādu-
ccarantī dvitīyādivibhaktiḥ”</quote> iti । anvitārthamēva prātipadikaṁ smaranti;
﻿<pb n="399"/>
yataḥ karaṇavācinaḥ prātipadikāt tr̥tīyāṁ vidadhati । vibhaktayaśca
parasparānvayapratipādikāḥ prayōgāntarasmr̥tasyārthasyānvayitāṁ śrutyaiva darśayanti ।
atō'bhyuccayōpapattiriyam । pratyuktamanumānam <quote>‘kr̥takatvāt’</quote> iti vr̥ddha-
vyavahārasya nimittatōpapattyā । <quote>“api ca”</quote> ityanēna pūrvōktasambandhakara-
ṇāśaktiṁ darśayati ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="400"/>
<p>lōkē punaḥ pramāṇāntarapramitaviṣayatayā yuktaiva, tatpūrvakatvāt
śabdavyavahārasya । <quote>“tasmāt padēbhya ēva padārthapratyayaḥ, padārthabhyō
vākyārthapratyayaḥ”</quote> iti vyākhyātam । tasmādupapannaṁ vr̥ddhavyavahāra-
﻿<pb n="401"/>
nimittamautpattikatvaṁ sambandhasya, vēdavākyārthapratipattihētutvaṁ ca ।
vilambatē---ityādayastu śabdapratyabhijñayaiva; abhidhānē hi sa dōṣaḥ ।
samāsādīnāṁ tu tatra tatra parihārō'bhidhīyatē ।।</p>
<p><quote>“vēdāṁścaikē sannikarṣaṁ puruṣākhyāḥ”</quote> । <quote>“padavākyāśrayaḥ”</quote> iti ।
vibhāgābhidhānādavibhaktakāryatvācca vivēkaḥ । yaduktam <quote>“asmaraṇāt”</quote> iti,
﻿<pb n="402"/>
tat viruddhaṁ samākhyayā । kiṁ kāryanibandhanaivēyaṁ samākhyā ? bāḍham; asādhāra-
ṇēna hi vyapadēśō bhavati, sādhāraṇaṁ ca pravak‍tr̥tvam । kathaṁ tarhi---<quote>“kr̥tē
﻿<pb n="403"/>
granthē”</quote>, <quote>“tēna prōktam”</quote> iti ca sūtradvayaṁ bhagavataḥ ? prōktavacanamayuktam,
<quote>“samarthānām”</quote> iti virōdhāt । tasmāt kāryataiva vēdasyāvagamyatē ।।</p>
<p>kēyaṁ kāryatā nityatvācchabdānāmautpattikatvācca sambandhasya ?
pramāṇāntarāpēkṣitā । tathā ca tadanurūpaṁ vēdavacō dr̥śyatē---<quote>“babaraḥ
prāvāhaṇiḥ”</quote> ityēvamādi । atrōcyatē---syādētadēvam, yadyanyathā
﻿<pb n="404"/>
asādhāraṇavyapadēśō nōpapadyatē । prakarṣādapi hyasādhāraṇavyapadēśō dr̥ṣṭō
lōkē; yathā bādarāyaṇēna vēdaprāmāṇyaṁ samākhyāyatē । ata ēva sūtradvayapraṇayanaṁ
bhagavataḥ pāṇinēḥ । <quote>“samarthānām”</quote>---iti cāvirōdhaḥ ।।</p>
﻿<pb n="405"/>
<p>yaduktam <quote>“babaraḥ prāvāhaṇiḥ”</quote> iti, sthitē prāmāṇyē guṇavādaṁ
vakṣyati । vakṣyamāṇamēva ca bhāṣyakārēṇātra vyākhyātam । kimartham,
<quote>‘vakṣyāmaḥ’</quote> iti nōktaṁ ca ? asambaddhatvōpanyāsārtham---na śakyatē
﻿<pb n="406"/>
jyōtiṣṭōmādiṣu vidhyuddēśēṣu kalpayituṁ tat; ēkavākyatvācca <quote>“vanaspatayaḥ”</quote>
﻿<pb n="407"/>
ityēvamādīnām ? <quote>“api ca avigītaḥ suhr̥dupadēśaḥ”</quote>---iti sārvajanīna-
maviparyayaṁ darśayati । tasmāccōdanaiva pramāṇaṁ dharmasyēti sthitaḥ
pratijñārthaḥ ।।</p>
<p>।। iti br̥hatyāṁ prathamādhyāyasya prathamaḥ pādaḥ samāptaḥ ।।</p>
